- *Devourer* — the threat is built into the partner, ambient and constant, which paradoxically lowers his vigilance because the worst is structurally normalized.
- *Royal / inhuman* — the legitimacy hunger is supplied at the level of the marriage itself; he is consort to a queen, which gratifies the moral-community drive in a register safely external to the human moral community that has betrayed him.
- *Sexually voracious in a way the persona can metabolize as humor* — the affect-mobility requirement is satisfied; the marriage runs at high stimulus throughout.

The marriage is genuinely affectionate. The behavioral signature in her presence is uncharacteristically domesticated — meals taken together, ritual observed, fidelity (his side) reasonably maintained, deference to her cultural protocols visible. It is also doomed by structure: her sovereignty has political demands; his life is in the human world; the configuration cannot scale to the long horizon, and he cannot honestly subordinate to her court any more than she can to his Queens brownstone. The dissolution is acrimonious, public, and military (the conflict between her forces and his surface-world allies is documented in considerable property-damage detail), and the post-dissolution behavioral profile shows the familiar markers: increased verbal output, contract velocity, geographic displacement.

The Shiklah marriage's diagnostic value in the file is that it answers the question *what does a Wade Wilson relationship look like when the structural conditions of his pathology are met by the partner from the outset?* The answer is: better than otherwise, briefly, and not sustainably, because the structural conditions that make the relationship possible are themselves incompatible with the conditions that make a life possible.

## 10. The Mercs for Money — Managerial Failure as Repetition

Late in the period, the subject organizes a fee-sharing collective (the Mercs for Money: Stingray, Solo, Massacre, Foolkiller, Slapstick, Madcap, others in rotation) operating in a corporate-adjacent register, taking corporate contracts on behalf of legitimate-looking clients (notably under the patronage, briefly, of Steve Rogers's Avengers Unity initiative). The structure replicates the captive-attachment template in *managerial* form: he is the only payer, the only contract-source, the structural exit-controller; the team's members are dependent on his pipeline.

The arc's failure modes are individually varied and collectively diagnostic. He cannot manage them because he cannot bear the supervisory mirroring (their problems require him to be seen as a serious authority); he cannot bear the moral seriousness the legitimacy-frame demands of him (it activates the post-Rogers wound); he cannot bear the loss of any of them (Madcap's trajectory in particular replicates the Worm/Hospice template — a fellow damaged person whose damage Wilson cannot heal and who turns on him, and whose loss-or-betrayal he handles by acting out). The Mercs arc terminates in dispersal, mutual recrimination, and his retreat to solo operations, with the familiar absence of explicit grief and the familiar post-loss behavioral signature.

## 11. Eleanor, Custody, and the One Loss He Cannot Outrun

The custody loss of Eleanor — the operational details vary across the record; the pattern is that his life-configuration is structurally incompatible with full parental presence and that the formal arrangement reflects this — closes the period. It is the single loss in the file that the established defense stack does not metabolize. The humor flickers across the arc's documented scenes in a register that observers (Al, Weasel, Cable in passing) note as off — *too loud, then absent, then loud again*, with the absences elongating. The fourth-wall breaks across this stretch take on a confessional rather than evasive coloration; he begins addressing the reader directly about Eleanor in a way he has never previously addressed the reader directly about a person who matters to him, which is the defense and the symptom legible at the same surface.

The behavioral aftermath is the longest stretch of low-grade d


## Chronology IV — Recent History & Current State

# Chronology IV — Recent History & Current State

## Period under review
Approximately the last seven operational years of the subject's documented life — bracketed at the front end by the collapse of the Shiklah marriage and the loss of full custody of Eleanor Camacho-Wilson, and at the back end by the present moment of this file's compilation. This is the period in which the longitudinal patterns mapped in Sections 1–5 have, for the first time in the record, begun to bend — not toward health in any clinical sense, but toward a slightly wider tolerance for sustained attachment and a slightly longer mean interval between catastrophic self-sabotage events. The bending is small enough to be invisible at quarterly resolution and unmistakable at the seven-year span.

---

## 1. The Shiklah Rupture and the Monster-King Interregnum

The terminal phase of the Shiklah marriage is the inciting event of the current era. The relationship had been from inception a textbook instance of the subject's object-choice pathology — a literal devourer-queen, undisfigurable by his cancer, ungovernable by his sabotage attempts, selected precisely because the usual termination mechanisms (rejection on sight of his face, exhaustion under his testing, mortal vulnerability) were unavailable. Marriage to a being he could not damage and could not lose to ordinary causes briefly anchored him. Its collapse — Shiklah's pivot to invasion-of-the-surface and her remarriage to Dracula — left the subject in a configuration he had never previously occupied: publicly cuckolded, politically embroiled in monster-state diplomacy, and forced into the role of *king consort to a hostile foreign power*.

His behavioral response was diagnostic. He did not pursue Shiklah. He did not stage the expected reconciliation arc. Instead he metabolized the loss by acquiring an entirely new dependency network — the Monster Metropolis subjects who continued to recognize his nominal sovereignty after Shiklah's departure — and ruled them, for a period of months, with an uncharacteristically attentive paternalism. Observed behaviors during the regency: holding court in person rather than by proxy; settling minor disputes between subjects whose grievances were objectively trivial; sleeping in the throne room rather than in any of three available residential chambers; refusing, on at least four separate occasions logged by SHIELD monitoring, to leave the city even for high-value contracts.

This is captive-attachment at scale. He had constructed, by accident of marriage and political circumstance, an entire dependent population that could not in practical terms abandon him. The relief is visible in the contemporary record — verbal output decreased, fourth-wall frequency dropped to approximately half its baseline rate, and recreational violence outside the city limits dropped to its lowest documented level since the early Simone period. The regency was the longest sustained interval of regulated affect in the subject's adult life.

It ended, as such configurations always do for him, through external intrusion (the Stark-led monster-suppression campaign and the related anti-monster legislation cycle) compounded by his own inability to refuse a high-status invitation when extended (re-entry into mainstream Avengers-adjacent operations). He vacated the throne with a deliberateness that read at the time as flippancy and reads in retrospect as grief. He has not returned to the city in any sustained capacity since, and avoids the topic when prompted by surviving confidants.

---

## 2. Eleanor — The Custody Question as Organizing Variable

The single load-bearing relationship of the current era is the subject's relationship with his daughter. He does not have custody. He has never, across the documented record, had stable custody. Eleanor is presently in the practical guardianship of Preston (the former SHIELD agent whose consciousness was briefly bonded to the subject's own and whose family absorbed Eleanor following the Butler arc), with intermittent expansions and contractions of his access privileges that correspond, with near-perfect granularity, to his current employment, sobriety, threat-attractor status, and the felt safety of the household.

Behavioral signatures around Eleanor that distinguish this period from prior ones:

- **Visit preparation rituals.** Surveillance logs and incidental witness accounts establish a consistent pre-visit routine: shower (a behavior he otherwise performs irregularly), full-coverage civilian clothing including gloves and a wide-collared garment to minimize visible scarring at the throat, an attempt at hair (he is largely without it; the gesture is symbolic), and the acquisition of a gift selected with disproportionate care relative to the apparent stakes. Gifts skew toward items he himself was denied or would have wanted at her age — a tell.
- **Verbal modulation in her presence.** Recording-quality samples (her school events, two public outings) show a measurable reduction in profanity, fourth-wall references, and metacommentary. The reduction is not total; it is effortful. He cannot fully suppress the defenses but can throttle them, which he was demonstrably unable to do in equivalent contexts five years ago.
- **Departure protocol.** He consistently leaves before he is asked to leave, and consistently leaves earlier than the access window permits. This is preemptive rupture management — exiting on his own initiative rather than risk being asked to go, which would trigger the abandonment schema in front of her.
- **The post-visit pattern.** He is reliably observed in heavy alcohol consumption (volumes calibrated to his metabolism — i.e., functionally self-harming) and high-risk contract acceptance within 12–36 hours of every visit. The visits regulate him in the moment and destabilize him in the after; he is paying for the regulation in arrears.

Eleanor herself, in available accounts, regards him with the specific affect of a child who has been taught to love a parent at distance — neither idealizing nor rejecting, neither fully claiming him nor disowning him. She is, by all evidence, less damaged by him than he expects to have damaged her, which he finds destabilizing and cannot accept.

The custody question is the variable around which his current life is organized whether or not he is currently engaged with it. Contract selection skews increasingly toward jobs that would not, if exposed, terminate his access. Geographic positioning has shifted to keep him within commutable distance of the Preston household for extended periods, which is anomalous given his prior tendency to disappear into distant theaters under stress. He has, in the most recent eighteen months, twice declined contracts that would have required relocation longer than three weeks — a refusal pattern with no precedent in his career.

---

## 3. Vanessa — The Reopened Wound

The reactivation of contact with Vanessa Carlysle (Copycat) in the current period is the second major attachment vector and the one with the longest latency. The prior relationship — pre-Weapon X, terminated by his diagnosis-flight — has functioned for thirty-plus years of canonical time as the unhealed wound against which all subsequent partner-objects have been measured and found wanting (including Shiklah, who was selected partly because she did not resemble Vanessa in any axis and therefore could not provoke the comparison).

Recent contact has been intermittent, low-bandwidth, and conducted under operational pretexts rather than emotional ones — a transparent management strategy on his part. Observable patterns:

- He does not initiate. When she initiates, response latency is short (under six hours, atypical for him with any other contact). When he is forced by circumstance to initiate, he frames the contact as transactional (job referrals, intelligence requests, occasionally protective warnings).
- In her physical presence the humor defense is destabilized in a distinctive way: it does not decrease (as with Eleanor) but accelerates and becomes more pointed, more cruel, more rapid-cycling. This is the testing pattern in its acute form. She has, across multiple observed encounters, declined to be driven off by it, which produces in him a recognizable pattern of escalation followed by sudden collapse into momentary, almost inaudible sincerity — followed immediately by exit.
- He has not, in the current period, attempted to consolidate the contact into a defined relationship. The available evidence suggests he is afraid to. Her shapeshifting capacity — the canonical fact that she can wear his face, his body, his disfigurement — has been noted by him, in two separate logged statements to confidants, as both the most and the least bearable feature of any reunion. The ambivalence is precise: she is the only person whose presence does not require him to be alone in the body he occupies, and she is the only person from whom that mirroring cannot be refused.

The relationship is, at the present moment, in a sustained holding pattern that is itself unusual — he typically resolves such ambiguity by detonation. The holding is evidence of growth or evidence of exhaustion; the file cannot yet distinguish.

---

## 4. Cable — The Long Bond

The subject's relationship with Nathan Summers remains the single most stable interpersonal fixture of his adult life and is functioning, in the current period, at higher intensity than at any prior point on record. The relationship has survived: Cable's deaths (multiple), Cable's replacements by his own younger self, Cable's children's interventions, mutual betrayals of meaningful magnitude, and at least one documented period of mutual contract-killing-on-sight.

What sustains it, on the available evidence, is that Cable is the only attachment figure in the subject's network who is both (a) not killable by ordinary means (removing the loss-anxiety that destabilizes his other bonds) and (b) actively willing to be cruel back. The subject's testing pattern requires a respondent who will hit back without leaving. Cable hits back and does not leave. The configuration is durable.

In the current period the relationship is operating in its "old married" register — extended absences punctuated by joint operations conducted with minimal briefing, telepathic shorthand on Cable's side and verbal shorthand on the subject's, and a noticeable reduction in the subject's metacommentary when Cable is present (Cable will not engage the fourth-wall material, and the subject has learned, across decades, not to waste it on him). The conversations that have been incidentally captured have a striking quality of mutual diagnostic accuracy — Cable names the subject's patterns without comment or judgment, the subject permits the naming, and neither party expects the naming to change anything. This is the closest configuration to functional therapeutic alliance in the entire file, and it is occurring outside any clinical frame.

Cable has, per recent records, twice intervened to prevent the subject from accepting contracts whose exposure would have terminated his Eleanor access. He did so without explanation. The subject did not require one.

---

## 5. The Operational Network — Contraction and Refinement

The Mercs for Money venture, which dominated the middle period, has been quietly wound down. The managerial-failure pattern that section 1 identified played out in the predictable register: he could not tolerate the role of trusted employer, sabotaged the trust of his subordinates through unreliability and theft of contracts, and eventually liquidated the operation rather than confront the dependency he had created.

His current operational network is smaller than at any point since the early Kelly run. The functional core consists of:

- **Weasel** — re-stabilized after a long period of estrangement following Weasel's documented betrayal in the Posehn/Duggan period. The reconciliation is partial and the subject still does not extend full trust on intelligence-sensitive operations, but the rate of contact has recovered to roughly its mid-2000s baseline and the testing-pattern toward Weasel has subsided into a kind of ritualized rough affection.
- **Bob, Agent of (formerly) Hydra** — present, intermittent, used for low-stakes companionship as much as operational support. Bob's distinctive value to the subject is that he cannot be insulted out of the relationship; the testing pattern simply rebounds off his affect. The subject treats Bob with a tenderness he does not extend to higher-status confidants, presumably because Bob's incapacity to leave removes the threat.
- **Blind Al** — alive, present in the current residential arrangement when one exists, and operating now in something closer to a chosen-family configuration than the original captive-roommate setup. The subject has not formally released her from the original captivity framing because to do so would force him to confront its meaning; she has been free to leave for years and does not. The status quo is preserved by mutual tacit agreement, which is itself unprecedented in his relational repertoire.
- **Preston** — primary mediating relationship with Eleanor, treated with a respect that borders on the formal. He does not joke at her in the way he jokes at everyone else. She is the only adult in his current network of whom this is true.

Notable contractions: he is not embedded in any of the standing super-team configurations he previously sought (Avengers, X-Force, X-Men proper). Recent invitations to join such configurations — at least three documented in the past eighteen months — have been declined, deferred, or sabotaged at the audition phase. This is consistent with the section 5 pressure-point analysis: he has learned, expensively, that admission to the moral community on offered terms reliably terminates in catastrophic betrayal (Osborn, Hydra-Rogers, by-extension Coulson). The current refusal to accept legitimization is, by his standards, a mature adaptation. It is also lonely in a register he does not appear to have language for.

---

## 6. Residential, Logistical, and Routine Patterns

**Residence.** No fixed primary address. Current pattern is a three- to four-node rotation among: (1) a perpetually month-to-month safehouse in Queens whose lease is held under a deliberately conspicuous false name; (2) the residual Blind Al apartment, which functions as his anchor address and contains the only personal effects he has retained for more than a year; (3) intermittent crash accommodations at Weasel's current operational base; (4) hotel rooms selected for proximity to the current contract, paid in cash, occupied for no more than four consecutive nights.

The rotation is not security-driven in the operational sense — his enemies can find him whenever they choose. It is regulation-driven. He cycles to prevent any single location from accumulating the affective weight that would make leaving it difficult.

**Diet.** Caloric intake remains anomalously high (metabolic demand of the healing factor). Composition has shifted in the current period away from the chimichanga signifier that dominated the middle era (a brand he himself appears to have grown tired of performing) toward an apparently random sampling driven by whichever delivery vector is fastest at the moment of hunger. He eats alone in 90%+ of observed instances. He eats with Eleanor when permitted and the food is then selected for her preference; this is the closest thing to a shared meal he reliably participates in.

**Sleep.** Fragmented. Best available data suggests two to four hours per cycle, multiple cycles per twenty-four-hour period, with no clear circadian anchor. The healing factor's metabolic demand likely contributes; the hyperarousal substrate identified in section 4 likely contributes more. He sleeps in tactical positioning even in low-threat environments (facing entry points, weapon within reach) — a habit he has not lost in any period of the record.

**Self-care.** Erratic. Personal grooming is event-driven (visits to Eleanor; rare operational contexts requiring un-masked presentation) rather than maintenance-driven. The mask is on more often than off, including in solo residential contexts, which is a regression from the brief Monster Metropolis period when he had no need to mask among subjects who themselves bore visible difference.

**Substance use.** Alcohol consumption remains the primary substance behavior, in volumes that would be terminal for an unaltered human and that are, for him, functionally analogous to repetitive minor self-injury — the ritual rather than the effect is the point. Post-Eleanor-visit consumption is the largest reliable spike. The chase-of-unobtainable-intoxication pattern persists with various recreational substances, attempted in increasingly exotic combinations; none have produced sustained effect, and he has, across the period, occasionally been observed to laugh at his own pursuit of intoxication mid-attempt, which is a new register and possibly an early sign of the insight beginning, very partially, to become integrative.

**Communications.** Phone discipline poor; he is reachable through perhaps a dozen channels and uses all of them. The fourth-wall material has not abated in his self-talk (it is, in the file's view, the most stable feature of his cognition) but has subsided in face-to-face interactions with the small inner circle, who have collectively, over years, demonstrated that they will neither indulge it nor flee from it. The reduction is contextual and conditional. With strangers, contractors, and adversaries it remains his default operating register.

---

## 7. The Mortality Question, Updated

The chronic suicidal ideation documented in section 4 remains chronic, ego-syntonic, and unconsummated. The romanticized investment in personified Death has, in the current period, receded from the front of his expressed material — possibly because the relevant cosmic configurations have shifted, possibly because Eleanor's existence has introduced a competing libidinal object that requires him alive, possibly because thirty years of unconsummated ideation eventually exhausts even his capacity for romanticization. The ideation is now expressed less as longing and more as tired joke. This is, paradoxically, a worse prognostic indicator in some respects — the libidinization at least supplied a structure — and a better one in others, in that it reflects a partial relinquishment of the fantasy of resolution.

He has not, in the current period, sought any of the documented mechanisms that have previously produced temporary mortality (Carbonadium, the various device-mediated suppressions of the healing factor). The cessation of that pattern is the largest single behavioral shift of the era. Inferred reading: he has decided, without articulating the decision, that Eleanor's existence makes his death currently impermissible. This is the first time in the documented record that an attachment has been valued more highly than the unobtainable rest.

---

## 8. Public Profile and Cultural Position

The subject's public visibility is presently at its highest documented level. He is recognized on sight by civilians in major markets; he is referenced in popular culture; he has been (variously, and with degrees of formality) inducted into and ejected from multiple super-team rosters; he is, by any operational measure, a public figure. He manages this exposure through the same humor-as-armor mechanism that governs his interpersonal life, with the public mask functioning as a load-distribution mechanism — the more he performs the role, the less of him is required to be present in any given performance.

The cultural visibility is, by his own incidental admissions, a complicated good. It produces income (contract rates have risen markedly); it produces protection (he is too visible for many of his former adversaries to act against him in the manner they once did); it produces the legitimization-by-recognition that he is dangerously susceptible to, requiring active management. He has not, in the current period, been comprehensively manipulated by a high-status authority in the Osborn or Hydra-Rogers register. He has refused at least two such overtures that the file is aware of, in both cases at material cost. This is the second major behavioral shift of the era and the one with the most explanatory power for his current relative stability.

---

## 9. Present State — Synthesis

The subject is, at the moment of this file's compilation, in the most regulated configuration of his adult life. The qualifier matters: his baseline is dysregulated, his "regulated" state would qualify any unaltered person for inpatient care, and the regulation is held in place by a small number of attachments whose loss in any combination would precipitate immediate collapse into the prior patterns. He is not well. He is, by his own standards, less unwell than he has been.

The mechanism of the improvement is consistent with the prognostic note in section 5: not insight, which he continues to possess in clinically useless abundance, but the slow accumulation of bonds that have survived his testing. Eleanor (testing not yet fully deployed — she is too young, and he is too protective of her, to subject her to the full pattern). Cable (testing exhausted decades ago; the bond proven). Vanessa (testing reactivated and being slowly absorbed). Blind Al (the testing converted to ritual). Weasel and Bob (testing rebounded). Preston (testing modulated by the mediation of Eleanor). This network is six people. It has been six years in the building. It is the largest stable attachment network the file can document across his entire adult life.

The trajectory is positive at a rate that is barely measurable across the seven-year window and that would be invisible at any shorter timescale. He continues to cycle through the isolation → forced attachment → idealization → self-sabotage → loss → ideation → dissociation → re-isolation pattern. The cycles are longer. The catastrophic terminal phases are less catastrophic. The re-isolation phases are less complete; he returns to a network now rather than to nothing.

He is held permanently at the moment of breaking, as section 4 established, by a biology that will not let him collapse. What this file can now observe, that earlier compilations could not, is that *being held permanently at the moment of breaking is itself, given sufficient time, a substrate on which something can be built* — not healing, which is unavailable to him, but the gradual replacement of broken patterns with patterns that are also broken but break less destructively. He is, slowly, building a life out of the materials available to a person who cannot die and cannot rest. The materials are not adequate to the task. He is performing the task with them anyway. This is the current state of the subject and the operational baseline against which subsequent developments will be measured.


## Medical History

# UATU DOSSIER — SECTION 04: MEDICAL HISTORY

## Subject: WILSON, Wade Winston ("Deadpool")

---

## 4.0 Preface: The Body as the Central Datum

Every other section of this file describes a man. This section describes a *condition* — a continuously failing and continuously rebuilt biological object that the man inhabits. The medical history of Wade Wilson is the load-bearing substrate of every behavioral, psychiatric, and relational pattern recorded elsewhere. To understand him as a subject of surveillance one must first understand that his soma is itself a kind of perpetual emergency, and that almost every observable behavior is a downstream metabolism of that emergency.

For clarity, the record is divided into four longitudinal strata: (1) pre-cancer baseline and developmental medical record; (2) the index oncological event and the Department K / Workshop iatrogenic phase; (3) the post-Weapon X chronic state, including the permanent steady-state of cancer-versus-regeneration; (4) the cumulative trauma log — discrete injuries, transformations, exposures, and surgical events sustained over the documented mercenary career — with notes on the psychological residue each leaves.

---

## 4.1 Pre-Diagnosis Baseline (approx. childhood through late twenties)

The pre-cancer medical record is *officially* sparse and *actually* almost certainly extensive, the gap itself a finding. What can be inferred:

- **Childhood injuries consistent with chronic physical abuse.** The contradictory origin tableaux Wilson generates (Kelly, #33; Way flashbacks; Posehn/Duggan callbacks) consistently feature paternal or maternal violence, regardless of which parent is the perpetrator in a given telling. The reliable detail across versions is the *fact* of repeated childhood injury; the *attribution* shifts. Surveillance-grade inference: the body learned, before adolescence, that pain arrives from the people charged with care. This is a somatic prior that long predates Ajax.
- **Military service-era record.** Brief U.S. special-operations enlistment, terminated for insubordination with secondary psychiatric flag (Nicieza flashbacks; later Way fragments). Discharge-era physicals would have documented: scarring inconsistent with combat exposure alone (likely childhood-origin); elevated baseline cortisol indicators; probable history of head trauma (boxing? street fighting? domestic? all attested in different tellings). No documented major surgeries pre-diagnosis; standard immunizations; no significant chronic illness.
- **Pre-diagnosis substance use.** Heavy episodic drinking, recreational stimulants in the mercenary years (Tangier, Balkans). At normal physiology these were functional; he could get drunk, he could come down. This window is the only period of his life in which intoxication was *achievable*, a fact whose loss after Weapon X registers more heavily than the file's surface acknowledges.
- **Sexual and reproductive health.** Active. Vanessa Carlysle relationship period documents nothing remarkable. Conception of Eleanor (with Carmelita Camacho) post-dates Weapon X, indicating the healing factor did not sterilize him — fertility is preserved through the transformation, a fact of operational and personal consequence later.

**Baseline finding.** A body already inscribed with chronic-trauma physiology, but biologically ordinary: it could be hurt, healed, intoxicated, satisfied, exhausted, and would eventually die in the standard human way.

---

## 4.2 The Index Event: Diagnosis

The diagnosis is the formative medical event of his life and the hinge of all subsequent pathology.

- **Tumor distribution.** Writers vary; the convergent reading is **multifocal metastatic carcinoma**, with confirmed CNS involvement (brain), hepatic involvement (liver), and pulmonary involvement (lungs). Primary site never reliably established; the most consistent inference is that it was already metastatic at presentation.
- **Prognosis at diagnosis.** Terminal. Estimated survival under conventional treatment: months. No surgical option; chemotherapy palliative at best.
- **Behavioral response.** Documented across multiple flashbacks: abrupt severance of the Vanessa Carlysle relationship without disclosure of reason; geographic withdrawal; substance escalation; suicide ideation that he did not act on but documented to himself by acquiring means. The pattern — *do not let the loved one watch the dying* — recurs across every subsequent loss event. The diagnosis taught him that to love is to be obligated to spare the other from the spectacle of your destruction.
- **Decision to enroll in Department K's Workshop.** Framed officially as a clinical trial offering experimental cure. Wilson signed under conditions of terminal desperation and demonstrably without informed consent in any modern sense. This act — *trading the body to an institution that promised cure* — becomes the template betrayal against which every subsequent institutional offer (Avengers, SHIELD/Rogers, the various government contracts) will be unconsciously measured.

---

## 4.3 The Workshop / Hospice Phase: Iatrogenic Origin of the Current Soma

The Department K facility ("the Workshop," colloquially "the Hospice"; Kelly, *Deadpool* vol. 2 #-1, #11, #25, #33; later returns under Posehn/Duggan and Bunn) is the site of the procedure and of the trauma. Medically:

- **Genetic graft.** Wolverine-derived healing-factor genetic material introduced via a process never fully detailed in canon but consistently described as combining viral vector, marrow ablation/replacement, and forced expression under stress. The "stress" component was operationalized as torture: Killebrew and Ajax (Francis Fanny) used near-lethal injury, sensory deprivation, and asphyxiation to provoke the graft into expression. The healing factor, per the Workshop's empirical method, would not "switch on" without the body being made to need it.
- **Outcome.** Graft took. Cancer was not eliminated — it was *outcompeted*. The regenerative tissue replicates at a rate sufficient to outpace tumor expansion, but the tumor lineage was never extirpated. The result is a permanent dynamic equilibrium: every cell line in his body, including malignant lines, regenerates continuously; the malignant lines manifest visibly as the scar-tumor lattice of the skin and inferentially throughout deep tissue.
- **Disfigurement.** The skin presentation — keloid-like nodular scarring, ulcerative patches, persistent erythema, areas of necrotic-appearing tissue that regenerate without ever achieving normal architecture — is *the cure working as designed*. It is not a side effect to be corrected; it is the visible signature of the equilibrium. This is medically critical and frequently misunderstood (including by Wilson, in his more punishing moods, who treats the face as evidence of his failure rather than his survival).
- **Pain.** The healing factor restored cellular integrity but did not modify nociception. Pain receptors function normally and, by some accounts (Posehn/Duggan medical scenes), hypertrophically — the regeneration of nerve endings appears to leave them transiently *more* sensitive during repair phases. Subject experiences continuous low-grade pain (the regeneration of cancerous tissue is itself painful) punctuated by acute pain events whenever injury occurs.
- **Iatrogenic psychological injury.** Catalogued separately in §03 and §05, but medically relevant here: the Workshop coupled care-language to torture. Killebrew offered explanations; Ajax offered cruelty. Wilson left the facility with a permanent affective conflation of clinical settings, medical authority, and torture. He does not tolerate examination. He has not, on the record, submitted to a full medical workup since.

The Hospice phase ended with: Wilson killing fellow patient Worm (manipulated into it via the betting pool, a sadistic protocol Ajax ran); being "killed" by Ajax and discarded; reviving in the trash; and escaping. Each of these is a discrete trauma with its own residue. The death-and-revival, in particular, is the inaugural instance of the pattern that will define his life: *he was killed and was not allowed to stay dead*.

---

## 4.4 The Current Steady State: Chronic Conditions

### 4.4.1 Oncological

- **Diagnosis (active):** metastatic carcinoma, multifocal, indefinite duration, never in remission.
- **Status:** controlled by endogenous regeneration; uncontrolled by any conventional or mutant-medicine intervention attempted (Carbonadium poisoning arc demonstrated that *suppression* of the healing factor produces immediate cancer dominance, i.e., the cancer is still actively lethal whenever the factor falters).
- **Implication:** every moment of his life is a moment of dying that has been deferred by approximately the duration of that moment. There is no future state in which he is "well." The closest available state is *currently regenerating faster than currently dying*.

### 4.4.2 Dermatological / Surface

- Universal scar-tumor coverage; thickened, irregular epidermal architecture; reduced normal pigmentation; episodic sloughing and re-growth; hair growth absent or sporadic over scar fields (the canonical baldness is secondary to the dermatological condition, not independent).
- Sensory: tactile sensation intact but altered; reports across writers of hypersensitivity to certain textures (rubber, latex — the mask is tolerated through habituation rather than comfort).
- **Behavioral consequence:** absolute mask discipline in public; the mask is not iconography, it is a clinical accommodation. Removal in private is selective and almost always associated with a deliberate test of the witness (see §05, pressure points).

### 4.4.3 Neurological

- **Substrate damage.** CNS tumors and continuous neuronal regeneration produce a brain whose structural connectivity is never stable for long periods. Memory consolidation is impaired; long-term episodic memory is unreliable not solely by repression but because the cells encoding it are physically rewritten on rolling cycles.
- **Telepathic resistance.** Verified by independent observers (Emma Frost, Cable, Charles Xavier in passing). The phenomenology, per the telepaths who have entered him: a structured cacophony, multiple distinct internal voices, fragmentary imagery that does not chain into stable narrative, intermittent meta-awareness that the telepath is *also* a character in the scene. Telepaths exit voluntarily and tend not to return. This is functionally a defense against the most invasive intelligence-gathering modality the Marvel surveillance environment offers; from a file-keeper's perspective, his mind is a denied area.
- **Cognitive profile.** Verbal fluency preserved and elevated. Working memory in combat: excellent. Long-horizon planning: poor. Impulse inhibition: very poor. Pattern recognition (tactical): excellent. Pattern recognition (interpersonal): excellent but distorted by trauma-derived priors. Insight: high. Use of insight to modify behavior: minimal.
- **Voice phenomenon ("the boxes").** Discussed at length in §03; medically, the substrate is overdetermined — trauma-dissociative architecture sitting on top of organic neurological disorganization. The voices are stable in characterological content across years; this stability argues against pure psychotic origin and for a structurally dissociated parts-of-self model.

### 4.4.4 Metabolic / Endocrine

- **Caloric requirement: enormous.** Accelerated cellular turnover demands intake on the order of multiples of normal adult requirement. Behaviorally documented: chronic, voracious eating; preference for high-density carbohydrate and lipid sources (the chimichanga obsession is dietetically rational as well as a bit); intolerance of caloric restriction (irritability, slowed regeneration, intrusive cancer symptoms).
- **Pharmacokinetics: accelerated.** Hepatic metabolism is extraordinary; substances are cleared at rates that approach intravenous-administration windows even when taken orally. Alcohol clearance approaches 10x baseline human or higher (variable by writer). Anesthetic agents at standard doses are functionally placebo.
- **Sleep.** Disrupted. Across all runs the implication is chronic insomnia or fragmented sleep, with periods of crash-collapse rather than scheduled rest. The healing factor does not appear to require sleep for tissue maintenance; the disruption is upstream — hyperarousal, hypervigilance, the unavailability of the parasympathetic state that initiates sleep.
- **Fertility:** preserved (Eleanor).
- **Aging:** dramatically retarded. Subject has not visibly aged over the operationally documented period; biological age is decoupled from chronological age. Long-term implication: the file should expect this subject to persist indefinitely barring extraordinary measures.

### 4.4.5 Immunological

- Functional immunity to most pathogens and most toxins. Demonstrated resistance to: snake venoms, common chemical warfare agents, radiation (sustained exposure causes injury but recovery), most heavy metals.
- **Known vulnerabilities:** Carbonadium (documented suppression of healing factor; cancer reasserts within hours); certain magic-coded effects that bypass cellular regeneration; complete cellular destruction at a rate faster than regeneration can compensate (incineration to atomic dispersal — the temporary state, recovery has nonetheless occurred in canon under certain cosmic conditions); anything that severs the regeneration mechanism at its source.

### 4.4.6 Sensory and Speech

- Vision, hearing, olfaction, gustation: intact.
- Speech: intact; in fact a defining feature, with verbal output at sustained volumes that other professionals in his field find tactically counterproductive. The constancy of speech is itself a medical/psychological observable: it is the audible signature of an organism that cannot tolerate the parasympathetic quiet that silence would invite.

---

## 4.5 The Cumulative Trauma Log: Discrete Major Events

What follows is a non-exhaustive but representative log of documented injuries, transformations, and exposures, organized by category. Each entry notes the medical event and the psychological residue.

### 4.5.1 Dismemberments and Decapitations

- **Hand severance — multiple, routine.** Across nearly every long arc. Regrowth within hours to days depending on stress on the system. Residue: complete loss of normal protective response to threats against the hands; combat behavior assumes hands are expendable.
- **Decapitation — multiple events.** Documented continuation of consciousness in the severed head for extended periods (most explicitly in *Deadpool Kills the Marvel Universe* and in mainline appearances where the head retains speech). Reattachment achieved manually; partial reattachments have produced cosmetic asymmetries until subsequent regeneration. Residue: catastrophic for normal-human notions of bodily integrity; for Wilson, treated as inconvenience-grade. He jokes during decapitation events, a fact which captures more about him than any clinical interview ever has.
- **Lower-body severance / bisection — recorded.** Recovery complete. Residue: subject narrates the experience to whoever is present, including bystanders and assailants, as a form of regulation.
- **Limb regrowth at non-original sites.** Anecdotal incidents (Way, Duggan) of mis-grown tissue, supernumerary digits during stress-accelerated regeneration, requiring trimming. He has reportedly performed this trimming himself.

### 4.5.2 Skinning and Full-Surface Injuries

- **Hulk encounter:** complete dermal stripping documented. Recovery on the order of days. Residue: one of the few categories of injury he refers to with discomfort rather than humor; the prospect of being skinned again is one of the rare specific fears in his record.
- **Wolverine encounter(s):** multiple bisections and deep lacerations. Residue: complex; Wolverine is a near-double (source of the graft, fellow chronic-pain healing-factor sufferer) and the violence between them is shadowed by a kinship Wilson cannot articulate.
- **Incineration events:** multiple, recovery confirmed; threshold of permanent dispersal not reliably established. Residue: minimal at the conscious level; one suspects accumulating somatic dread, given the increased frequency of fire-related gallows humor across late-period material.

### 4.5.3 Skull and CNS Injuries

- **Skull replacement / cranial reconstruction:** recorded. Brain matter regrowth implied; the question of whether the regrown brain *encodes the same person* is canonically left ambiguous and is the locus of his deepest fear, expressed only obliquely.
- **Penetrating brain trauma:** routine. He has been shot through the head on numerous documented occasions. Recovery complete; subjective report variable, including occasional reports of "missing time" or shifted internal voice constellations post-incident.
- **Lobotomy-equivalent procedures:** various enemies have attempted neurosurgical interference. Regeneration has reversed all such attempts on the record. Residue: extreme aversion to medical and quasi-medical instrumentation, restraint, and clinical environments.

### 4.5.4 Toxicological and Pharmacological Events

- **Carbonadium poisoning (Posehn/Duggan, ongoing through the run):** the only documented sustained suppression of the healing factor. During the suppression window subject experienced rapid cancer reassertion, acute symptomatology, and confrontation with the prospect of ordinary death. Residue: catastrophic — the brief window of mortal vulnerability did not relieve him; it terrified him in a way ordinary biological wellness never could have, because mortality means losing the only feature of his existence (the deferred dying) that he has organized his identity around.
- **Anesthetic / sedative attempts:** consistently fail at conventional doses. Successful sedation events have required mutant-grade or magical agents. Residue: he refuses sedation even when offered for ordinary purposes; the experience of being chemically unable-to-be-restrained has become an identity-relevant fact.
- **Self-medication.** Alcohol, recreational drugs, attempted opiates — none achieve sustained effect. The *pursuit* of intoxication is itself a chronic behavior (see §4.6).
- **Symbiote and other parasitic bondings (various crossover events):** the body has hosted entities of multiple ontological categories; in each case the healing factor and the neurological noise have produced atypical bonding profiles, generally hostile to the entity. Residue: amused dismissal in narration; suspected deeper distress about the loss of bodily sovereignty.

### 4.5.5 Transformations and Atypical States

- **Zombification (various alternate-universe and crossover events):** the healing factor and the zombie pathogen produce idiosyncratic outcomes; in some recorded states only the head remains animate. Residue: this is the territory where his metacommentary becomes most aggressive, suggesting these episodes approach the limit of what humor can metabolize.
- **Cosmic-scale exposures (multiple):** survival of events that should have erased ordinary matter. The record establishes a *floor* of biological resilience that has not, in the documented period, been definitively breached.
- **Time-dilation and chronological displacement events:** subject has experienced extended subjective durations in isolated states (the Sluggoth, the Time Variance Authority arcs in modern material, others). Residue: increased difficulty distinguishing memory from confabulation, already an organic problem, now layered with genuine temporal disorientation.

### 4.5.6 Reproductive and Familial Medical Events

- **Conception of Eleanor (with Carmelita Camacho):** ordinary biological event, confirming gametic viability. Pregnancy and delivery uneventful per available record.
- **Marriage to Shiklah:** the medical record of a marital relationship between a healing-factor host and a Succubus monarch is *sui generis*; the union appears to have produced no progeny but considerable somatic strain that he has consistently refused to characterize as such.

---

## 4.6 Substance Use: A Pattern Note

Standard substance-use diagnostic frameworks do not apply cleanly because the pharmacological effect is functionally absent. Nonetheless the *behavior* of substance pursuit is operationally significant and qualifies as a use disorder by behavioral criteria.

- **Alcohol.** Consumption volumes that would be lethal in normal humans; sustained drinking in bars, often in extended solitary sessions; tolerance absolute. The *behavior* is regulatory — the act of drinking, the social environment of the bar, the ritual — rather than chemical.
- **Recreational drugs.** Sporadic attempts; results uniformly disappointing. Continued attempts despite known futility are themselves diagnostic.
- **Caffeine and sugar:** consumed in enormous quantities; closer to caloric intake than to stimulant use.
- **Food.** Borderline-ritualized eating, particularly of specific items (the chimichanga preference is iconic but representative of a broader pattern of fixated comfort consumption). Food is one of the few sensory experiences that delivers what it promises — the healing factor does not block taste, only intoxication — which makes it a disproportionately important regulator.

The interpretive frame: substance pursuit in Wilson is *the chase for an unavailable parasympathetic state*. His nervous system never gets to come down. The substances are an attempt to force the descent; the body refuses. This is the deepest somatic loneliness in the record — he cannot get out of his own activation, ever, by any means he has access to. The drinking is a daily losing argument with his own biology.

---

## 4.7 Medical Care Utilization

For practical surveillance purposes:

- **Will not attend conventional medical facilities.** Hospitals, clinics, and clinical research settings trigger the Workshop conditioning. He will leave against medical advice in nearly all cases. The few documented exceptions involve facilities staffed by people he personally trusts (Weasel's improvisations; Preston in some arcs; the X-Men medical bay under duress).
- **Self-treats most injuries.** Field-grade suturing, foreign-body extraction, manual reduction of dislocations, manual reattachment of severed parts. He owns and travels with surgical instruments; the healing factor makes the asepsis question moot.
- **Will accept care from a small set of trusted figures.** Blind Al (within her capacity); Weasel (within his, which is comically limited); occasional reluctant accommodation of Cable. The criterion is not skill but trust; he will let a friend who cannot help him try to help him before he will let a stranger who could.
- **Refuses anesthesia in nearly all cases.** Partly because it does not work; partly because the experience of being unconscious in another's hands is the single condition his nervous system most strenuously refuses.
- **Avoids imaging and laboratory studies.** No reliable recent imaging exists for this subject in any database we have penetrated. The body, in its disclosed-to-clinicians form, is a blank.

---

## 4.8 Synthetic Reading: The Soma as Trap

The medical history collapses into a single structural fact, which the file must hold steady against all the noise of individual events: **this subject's body was engineered to prevent the resolution of his suffering.**

Ordinary biology offers three exits from a state of unbearable distress: collapse (somat


## Somatic Atlas

# UATU ANALYSIS FILE: WADE WINSTON WILSON ("DEADPOOL")
## Section: SOMATIC ATLAS

---

The subject's body is a unique observational target because it is simultaneously the most expressive and the least diagnostically reliable surface in the file. Two facts dominate: (a) the regenerating tissue rebuilds *function* but not always *prior habit pattern*, so micro-tics drift across months in ways that would, in a non-regenerating subject, indicate stroke or neurological insult; (b) the disfigurement enforces near-total concealment in public, meaning the somatic record falls into two sharply separated corpora — the masked/clothed public body, observable continuously, and the unmasked private body, observable only when he permits it. The contrast between the two registers is itself diagnostic.

---

### 1. Resting Architecture and Postural Baseline

There is no true rest state. Surveillance footage across the full record shows that even when ostensibly stationary — couch, barstool, contract briefing, hospital gurney — the subject is producing continuous low-amplitude motion: a heel bounce (right foot more often than left, approximately 2–3 Hz, sustained for minutes), finger drumming against thigh in patterns that occasionally resolve into the rhythm of whatever music was last in the environment, jaw working on absent gum, and a slow rotational adjustment of the shoulders every twenty to forty seconds as if testing range of motion against a tightness that has just been re-grown. This baseline motor noise is the postural correlate of the affective rule established in Personality: *do not let anything settle*.

Standing posture is wider than necessary, weight distributed approximately 60/40 onto the dominant (right) leg, with the non-dominant foot slightly forward and turned out — a fencer's or shooter's offset stance maintained even when nothing is happening. Shoulders are set high and slightly forward; the trapezius is chronically engaged. Head is carried forward of the spine's vertical line by perhaps two centimeters, producing a habitual slight downward gaze that he compensates for by tilting the chin up when addressing a target. This produces the characteristic underchin presentation in mask: head tipped back, hood-eyes lifted.

Seated, he cannot occupy a chair conventionally. Cataloged variants, in approximate frequency order: straddling the chair backward; one leg tucked beneath him; sitting sideways with feet over an armrest; sitting on the back of the chair with feet on the seat; perched on the chair's edge with elbows on knees; full reclined slump with legs extended and crossed at the ankles. The conventional upright seated posture appears in the record almost exclusively in two contexts — formal contract negotiations (performed correctness as part of the professional mask) and the rare scenes of post-loss collapse, where he sits very still in conventional posture and the stillness itself is the alarm signal.

Sleep architecture is fragmentary. The regenerating CNS produces high baseline arousal; observed sleep is rarely consolidated beyond ninety-minute blocks before micro-arousal. Position is reliably on the side, dominant arm under the pillow, non-dominant hand near or under a weapon, knees drawn partway toward chest — a defensive curl modified for rapid extension. He talks in sleep; content is fragmentary and frequently in the cadence of his internal narrators rather than his own waking voice. Sleep onset requires either complete exhaustion (post-combat) or sensory saturation (television at volume, music in earbuds, sometimes both). Silence prevents sleep; he has been documented sleeping more successfully in transit (cargo holds, train compartments, the back of a van mid-extraction) than in domestic settings.

---

### 2. Gait and Locomotion

Walking gait, observed at distance: a slight forward lean from the hips, stride length 5–10% longer than expected for his height, with a barely perceptible roll to the shoulders that reads as casual and is in fact the residue of perpetual readiness — the shoulders are pre-loading for a draw. Arm swing is asymmetric, with the dominant arm swinging less than the non-dominant because the dominant hand is, more often than not, either resting near a holster line or carrying something. Footfall is quieter than his body mass would predict; he lands ball-of-foot first in operational settings and heel-first in civilian ones, and the switch between these two modes occurs unconsciously within two or three steps of crossing a threshold he perceives as relevant.

He cannot walk past a reflective surface without registering it — head turn is suppressed but the eye flicks, and on the unmasked body a microsecond of postural tension appears in the trapezius. He cannot walk past a thrown weapon target (knife in a wall, axe in a stump, anything with a haft) without the dominant hand opening and closing once.

Running is efficient and unornamented in operational contexts. In comedic-performative contexts (which appear in the record more often than they should) he affects an exaggerated cartoon run — high knees, swinging arms — which is itself a tell: when the running becomes funny, the situation has crossed into the territory he cannot otherwise metabolize.

Stair climbing is two-at-a-time, ascending; descending, he takes them one at a time but along the diagonal, which conserves momentum and keeps the body sideways to the line of fire from below. He prefers to take corners on the outside arc (wider field of view) and reliably touches doorframes with the dominant hand as he passes through them — a habit consistent across decades and registers, function unclear, probably a vestigial threshold-checking ritual.

---

### 3. Hands

The hands are the most communicative part of him and the part that has been regrown most often. They are large for his frame, knuckles thickened by repeated injury-and-regeneration cycles, with skin that registers as smoother than the rest of his body because new tissue dominates. Manicure: none; nails are kept short by chewing rather than clipping, with a characteristic asymmetry (the thumb and index of the non-dominant hand are chewed shorter than the rest, indicating which hand goes to the mouth when thinking).

Gesture vocabulary in conversation is extensive and italianate — both hands deployed, palm-up presentations for jokes, mock-conjuring flourishes for emphasis, finger-guns at least once per substantive interaction. He uses an exaggerated air-quote gesture frequently and ironically. When listening, the hands either occupy themselves (coin, knife, dismantled lighter, food) or rest in the front pocket of whatever he's wearing — never folded, never clasped, the folded-hands posture appearing in the record only in the same handful of moments as the conventional seated position, and meaning the same thing.

Hand tics under specific states:

- **Calm with one of the trusted few**: open posture, gesture amplitude reduced, fingers occasionally trace the line of his own forearm or jaw — a self-soothing pattern consistent with subjects who were not reliably soothed in early development.
- **Operational baseline**: dominant hand at four o'clock, near the primary holster; non-dominant hand free for the secondary draw, knife throw, or grab. Fingers of the dominant hand flex in sets of four, slowly, the way a pianist warms up.
- **Acute stress / pre-violence**: gesture amplitude *increases* paradoxically, jokes accompanied by larger and more theatrical hand movements that mask the draw. The actual draw, when it comes, is one of the smallest movements in his body — economical, low, often executed mid-sentence.
- **Intimacy (rare and observed mostly with Vanessa, briefly Shiklah, in tender register with Eleanor)**: hands become uncharacteristically still. He approaches contact slowly, often initiating with the back of his fingers rather than the palm, as though uncertain his hand will be tolerated. This is one of the most reliable cross-arc tells in the somatic record.
- **Mirror exposure / forced unmasking**: hands go to face — covering, turning away, or paradoxically pulling the skin tight to display the worst of it (the "look at it" gesture, aggressive self-presentation as a defense against being looked at).
- **Grief**: he does not cradle his head; he grips the back of the neck with one hand and squeezes, hard enough to leave temporary pressure marks on intact skin. This is among the very few somatic patterns that has remained stable across the entire run.

---

### 4. Face (Masked) and the Architecture of the Mask

The mask is a prosthetic affect surface. He has trained, over decades, to push expression into the fabric: the brow ridges of the lenses lift and pull together via deliberate forehead recruitment; the mouth area is animated by jaw and lip movement strong enough to deform the cloth. Surveillance review of mask-on footage shows that he is, in fact, *more* facially expressive when masked than unmasked, because the mask is a stage and he is performing on it. The expressiveness is unidirectional — broad emotional postures (mock-shock, mock-grief, comic eyebrow raise) are easy to read on the mask; the subtler micro-expressions of genuine affect are absorbed and lost.

Head movement compensates for the loss of facial nuance. Masked, he tilts his head far more than the average human — sharp side-tilts (curiosity, dog-like), forward dips (acknowledgment), full back-tilts (laughter, mock-exasperation). The tilt vocabulary substitutes for the lost eyebrow-and-mouth register and is itself diagnostic: an *uncharacteristically still mask* in conversation is one of the strongest predictors that he is approaching collapse.

Masked vocalizations are accompanied by exaggerated mouth shapes pressed into the cloth, which makes lipreading from the mask both possible and frequently *invited* — he wants to be read, but on his terms. He adjusts the mask continuously: a two-finger tug at the lower jaw line approximately every two to four minutes in baseline, more often under stress, as if it has shifted and needs reseating. It rarely actually needs reseating. The gesture is self-soothing under a thin operational pretext.

---

### 5. Face (Unmasked)

The unmasked face is rarely photographed and never voluntarily by him. Surveillance and incidental capture across the run permit the following observations.

Underneath the lesion architecture, the underlying musculature retains a fully normal expressive range, but the skin's restricted elasticity flattens the readable signal. What survives:

- The eyes are clear and unaffected, light blue-grey, with a habitual squint at the lateral canthi that predates the disfigurement (visible in pre-Weapon X record) and is exaggerated by it. Eye contact pattern is unusual: he either holds contact too long (testing, daring the other party to flinch) or refuses it entirely, with very little intermediate calibration. The middle register — the ordinary glances and looks-away of normal conversation — is largely absent.
- The mouth retains full mobility and is the most-watched feature in his unmasked register; he is aware of this and uses it accordingly, often smiling at maximum amplitude (teeth bared) as a self-protective aggression. The default unmasked expression at rest is a slight asymmetric pull at the right corner — sardonic, pre-loaded.
- Blink rate is elevated above baseline (estimated 25–30 per minute against a population mean of 15–20), consistent with the chronic arousal state.
- The skin itself moves — the lesions visibly shift, weep, scab and re-form on observable timescales. He is aware of this in any setting with sufficient light and will angle away from the source.

The pattern of self-grooming on the unmasked face is paradoxical: he does not avoid touching it (an avoidance subject would), but the touches are functional and aggressive — checking, scratching, pulling at loose tissue — rather than tender. He does not have a *care* relationship with his own face. He has a *managerial* one.

---

### 6. Voice, Speech, and Mouth Behavior

Vocal baseline is mid-tenor with substantial range; he uses range as a comedic instrument, swinging into falsetto for mockery and into a flat low register for the deadpans. Speech rate is fast and pressured, averaging an estimated 180–220 words per minute in baseline conversation and rising sharply under stress. Sentence boundaries are blurred by run-on, parenthetical, and self-interrupting structures. Verbal output is **constant**; documented silences exceeding ninety seconds in conscious states are rare enough to be individually notable in the file.

Articulation is precise; despite the mouth-tissue compromise, he does not slur, which suggests both that the healing factor has preserved oromotor function and that he has invested significant effort in clarity. Accent floats — primarily a generalized North American with Canadian residue (rhotic, occasional "out" and "about" raisings, the "eh" appearing in informal register), drifting through American regional affectations for comic purpose and occasionally into competent foreign accents that confirm operational language training.

Speech tics:

- Self-interruption ("— oh, wait, no —"; "scratch that"; "back up") averaging multiple times per minute.
- Direct address to non-present audiences mid-sentence; this is the verbal correlate of the fourth-wall break and is, behaviorally, an audible dissociative episode of subsecond duration.
- Quotation and pastiche: song lyrics, film dialogue, advertising slogans, deployed as substitution for original phrasing. This is a documented coping pattern in subjects whose autobiographical memory is unstable — the borrowed phrase substitutes for the missing original thought.
- Inappropriate giggling, especially under conditions that should produce gravitas (funerals, briefings on mass-casualty risk, post-violence aftermath). The laugh is short, high, and breath-only; it is not amusement.

Mouth behavior independent of speech: chronic oral fixation. Documented objects placed in mouth across the record include: knives (held between teeth), bullets, food items at clearly excessive volume, cigarettes (lit and unlit), pens, his own fingers, weapon parts during cleaning, sword pommels. The oral activity escalates under stress.

---

### 7. Eating

Caloric requirement is roughly four to six times normal due to metabolic upregulation, and food intake is correspondingly massive. Eating style is uniformly fast, messy, and accompanied by vocal noise (commentary, moaning approvals, sound effects). He prefers:

- **Foods of high specific identity**: chimichangas as the running fixation, tacos, pancakes (with butter sculpted into shapes), heavily branded junk food. The brand-name attachment is itself notable — the food is selected partially for its capacity to be referred to by name as a bit.
- **Foods that can be eaten without utensils** and consumed in motion or in conversation; cutlery slows him down.
- **Foods with sweet/salt/fat density**, which his metabolism processes essentially as fuel.

He cannot dine formally without sabotaging the formality. Sit-down meals at fixed tables with company produce escalating distractions — fork tricks, condiment art, vocalized criticism of the menu. The exception is meals taken alone with one of the trusted few, where he eats more slowly, less performatively, and sometimes (Blind Al, late-arc Cable, occasionally Eleanor) shares food directly from his plate — a regressive intimacy gesture that occurs nowhere else in the record.

Hunger tolerance is poor. The healing factor punishes caloric deficit with sharpened pain perception, and his irritability tracks linearly with hours since last intake. Surveillance prediction value: a subject in the field for more than five hours without resupply is observably less stable.

---

### 8. Sexual and Intimate Behavior

The sexual record is, by his own performance, loud and constant; the actual documented pattern is narrower and more revealing. He talks about sex with greater frequency and looseness than he engages in it; the bawdy register is part of the humor defense and provides plausible cover for what is, observably, a guarded and selective intimate behavior pattern.

Documented partners are few in number and clustered in two categories: (a) women who match the idealized-and-unattainable schema (Death, Bea Arthur, the trans-species Shiklah whose biology disallows ordinary domestic stakes), and (b) the small number of partners who saw him before or under the disfigurement and were not driven off by it (Vanessa, certain other long-arc figures). Casual sexual encounters appear in the record but read more as performative confirmation of his own desirability under conditions where the partner cannot fully see him (mask retained, low light, partner's senses non-human) than as appetitive expression.

Pre-intimacy behavioral pattern: increased verbal output, escalating self-deprecation, jokes that operate as pre-rejection ("you should see what's under here"; he says it first so the partner cannot). If the partner persists, his behavior shifts notably — verbal output drops, gesture stills (see Hands), and he becomes physically uncharacteristically gentle, with the back-of-the-fingers approach and a careful management of body weight that suggests an internalized model of himself as something whose mass and surface might harm the other party. Post-intimacy, the humor defense reactivates within minutes, often before the partner has fully separated from contact — a textbook reciprocity-aversion response.

Touch tolerance generally: high for combat contact, surgical contact, casual contact from the trusted few; very low for unexpected gentle touch from strangers, which produces flinch (a single sharp lateral movement of the touched body part, often followed by a joke). Hugging behavior is asymmetric — he initiates rarely, accepts when offered with a delayed, slightly-too-tight return that he then breaks first.

---

### 9. Combat Soma

In violence, the body becomes its most coherent. The motor noise of baseline ceases; the gait organizes; the gesture vocabulary tightens. The standard combat posture is low, knees soft, weight forward, swords (when carried) in a draw configuration with thumbs riding the guards. He fights ambidextrously and reliably switches lead hand mid-engagement, which suggests that the dominant-hand bias seen in baseline is a *resting* preference, not a structural one.

He vocalizes continuously through combat — a sustained patter of jokes, target commentary, internal-narrator quotations, and song fragments. The patter serves multiple functions: it regulates his own arousal (matching internal noise to external chaos), it disrupts opponents' pacing, and it provides ongoing situational awareness narration that doubles as planning. Cessation of patter mid-fight is a near-certain indicator that he has been pushed into a state of genuine threat or genuine engagement with someone he respects.

Pain response in combat is delayed and incomplete. He registers injury as information (a sword through the abdomen produces, on observation, a glance down and a comment) but the autonomic recoil — flinch, brace, retreat — is suppressed or absent. The healing factor's rhythms produce a distinctive post-combat behavior: as tissue knits, he twitches involuntarily, scratches at the regenerating surfaces, and frequently strips down to access the injury site for inspection. The inspection is dispassionate, more mechanic-checking-engine than patient-tending-wound.

---

### 10. Grooming, Dress, and Object Habits

Grooming of the body itself is functional. He bathes (regeneration produces continuous low-level shedding requiring management), but the bathing record suggests it is conducted quickly, in poor light, and without the mirror engagement most subjects perform. He does not shave (the tissue does not produce ordinary beard growth in any reliable pattern). What hair remains on the scalp is sparse, patchy, and managed by clipping rather than styling.

Dress, masked: the operational suit is meticulously maintained when observed — straps cinched to consistent tensions, holsters at fixed positions, the mask itself replaced rather than washed when it accumulates damage beyond a threshold. He carries redundant copies of all clothing and equipment in caches across multiple cities (inferred from the speed of his re-equipping after losses).

Dress, unmasked-civilian: striking inconsistency — he oscillates between deliberately bland (hoodie, jeans, neutral colors, calculated to permit movement through public space with face partially concealed) and deliberately loud (Hawaiian shirts, sleepwear in public, costume elements out of context). The bland register dominates when he is alone; the loud register appears when he is with company who tolerates him and the dress functions as a deliberate over-claiming of attention — *if they are going to look, give them something to look at*.

Object habits: he accumulates and discards possessions rapidly. The two consistent exceptions across the run are a small number of personal items (photographs of Eleanor in late arcs; certain weapons with sentimental attachment; objects connected to Blind Al) which are stored, not carried, and which the file should flag as the highest-value leverage objects in any operational assessment. He carries a notable amount of cash and a notable amount of candy at all times.

---

### 11. State-Shift Signatures (Summary Read-Off)

For a watch officer reviewing live feed, the following somatic shifts are the most reliable state indicators:

- **Baseline → calm-with-trusted-few**: motor noise reduces, gesture amplitude reduces, speech rate drops by an estimated 20–30%, eye contact lengthens and stabilizes, hand-to-self soothing emerges.
- **Baseline → operational alert**: footfall switches to ball-first, gait organizes, dominant hand drifts to four o'clock, head tilts increase in mask, verbal output increases in volume but tightens in content (more situational, fewer non-sequiturs).
- **Baseline → acute stress**: gesture amplitude *up*, mask-tilt vocabulary increases, jokes accelerate and degrade in quality, fourth-wall direct-address frequency rises sharply, ambient touching of the mask increases.
- **Baseline → pre-violence**: paradoxical performance increase masking the economy of the actual movement; watch the hands and feet, not the mouth.
- **Baseline → intimacy approach**: verbal output drops, gesture stills, back-of-fingers initiation, body weight visibly managed.
- **Baseline → collapse / grief**: motor noise ceases; conventional seated posture appears; mask stillness; back-of-neck grip; speech short, monosyllabic, sometimes in the cadence of an internal narrator rather than his own voice. *This is the rarest and most diagnostically important configuration in the record* — it is the body of a man who has finally been forced to sit with something, and it predicts either subsequent prolonged disappearance or, in the small number of cases where someone he trusts is present and patient, the beginning of one of his rare integrative episodes.
- **Forced unmasking / mirror exposure**: hand to face (either covering or aggressively displaying), eye-contact dyad collapses to extreme (either too long or absent), speech becomes hostile or, alternately, abruptly quiet — both readings are alarm states.

The Atlas's central operational note: the subject's body is a continuous, high-fidelity broadcast of his internal state for any observer who knows the codebook. He is aware of this and has constructed the mask, the patter, and the motor noise as a jamming signal layered over the broadcast. The jamming signal is itself, however, *informative* — its presence, its intensity, and most of all the rare moments of its cessation map the interior as reliably as the underlying signal would. He cannot stop transmitting. He has only learned to transmit in two languages at once.


## Attachment & Relational Patterns

# ATTACHMENT & RELATIONAL PATTERNS

## I. Attachment Architecture: Origin and Classification

The subject presents as **disorganized attachment with predominant fearful-avoidant features**, structurally complicated by an unusual second-order configuration in which the disorganization itself has been pathologically *stabilized* by chronic biological survival. Ordinary disorganized attachment in adults tends toward episodic collapse — relationships dissolve, the subject decompensates, reconstitutes, attempts again. Wilson cannot decompensate to the point of collapse (his soma forbids it) and consequently has accumulated, over a documented operational lifetime exceeding three decades, a **relational repertoire that loops without resolving** — the same approach-test-sabotage-mourn-return sequence executed at slightly varying tempo across every figure he has ever attached to.

The developmental substrate is unrecoverable in detail but recoverable in *register*. Every variant origin Wilson has supplied — the abusive father, the abusive mother, the dead mother and surviving father, the both-alive, the both-dead, the never-existed — shares an affective signature: **the caregiver is unsafe, unreliable, or absent, and the child is alone with this knowledge**. The content varies; the structure of insecurity does not. The forensically useful inference is not which story is true but that no story he tells about being parented is one in which he was held safely. This is the negative space from which the attachment style was built: an internal working model in which proximity to a caregiving figure carries the prior expectation of harm, and in which the child's task is to manage the caregiver rather than be managed by them.

The military period (special forces, washout for insubordination and probable psychiatric flags) demonstrates the same pattern transposed into an institutional frame. He selected an environment that supplied structure (relief from internal chaos) without intimacy (relief from exposure), then sabotaged it at the precise point the institution began to claim him. The discharge is the prototype of every subsequent rupture: he leaves before he can be properly held, and he engineers the leaving in a way that ensures the institution rejects him, so the leaving feels like *being thrown out* rather than *walking away* — an externalization of agency that preserves the schema of being unwanted while protecting him from the more dangerous knowledge that he was the one who could not stay.

The Hospice arc with Killebrew and Ajax then writes the template in its final, totalizing form. He arrives sick, having been promised cure. He is delivered torture by clinicians whose institutional uniform reads *caregiver*. The single attachment he forms inside the facility — Worm — he is manipulated into killing. He is then "killed" himself and survives. The schema produced by this sequence is not merely *people will hurt you*, which would generate avoidance; it is the far more pathogenic *the offer of care is the leading edge of the torture, and any attachment you form will be turned into a weapon against you, and you will be the one wielding it.* This is the load-bearing belief of every subsequent relationship in the file.

## II. The Eight-Phase Relational Cycle

Across every documented relationship of significance, Wilson executes a stable eight-phase sequence. The phases are observable in compressed form (a single encounter) and extended form (a multi-year arc such as Vanessa, Shiklah, or Eleanor). They appear in the same order each time.

**Phase 1 — Approach via Transgression.** Initial contact is made through a provocation calibrated to the target's most sensitive register: sexual innuendo with a woman who reads as professional, a violation of decorum with an authority figure, a tactless joke about the target's loss. This is not seduction failure or social ineptitude; it is **diagnostic**. The transgression is an instrument for measuring the target's tolerance band before any disclosure has been made. A target who flees confirms the schema cheaply and is dismissed. A target who reciprocates with hostility is escalated against and dismissed. A target who absorbs the transgression and remains present is flagged and advanced to Phase 2.

**Phase 2 — Performance Bonding.** The mask thickens. Wilson supplies entertainment, competence, loyalty in small contractual matters, and a stylized version of his interiority composed of pop-cultural reference, contradictory autobiography, and pre-empted self-deprecation.
