The performance is meticulously good — Weasel, Bob, the Mercs for Money, and even Cable have all been recruited or held through this phase's deliverables. The crucial feature is that **everything offered is repeatable and replaceable**; nothing yet offered is irreplaceable, so nothing yet offered exposes him to loss.

**Phase 3 — Selective Disclosure as Test.** A controlled leak of a piece of true interiority — the cancer, the face beneath the mask, a fragment of a real origin, an admission of fear. Disclosures are micro-dosed and immediately followed by a humor-flush that gives the target the option to treat the disclosure as a bit and let it pass. The test is precise: *did you notice that was real, and are you going to do anything dangerous with the noticing?* Most targets accept the flush. The rare target who notices and stays still without comment — Blind Al's particular gift; Bob's accidental gift; Cable's deliberate gift — passes the test, and is advanced to Phase 4. Targets who exploit the disclosure are mapped as predators (Osborn). Targets who refuse to acknowledge it at all are downgraded to operational acquaintances.

**Phase 4 — Captive Configuration.** With targets who have passed Phase 3, Wilson constructs a relational geometry in which **he controls the exit**. The forms vary by target and era. Blind Al was literalized captivity — she was held, in his apartment, against her will, across years. Weasel was held by economic dependency, professional symbiosis, and the threat-laced affection of someone who would not let him quit. The Mercs for Money were held by managerial structure that put Wilson at the org-chart node where he could not be left without the entity dissolving. With Vanessa, the captive configuration was attempted via the intensity of the relationship itself — a romantic enclosure so total that exit would have required tearing — and it failed precisely because Vanessa was structurally his equal. With Eleanor, the captivity was the asymmetry of parent and child. With Shiklah, the captivity was supernatural marriage to a being who literally could not be killed by him. The pattern is consistent: **bonds Wilson values are bonds he has arranged so they cannot be cleanly severed by the other party**. This is the operational solution to abandonment terror: build the relationship in a substrate where ordinary leaving is impossible.

**Phase 5 — Idealization with Sabotage Latency.** Once captivity is established, Wilson elevates the figure into a quasi-sacred position. Vanessa becomes the lost beloved he organizes nostalgia around. Eleanor becomes the redemptive future. Cable becomes the older brother / superego he half-resents and wholly relies on. The idealization is genuine but contains the seed of its own undoing — the figure is being held to an impossible standard (perfect tolerance, perfect mirroring, perfect non-departure) that the figure will inevitably fail to meet, supplying the pretext for Phase 6.

**Phase 6 — Sabotage.** This is the diagnostic phase. Sabotage takes distinct forms by relationship type:

- *Romantic*: withdrawal-via-diagnosis (Vanessa, on receiving terminal cancer news, is abandoned for her protection — the cover-story he tells himself; the function is to preempt her abandonment of him); contradictory autobiography to lovers (so the lover cannot accumulate stable knowledge); reflexive infidelity-equivalent (the Shiklah/surface-world conflict, in which his choices ensure he cannot fully inhabit either marriage).
- *Mentor/peer*: provocation past the partner's tolerance (Cable has been repeatedly pushed to the breaking point and is the rare figure who refuses to break); operational unreliability that endangers shared missions; sudden disappearance.
- *Parental (Eleanor)*: episodic disappearance; placement of the child at distance via custody arrangements he claims to oppose but does not effectively contest; the catastrophic reveal of his violence-life in moments timed (probably non-consciously) to ensure the child or her guardians cannot un-know it.
- *Subordinate (Mercs, Bob)*: contractual mistreatment, broken pay, manic management decisions, public humiliation of those most loyal.
- *Captive (Blind Al)*: cruelty rituals (the boobytrapped apartment, the practical jokes) that simultaneously enact aggression and reaffirm the bond — the cruelty proves the bond is still load-bearing.

**Phase 7 — Catastrophic Loss or Stable Tolerance.** Most targets, having been sabotaged, leave or are killed by the cumulative gravity of association with him. This outcome confirms the schema and produces ritualized mourning, which Wilson conducts in a register of escalating absurdity (drinking binges that fail to intoxicate, contract sprees, monologues delivered to the audience). A very small subset of figures — Blind Al, Weasel, Cable, Bob, Outlaw — *do not leave* despite sabotage, and these figures become **permanent attachment objects**, held in a position of structural primacy regardless of the relational temperature in any given month. The functional criterion for permanent status is not affection or compatibility but **demonstrated non-leaveability under Phase 6 conditions**.

**Phase 8 — Return.** Wilson re-approaches the surviving figures after intervals proportional to the severity of the preceding sabotage. The return is rarely accompanied by acknowledgment; the bit is reanimated as though no rupture occurred. Permanent attachment figures absorb this without comment, which is precisely the property that defines them as permanent. The cycle then resumes at Phase 2 or 5, having confirmed once more that this particular bond holds.

## III. The Specific Relationships in Longitudinal View

**Vanessa Carlysle (Copycat).** The pre-diagnosis relationship is documented as the closest he has come to an unmediated intimacy with a peer. Her shape-shifting capacity is structurally significant — she is, by nature, a figure who cannot be fixed into a single image, which mirrors his own identity diffusion and resolves the usual problem that a stable beloved poses (the impossibility of being known and remaining safe). With her, he could be reciprocally illegible. The withdrawal upon diagnosis is overdetermined — protection, shame, terror of being witnessed in deterioration — but its structural function is to **convert the relationship from one of ongoing reciprocity into one of preserved memory**, which is a form he can manage. Memorialized Vanessa is safe; living Vanessa was not. He returns to her, in canon, in cycles, but each return is brief and each parting is engineered.

**Theresa Cassidy (Siryn).** The Kelly run's central romantic vehicle. Siryn offers him precisely the thing he cannot accept: a sustained, sober, non-ironic willingness to see him as a person worth loving. The relationship structurally cannot survive because she refuses to enter Phase 4 — she will not be made captive, she will not stop reflecting him with sincerity, she will not collude in the bit. Wilson's sabotage register with her is unusually direct: he behaves badly enough to make her leave, because her unwillingness to be captured means he must rupture the bond himself to restore the schema. The relationship is one of his most informative because it shows him **choosing rupture over tolerated love** when no other exit is available.

**Blind Al.** The literal captive. The relationship is a deliberate inversion of the parent/child template that failed him: he holds her, he controls the apartment, the cruelty rituals (the "Box," the boobytraps) are aggression deployed at a target who cannot leave to prove the bond's elasticity. Her blindness is structurally crucial — she cannot see his face — which permits an intimacy that visual reciprocity would forbid. She is the only figure to whom he is, in any sustained sense, ordinary, because she alone receives him without the disfigurement-mediated rejection-loop running. Across decades she is the single most stable attachment in the file. The configuration is morally indefensible by ordinary standards and, in the precise pathology of this subject, the only configuration that has produced durable holding.

**Weasel.** The pattern here is *coerced friendship* — Weasel is held by a mixture of financial dependency, professional necessity (his armorer/intel role), and the unsubtle understanding that disengagement would not be permitted. Wilson treats Weasel poorly and protects him absolutely. The relationship is the operational template for all his masculine peer attachments: hold them in place by force or asymmetry, mistreat them within a band that the relationship can absorb, defend them at any cost against external threat. Weasel is the bond Wilson would die for and would not be kind to.

**Cable (Nathan Summers).** The most psychologically generative attachment in the file. Cable is structurally suited to weather Phase 6: his temporal displacement, his messianic seriousness, his immunity to provocation, and his refusal to enter the bit make him incapable of being destabilized by Wilson's testing. Wilson responds with a mixture of erotic-tinged antagonism, fraternal loyalty, and superego-projection that has remained legible across every joint arc. Cable functions as the only relationship in which Wilson permits being **morally instructed** without immediate sabotage, because Cable refuses to occupy the *we believe in you, come be one of us* register that authority figures (Osborn, Hydra-Rogers) use to weaponize his hunger. Cable's instruction is delivered as disappointment rather than invitation, which paradoxically is the only modality Wilson can tolerate sustained moral input through.

**Bob, Agent of Hydra.** The accidental Phase-3 passer. Bob's anxious incompetence is structurally non-threatening; he cannot exploit a disclosure because he cannot organize one. Wilson treats him with the casual cruelty he reserves for permanent attachments, drags him through environments lethal to a normal human, and defends him with disproportionate force. Bob's value to Wilson is that he asks nothing and notices everything without consequence.

**Shiklah.** The marriage to a Succubus queen is the most concentrated expression of the object-choice principle: he selects a partner who is literally a devourer, supernaturally durable, who occupies a separate metaphysical jurisdiction (the Monster Metropolis) such that the relationship cannot follow him into ordinary life and ordinary life cannot follow him into it. The captive configuration is built into the cosmology. The marriage's collapse — Wilson's divided loyalty between the surface world and her court — is the predictable outcome of attempting to occupy two non-overlapping worlds, and is, in the longer pattern, another Phase 6 sabotage that the relational geometry was constructed to make inevitable.

**Eleanor.** The daughter is the most morally consequential relationship in the file and the one Wilson has been least able to sustain. Parenthood requires the steady, low-affect, day-by-day presence that his entire affective architecture is incompatible with. He loves her without question and cannot be near her without endangering her, which he registers and uses as license for the very absence that confirms the failure. The relationship has been routed through surrogate guardians, through extended absence framed as protection, through episodic catastrophic appearance. The child-protection override — the single most reliable feature of his behavioral profile — is in part a generalization of Eleanor across all children, an attempt to be, for every other child, the parent he has been unable to be for his own.

**Carmelita.** The mother of Eleanor, killed in the Butler arc, occupies the structurally significant slot of *the lover he did not have time to sabotage*, leaving the relationship preserved in a state of unrealized possibility. Like Vanessa, she becomes more functional to him dead than she could have been alive.

**Death (personified).** The libidinal investment in Death is the cleanest expression of the underlying romantic schema: a beloved who is, by nature, *the thing that will hold him without leaving*, who is structurally unattainable in life and therefore safe to idealize, and whose embrace would terminate the loop entirely. Thanos's interposition (the curse of immortality) externalizes the biological fact that the soma will not permit consummation. Death is the only beloved against whom no sabotage is possible — because no reciprocity is possible — and she is therefore his most stable romantic object.

**Ajax (Francis Fanny).** The negative attachment. Ajax occupies a position of obsessional centrality that survives Ajax's death and resurrections, returning across arcs whenever the trauma architecture is activated. The fixation has the structure of a trauma bond inverted into a hunt — Wilson cannot leave Ajax alone because Ajax wrote his nervous system, and any encounter with an Ajax-coded figure (sadistic clinician, mocking torturer, authority who couples cruelty with care-language) reactivates the full template. Identification with the aggressor has bled Ajax's affective register (mockery during violence) into Wilson's own combat style — the perpetrator is metabolized into the self.

**The Avengers / Captain America (legitimate-authority class).** Wilson's repeated, abjectly hungry approach to the Avengers, and his comprehensive exploitation by Osborn and by Hydra-Rogers, define the operational meaning of his largest exploitable surface: **the offer of admission to the moral community**. He is rendered legible by this offer in a way no other lure can match, because the offer addresses the unmet developmental need (be claimed by a caregiving structure that says *you are one of ours*) at its origin. Every figure who has framed an ask in this register has gotten everything they wanted from him, including the murder of Coulson. The dossier should treat this surface as the highest-priority counterintelligence vulnerability in the subject's profile.

## IV. The Texture of Intimacy and the Texture of Distrust

**How he bonds.** Bonding, when it occurs, is recognizable by a small set of behavioral markers: the disclosure-flush of Phase 3 begins to relax — disclosures are made and not immediately undone with a bit. The verbal output drops, briefly, in the figure's presence; the silences he cannot tolerate elsewhere become survivable with them. He cooks for them — the canon contains a surprising volume of domestic-food scenes, generally pancakes or chimichangas, prepared for figures he is bonded to; food preparation is one of the few non-verbal caregiving behaviors he can perform without it triggering the mockery defense. He shows them his face, eventually, without comment. He gives them weapons, which in his economy of meaning is the equivalent of giving a normal person a key.

**How he distrusts.** Distrust is the default and does not need to be earned. It is provisionally suspended for figures who have passed Phase 3 and structurally suspended (never actually relinquished) for figures who have passed Phase 7. Markers of active distrust: increase in pop-cultural deflection, multiplication of contradictory autobiographical statements, a particular kind of laughter that arrives a beat before any joke (the laugh as a pre-emptive frame around whatever is about to be said), physical positioning that maintains a line of egress, and — most reliably — the substitution of operational language for affective language when the conversation begins to require affect.

**How he betrays.** Betrayal, when Wilson commits it, is almost always a Phase 6 act dressed in operational rationalization. He betrays by disappearance more often than by active treachery. Active betrayals (Coulson, the assassinations under SHIELD direction) are the consequence of his admission-to-the-moral-community vulnerability rather than of any independent betraying disposition. He does not betray for advantage; he betrays because someone with institutional authority asked him to, framed as belonging. The exception is the small treacheries against captives and dependents (Blind Al's cruelty rituals, the Mercs' mismanagement) which are sabotage-class events rather than betrayals proper — they are designed to test the bond's durability, not to dissolve it.

**How he is betrayed.** Almost every authority figure in his life has betrayed him: the military discharged him, Killebrew tortured him, Ajax sold him to the dead-pool, Osborn played him, Rogers (in the Hydra register) weaponized him, SHIELD lied to him about who his targets were. Mercenary clients routinely double-cross him. He does not register these betrayals with surprise. The schema is so thoroughly confirmed that betrayal is the expected interaction with institutional figures, and his anger about it is brief, performative, and frequently turned against himself. The betrayals that wound him are the small ones from the permanent attachments — a slight from Cable, an exhausted dismissal from Weasel — which his nervous system processes with intensity disproportionate to the act because, within his economy, they should be impossible.

**How he repairs.** Repair, in any formal sense (acknowledgment, accountability, behavioral change), is not in his repertoire. What he has instead is **return without comment**. After a rupture, he reappears, executes the bit at slightly higher volume, demonstrates a small unsolicited service, and waits. The figure is invited to either accept the return (no apology offered, none required by the implicit contract) or refuse it. Acceptance restarts the cycle. Refusal is mourned. Cable, Blind Al, Weasel, Bob, and Outlaw have all accepted such returns repeatedly. Vanessa, before her death, accepted some and refused others. Eleanor, as a child, has no real option to refuse, which is part of why parenting destabilizes him: the absence of the *or refuse it* clause makes the return mean something he cannot quite metabolize.

## V. The Dependency Profile

Wilson is profoundly dependent on a small set of figures (the permanent attachments) and presents in every other context as defiantly autonomous. The dependency is hidden by its distribution: no single figure carries the weight, which would expose the need, but the redundant network of Blind Al, Weasel, Cable, Bob, and the periodically reactivated others supplies a baseline of relational holding that he requires to function. **When the network thins — when an attachment is lost or alienated — his pathology intensifies measurably**: more reckless contract selection, more substance pursuit, longer disappearances, higher fourth-wall-break density, increased frequency of the suicidal-ideation script. When the network is intact and tolerant, he can perform something approximating ordinary social functioning for stretches of weeks.

He does not name the dependency. He would deny it under direct questioning. It is detectable only by **the deterioration that follows withdrawal**, which is the empirical signature of unacknowledged dependence — the subject does not say *I need them* and does not need to, because his decompensation in their absence makes the statement on his behalf.

## VI. The Repeated Template, Stated Plainly

Across every relationship in the file, the same template runs: **provoke to measure, perform to attract, micro-disclose to test, capture to secure, idealize to sanctify, sabotage to falsify the idealization before it can be disproven by reality, lose or hold, mourn or return.** The template does not change with the type of relationship — romantic, parental, mentor, peer, subordinate, supernatural, captive — only its tempo and the local idiom of each phase. The template does not change with insight; Wilson can describe it with clinical precision and re-execute it the same hour. The template will not change without the collapse-and-reconstitution that his biology forbids.

What does change, very slowly, is the **size of the surviving network**. Across three decades of canon, the number of figures who have passed Phase 7 and remained in stable


## Defenses & Compensatory Mechanisms

# UATU DOSSIER — WADE WINSTON WILSON
## Section: Defenses & Compensatory Mechanisms

---

### Prefatory Note on Architecture

Most subjects present a defensive system with a primary mechanism and a fallback. Wilson presents a **stacked, redundant, multi-tier defensive lattice** of unusual depth, organized around a single structural necessity: he cannot achieve any of the natural endpoints by which severe pathology resolves itself. He cannot decompensate into catatonia (the regenerating neural tissue reboots); he cannot drink himself into oblivion (metabolism); he cannot suicide (the body refuses); he cannot dissociate into a fugue long enough to escape his identity (the substrate keeps rebuilding the substrate). His defenses therefore do not function, as in ordinary patients, to prevent collapse — collapse is biologically prohibited. They function to make the **uninterrupted continuity of an unbearable state** liveable in the next ten seconds, and the ten seconds after that. The defensive architecture is, in this sense, a **moment-to-moment metabolic process** rather than a structural buffer. It does not store; it burns.

What follows is a stratified inventory, ordered from most primitive (Vaillant Level I / psychotic) to most mature (Level IV), with operational behavior keyed to each. Within each stratum, the **positive (life-preserving, prosocially-compatible) and negative (self-damaging, relationally corrosive) faces** of the same mechanism are noted, since with this subject nearly every defense is double-faced.

---

### Tier I — Psychotic / Reality-Distorting Defenses

These appear under maximum acute stress (existential exposure, the unmediated sight of his own face, betrayal by a chosen authority, the death of an attachment).

**1. Delusional projection (intermittent, fragmentary).** Not florid. Wilson does not construct paranoid systems. What he does construct, under acute stress, is **brief attribution of his own intent to the environment** — the boxes start narrating the room's hostility before the room is hostile; he registers a neutral interlocutor as a target and acts before checking. The mechanism is observable in the seconds before unprovoked engagement and burns off within the same scene.

**2. Psychotic denial of biological fact.** He maintains, often as the load-bearing premise of an entire monologue, that the events around him are not occurring — they are panels, frames, scripts. *In-universe this is correct*, and this is the load-bearing oddity of his entire defensive architecture: the most primitive defense available to him is also factually accurate, which makes it non-falsifiable and therefore impossible to dismantle through reality testing. A clinician arguing that he is not in a comic would be wrong. This collapses the standard treatment ladder before it begins.

**3. Distortion via comic-script ideology.** Under maximum stress he will reorganize current events into the genre logic of his choosing (this is the third act; this is the cold open; this is a flashback) and act in accordance with the genre rather than the situation. The behavior is indistinguishable from a structured delusion, but its content is meta-textual rather than persecutory.

---

### Tier II — Immature Defenses (Primary Operating Stratum)

This is where Wilson lives. Eighty percent of observable behavior across the canonical record routes through this stratum.

**4. Splitting.** Operates at three levels:

- *Self-splitting*: the monster-self and the truth-seeing-untouchable-self alternate without integration. There is no continuous narrator. Within the same conversation he will refer to himself in third person as "Deadpool" (the function), in first person as "Wade" (the wound), and in second person as a thing being addressed by someone else (the dissociation). The pronoun drift is a real-time tell of which self is in the chair.
- *Object-splitting*: people are good (Cable, Bob, Al, Eleanor, the small permanent list) or fungible (everyone else, including most clients, including most victims). Movement between categories is rare and traumatic; when it happens (Rogers, Coulson), it produces protracted destabilization.
- *World-splitting*: the universe is either a cruel joke whose punchline is structural (his usual stance) or, briefly, redeemable (the Mithras arc, the post-Original Sin redemption push). He cannot hold both. When forced to, he ruptures the frame with a joke.

**5. Projective identification.** Heavily used in combat and in early-relationship testing. He **induces in the other person the affect he cannot tolerate in himself**: he provokes disgust (so he need not feel self-disgust), provokes rage (so the rage is in the room rather than in him), provokes dismissal (so the rejection is enacted rather than feared). The Mercs for Money management arc shows this at scale — he generated the contempt in his subordinates that he expected from them, then experienced their reaction as confirmation of his model.

**6. Acting out.** Affect that approaches consolidation is reliably converted to motor activity within seconds. The conversion menu is stable: violence, sex, food, contract acquisition, geographic displacement, property damage, mass collateral. The operational rule is *any motor program will do, provided it interrupts the settling of the feeling*. Observable temporal pattern: a window of approximately three to seven seconds between the threatening affect entering awareness and the motor discharge. Trained handlers (Cable, late-run Weasel) have learned to identify this window and intervene with redirection rather than confrontation.

**7. Somatization (inverted form).** Most patients somatize emotional pain into bodily complaint. Wilson does the inverse — he **routes overwhelming somatic input into emotional and verbal channels**, narrating his own dismemberments as comic incident. His body is in continuous pain; his speech is the spillover. The constant verbal output is, in part, a continuous somatosensory translation. Silence him and the pain returns to the body uncushioned.

**8. Passive aggression.** Mostly observable with authority figures and within the Mercs for Money management structure. The pattern: stated compliance, theatrical agreement, then sabotage delivered as incompetence-that-could-be-deniable. Used least with his small list of trusted figures, most with handlers and reluctant collaborators.

**9. Dissociation (immature, defensive variant).** Distinct from the structural dissociation described below. The defensive form is **on-demand depersonalization** — he can, and routinely does, vacate the experience of his own actions in real time, narrating from outside. This is the behavioral substrate of the fourth-wall break: not a literary device, a clinical disappearance dressed as one. The signature is a flattening of vocal affect, a shift to present-progressive narration ("and now he's doing this"), and a brief failure of eye contact replaced by an apparent middle-distance addressee.

**10. Fantasy (autistic withdrawal variant).** The Bea Arthur fixation, the marriage to a Succubus queen, the courtship of Death-as-entity, the running romantic conception of an impossible domesticity — these are not whimsy. They are sustained, structured fantasy investments in **objects selected for impossibility**, which permit the experience of longing without the risk of reciprocity. The fantasy life is rich, recurrent, and discussed openly precisely because public ridicule of the fantasies reinforces their distance from achievable reality.

**11. Devaluation / idealization cycles.** Standard borderline-level oscillation. New attachment figures are over-idealized for a measurable initial window (longer the more powerful the figure — Rogers got the longest idealization arc on record before catastrophic collapse), then devalued, often violently, when reciprocity is offered or imperfection exposed. The few who survive this cycle do so by neither accepting the idealization nor recoiling from the devaluation — Cable's tactical disinterest in being admired and Al's structural inability to flatter him are protective.

**12. Identification with the aggressor.** Wilson's combat affective register — mockery during violence, intimate verbal cruelty paired with bodily damage, theatricalized sadism delivered in the cadence of care — **is Ajax's**, learned in the Hospice and never relinquished. He is, in his working hours, the man who tortured him. This is the defense's most successful operation and its most damaging: it preserves the self by being the perpetrator rather than the victim, at the cost of remaking the self in the perpetrator's image. The recognition of this in himself, when it surfaces, is among the few stimuli that can produce genuine, unironized horror in him.

**13. Turning against the self.** Continuous, low-grade, and biologically obstructed in its consummation. The chronic recklessness is not, in the strict clinical sense, suicidal — he knows he will not die — but the impulse is suicidal in origin and the behavioral output (stepping into fire, refusing cover, accepting overwhelming odds) is identical to that of an actively suicidal patient. He has learned to perform the gesture of self-destruction continuously, as a kind of standing prayer that one day it will take.

---

### Tier III — Neurotic / Intermediate Defenses

Present, but secondary to Tier II.

**14. Reaction formation.** Operationally enormous. The murderous-mercenary presentation overlays a persistent prosocial drive that surfaces in: refusal of child-harm contracts (absolute, across all runs, all writers, no documented exceptions); client double-cross in favor of innocents at personal cost; the Mithras arc willingness to be the messiah he then could not bear to be; the Avengers obsession; the rescue reflex in the Posehn/Duggan and Kelly runs that triggers faster than his self-preservation reflex. The clown-killer presentation is sustained because it is *more tolerable to him* than the would-be-hero presentation, which exposes him to judgment against an unmeetable standard. The mask of monster is the reaction-formation against the wish to be good.

**15. Intellectualization (genre-theoretic variant).** Wilson is fluent in his own diagnosis. He can name his attachment style, his trauma history, his defensive operations, his pharmacological status, and the precise mechanism of his current dissociation, often in real time, often correctly. The intellectualization is **insight without mentalization**: the description is accurate and changes nothing, because the language describing the state is being generated by a self-state different from the one performing the behavior. This is the defense that most reliably fools observers into believing therapeutic progress is possible.

**16. Rationalization.** Used economically. He is too cynical to require elaborate justifications for his own conduct — he largely admits to whatever he has done. Rationalization concentrates in two domains: (a) the contracts he selects (always rationalized into a moral frame even when financially driven, never the reverse), and (b) the relational ruptures he engineers (the other party is reframed retroactively as having needed to be free of him).

**17. Displacement.** Affect generated by trusted figures (Cable, Al, Eleanor, Vanessa) is reliably displaced onto disposable targets — clients, marks, scenery, the boxes. He has never been observed expressing the actual valence of feeling directly to the actual object on first occurrence. The displaced version arrives first; the genuine version, if it arrives at all, arrives delayed, deflected, and routed through humor.

**18. Undoing.** Following moments of accidental sincerity, Wilson will execute an immediate undoing — typically a transgressive joke, a deliberate cruelty, or a violent escalation calibrated to retroactively void the sincerity. The temporal signature is reliable: sincerity, beat, undoing within one to three seconds. Trained observers can identify the sincerity in retrospect by locating the undoing.

**19. Isolation of affect.** Operates at the boundary between Tier II dissociation and Tier III intellectualization. The grief over Eleanor's custody loss, the betrayal by Rogers, the death of attachments — each is discussed with affective flatness while the corresponding behavioral disorganization escalates elsewhere. The feeling is not absent; it is decoupled from its representation.

---

### Tier IV — Mature Defenses (Selective, Hard-Won)

These are real, they are operational, and their presence in a personality this disorganized is the single most important prognostic finding.

**20. Sublimation (partial, conditional).** The mercenary trade is, at its higher functioning, sublimated aggression — channeled into structured competence, paid for, completed, walked away from. The capacity to convert the murderous impulse into a contract with terms is genuine sublimation, even if the substrate is grim. Similarly, the comic invention — the inventiveness of his humor, distinct from its defensive function — qualifies as sublimation of the verbal hyperactivity that would otherwise present as pressured speech.

**21. Suppression (rare, observed under combat priority).** Wilson is capable, when an attachment figure is in danger, of suppressing the entire defensive lattice for the duration of the engagement and operating with focused, undecorated competence. This is one of two states in which the joking stops. Its existence is critical evidence that the defenses are operations rather than the personality itself — there is a self underneath them that can take the field when the stakes are correctly configured.

**22. Anticipation (severely limited).** Long-horizon planning is poor, but he is capable of short-horizon anticipation in protective contexts (planning evacuations of dependents, structuring exit routes from theaters of operation, contingency-arranging Eleanor's safety). The anticipatory capacity tracks the attachment salience of the protected object — it is not generally available, only relationally activated.

**23. Altruism (genuine, suppressed-in-presentation).** Across the record, the volume of uncompensated protective behavior is substantial and consistent. He pays for it in cash, in injury, in reputation, in the loss of contracts. The altruism is **systematically disguised**, often performed in such a way that the protected party never learns who protected them or, if they learn, is repelled by the performance and cannot acknowledge it. This is altruism that has been routed through reaction-formation and undoing — it survives, it operates, it costs him, and he refuses to be credited.

**24. Humor (mature variant, present in trace amounts).** Distinct from the manic-defensive humor that dominates his presentation. Trace deployments of genuine, integrative humor — humor that holds the affect rather than dispelling it — appear most often with Cable, occasionally with Al, rarely with Weasel. These moments are identifiable by the absence of an undoing afterward; the feeling and the joke coexist and neither is voided. Their existence indicates the mature defense is available; their rarity indicates the conditions for its activation are narrow.

---

### Structural Defenses (Sui Generis to This Subject)

A residual category for mechanisms that do not fit standard taxonomy because they are unique to the soma-psyche configuration.

**25. Structurally dissociated self-states ("the boxes").** Discussed at length in the Psychiatric section. As a defense, the boxes function as a **distributed mind** — affect, impulse, and superego are externalized into voices that can argue, contradict, mock, and witness. The pressure that would otherwise overwhelm a single executive is distributed across two or three. The cost is the loss of unified agency; the benefit is that no single component need bear the full load.

**26. Captive-attachment construction.** A defense by relational architecture. By selecting or constructing relationships in which the other party cannot easily exit (Blind Al originally a captive; Weasel coerced into friendship via mutual mercenary entanglement; Mercs for Money managed through financial and operational dependency), Wilson eliminates the variable he cannot tolerate: unilateral abandonment. This is not malice. It is a structural prophylaxis against the loss that has destroyed him every previous time, implemented at the level of relational design rather than internal regulation.

**27. Autobiographical opacity (defense by data corruption).** The deliberate production of mutually contradictory origin stories — to handlers, lovers, captive audiences, himself — is a defense unique to him. By ensuring no fixed narrative of his life exists, he ensures no one (himself included) can form a stable assessment against which growth, failure, betrayal, or judgment could be measured. The data is corrupted at the source. This makes him unmappable, including to himself, and the unmappability is protective. The cost is that he cannot accumulate self-knowledge across episodes; the benefit is that no one can hold an account of him that he has not authored in the moment.

**28. Continuous verbal output as somatosensory cushion.** Discussed under somatization. As a defense, the verbal stream functions to **maintain a baseline arousal state above the threshold at which interoceptive pain becomes dominant**. He talks to keep the pain at the second rank of attention. When forcibly silenced (gagged, alone in confinement, the brief stillness arcs in Posehn/Duggan), the pain rises to the first rank and his presentation shifts visibly toward despair within minutes.

**29. The healing factor as terminal defense.** Worth naming explicitly: the body itself functions as the last-resort defense against every threat to existence except existence itself. The biology refuses every endpoint, which is why the psychology has had to develop a defensive architecture this elaborate — there is no falling back on dying. Every other patient has, as final defense, the possibility of not surviving. He does not.

---

### Operational Summary

The defensive system can be characterized by four properties:

- **Redundant**: every function (affect modulation, identity coherence, threat assessment, relational regulation) is served by multiple mechanisms across multiple tiers, so the failure of any single defense does not produce collapse.
- **Metabolic rather than structural**: defenses are burned in real time rather than relied on as stable buffers; the rate of consumption is high and continuous.
- **Inverted toward the mature end**: the mature defenses, where present, are paradoxically the ones he most aggressively conceals, because being seen practicing them threatens the monster-schema that organizes his livable identity.
- **Biologically anchored**: the entire architecture is shaped around the inability to access the natural defensive endpoint (cessation), which forces every other defense to bear more load than its taxonomic peers in any other patient.

The **clinically actionable observation** is this: with most patients, you work to dismantle primitive defenses so mature ones can take their place. With Wilson, the primitive defenses cannot safely be dismantled — they are the metabolic process keeping the moment liveable — and the mature defenses are already present and operational, hidden under the primitive ones, and need not be installed but **uncovered, named carefully (without triggering an undoing), and granted permission to operate openly**. The therapeutic task, if it could be performed, would be permissive rather than reconstructive. Whether anyone has the durability to perform it — to remain in the room across the testing cycle without flattering, recoiling, or rupturing — is the open empirical question of his life.


## Longitudinal Psychological Profile

# LONGITUDINAL PSYCHOLOGICAL PROFILE
## Subject: Wilson, Wade Winston — Decade-by-Decade Clinical Trajectory

---

A note on the temporal frame before we begin. The subject's publication history spans 1991 to the present, but his in-universe biography is non-linear, partially fabricated by the subject himself, and subject to neurological corruption (see Medical §2). The decadal divisions below are therefore organized by *publication-era cohort* of canonical material, which corresponds approximately to phases of the subject's adult life as they have been progressively rendered. Where the subject's own accounts conflict, the behavior under observation — not the autobiography supplied — is treated as the primary datum. This is the standard approach to a witness who lies reflexively but cannot help showing.

---

## Phase 0 (pre-1991 in-universe): Pre-Morbid Baseline and Developmental Substrate

**Reconstructable picture.** What can be triangulated from the consistent affective residue beneath contradictory origin stories (Kelly, *Deadpool* vol. 2 #-1 and #33; Nicieza flashbacks; Posehn/Duggan retrospective beats): a child whose early environment produced reliable expectation of caregiver-perpetrated harm and unreliable expectation of caregiver protection. The specific perpetrator rotates across his accounts (father, mother, both, neither) but the *affect tone* of every version is identical — apprehension, hypervigilance to mood-weather in adults, premature humor-deployment as appeasement. The constancy of the affect across rotating content is the diagnostic finding; he is telling the truth about how it felt and lying about who did it, almost certainly because the actual figures remain too dangerous internally to name.

**Cognitive style at baseline.** Even pre-trauma, evidence suggests a high-verbal, scanning, joke-precocious cognitive style — the kind of child who reads adult faces for the next blow and learns to talk fast as deflection. This is the cognitive substrate on which everything later is built. The verbal fluency that becomes pathological in adulthood was originally adaptive: a kid in a bad house who could make the room laugh stayed alive.

**Self-concept at baseline.** Already split. The Hospice did not invent the monster-schema; it confirmed one already operative. The military washout (Nicieza, special forces discharge for insubordination and "possible psychiatric grounds") suggests that by late adolescence the affect dysregulation was already incompatible with rule-bound institutional life. He selected mercenary work — Tangier, the Balkans — precisely because it monetized his existing structure: solitary, transactional, episodic, no requirement to integrate.

**Affect regulation at baseline.** Probably already managed by stimulation-seeking and humor. The Vanessa relationship (pre-diagnosis) is the only window onto Wilson in something resembling a stable attachment, and even there the canonical description is "intensity, jokes-as-armor" — i.e., the defenses are running at full power inside what is nominally a safe relationship. He had no resting state even before he had cancer.

---

## Phase 1 (Nicieza/McGuinness foundational arc, early canon): The Volunteer

**Diagnosis through Hospice escape.** This is the formative event horizon. Affect regulation in this phase shows the catastrophic collapse signature: when told he was terminal, Wilson did not metabolize the news — he ruptured the Vanessa attachment within days, presenting it to her as a unilateral abandonment without explanation. This is *protective foreclosure*, a recognizable pattern in newly-diagnosed terminal patients with avoidant or fearful-avoidant attachment: the prospective loss is so unbearable it is enacted preemptively, in the dimension the patient can control. He took the only loss he could administer himself.

**Cognitive style under Hospice conditions.** Sharpened, narrowed, tactical. Surveillance of Ajax's routines, identification of allies (Worm), assessment of escape geometry. The narrative voice in this period (where rendered) is leaner and less manic than later — the humor is present but compressed, deployed as in-the-moment irritant rather than the metastatic monologue it later becomes. The verbal pathology had not yet fully assumed defensive load because the body was carrying the work directly.

**Self-concept in formation.** This is the phase in which the monster-schema acquires its mature content. Three sub-events fix it: (1) being told the disfigurement is permanent; (2) the Worm killing, in which he is *manipulated into* killing an attachment figure — fixing the schema *I cannot safely love anyone because loving them is itself the mechanism by which I kill them*; (3) Ajax's "killing" and disposal of him, fixing the schema *I cannot die when I need to; my survival itself is the punishment*. These three propositions remain the load-bearing beams of his self-concept for the next several decades. Nothing subsequent dislodges them; everything subsequent is built around them.

**Defenses crystallizing.** Identification with the aggressor is consolidated here — Ajax's signature was mockery during violence, and this is precisely the affective register Wilson assumes the moment he picks up a weapon for hire. Dissociation as method (not yet structured into "boxes") is documented in his account of the Worm killing and his post-disposal revival. He describes both with the flat-affect, third-person tinge characteristic of peritraumatic dissociation in survivors of inescapable abuse.

---

## Phase 2 (Joe Kelly run, *Deadpool* vol. 2, 1997–1998): The Mithras Years — Affective Architecture Stabilizes Around a Failed Reach for Meaning

**Affect regulation in this phase** demonstrates the early-mature form of the pattern that will hold for life: tolerable at extremes, intolerable at baseline. With Blind Al (the captive-attachment, mother-coded figure he keeps in his apartment under coercion) and Weasel (the only "friend," held by transactional dependency), Wilson constructs a domestic environment that mimics intimacy while neutralizing its risks. The cruelty toward Al — the "Box," the petty humiliations — is not sadism. It is *attachment-testing*: he needs her to fail to leave under conditions that would justify leaving, so that the bond is proved by the failure of his attempts to break it. She passes. This is the first relationship of his adult life that survives his testing, and it sets the template (Cable, Bob, eventually a wider circle) by which all his durable attachments are formed.

**Cognitive style.** The internal monologue thickens. Not yet formalized into separate voices, but the narrative texture becomes the dense, associative, parenthesis-within-parenthesis flow that will be later split out into the boxes. Diagnostically this is the period in which *the monologue itself becomes the dissociation* — speaking-to-no-one as the externalized observer who keeps him from being alone with what he knows.

**Self-concept under stress: the Mithras arc.** The messianic prophecy storyline is the cleanest data point ever generated on Wilson's relationship to goodness. Offered a coherent prosocial role — *you are the chosen one, your suffering had meaning* — he accepts it tentatively, performs adequately, and then sabotages the framework rather than complete it. This is not nihilism; it is *intolerance of redemption*. Redemption would require him to revise the monster-schema, and the monster-schema is structurally necessary to him because it explains the Hospice (he deserved it) and exonerates the world (it wasn't gratuitous). Letting go of the schema would re-open the question of whether the suffering was meaningless, which is intolerable. He needs the suffering to have been earned more than he needs it to have ended.

**The Siryn pattern.** First clean instantiation of approach-then-sabotage-on-reciprocity. Theresa Cassidy responds to him with genuine interest and tenderness; Wilson, within the same arc, escalates self-presentation toward the grotesque, manufactures rupture, and treats the eventual loss as confirmation. The fearful-avoidant signature is unmistakable: hyperactivated attachment system simultaneously firing approach and threat-detection, with the latter winning whenever the former is reciprocated.

---

## Phase 3 (Simone, *Agent X* / *GLI*, mid-2000s): Stabilization-by-Holding — Evidence That Regulation Is Possible

**This is the dosimetric phase**: the run that demonstrates what Wilson looks like when held by a non-threatening, predominantly female social unit (Outlaw, Sandi, the loose Agency X structure). Affect regulation is observably better. Humor is still primary defense but its frame-breaks are less frequent; the manic ceiling is lower; the violence is less theatrical and more efficient. Cognitive style remains scanning and tactical but with longer planning horizons. He is, for this period, functional.

**Diagnostically critical inference.** The Simone period proves that the dysregulation is *not* an intrinsic personality structure beyond modification; it is a state maintained by interpersonal threat and relaxed by interpersonal safety. This is exactly the prediction CPTSD theory makes. The relevant variable is not insight or effort — it is the surrounding relational field. He cannot regulate himself, but he can be regulated *by environment*. This finding will hold for every subsequent decade: every period of relative stabilization correlates with a holding configuration of attachments, and every relapse correlates with their collapse.

**Self-concept in this phase** does not fundamentally shift — the monster-schema persists — but it becomes briefly bracketable. Wilson is able to operate without the schema dominating consciously, while still organizing behavior beneath. This is the closest thing to remission he ever achieves and it is preserved entirely by the surround.

---

## Phase 4 (Daniel Way run, 2008–2012): Decompensation, Voice Formalization, and the Hunger for Legitimacy

**The decompensation.** The Simone holding-environment dissolves and the affective baseline deteriorates sharply. The most diagnostically important development of this period is the *formalization of the internal voices into the canonical "boxes"* — yellow and white, with characteristic content. From a structural-dissociation framework (Van der Hart / Nijenhuis / Steele), this is the maturation of previously informal dissociated self-states into stable Emotional Parts of the Personality with distinct affective tone and function. The yellow-coded voice carries the impulsive, id-aligned, aggressive content; the white-coded voice carries the observational, cooler, often more cynical commentary; Wilson's host-consciousness sits between them, co-conscious, frequently negotiating. This is *not* DID (no separate executive control, no amnestic barriers, no fully distinct autobiographical memory per part) — it is structural dissociation of personality at a level between BPD and DID, exactly the band CPTSD predicts.

**Bea Arthur fixation.** Following Blind Al's loss in this run, the libidinal redirection toward an absent older woman (deceased actress, public maternal-grandmother cultural figure) is a textbook idealization of an unattainable maternal object. The selection criterion is impossibility: she cannot reciprocate, cannot reject, cannot be hurt by him, cannot die again. The fixation provides the function of an attachment without any of its risks. This is the same structural slot later occupied by his romanticization of Death.

**The Avengers obsession and the Osborn exploitation.** This is the single largest exploitable surface of Wilson's psychology, displayed unambiguously. The hunger to be admitted to a moral in-group is so acute that *anyone* who frames an offer in terms of belonging-to-the-good can route him. Norman Osborn reads this perfectly and uses him as an unwitting asset throughout Dark Reign. The clinical finding is that Wilson's reality-testing is intact regarding facts but compromised regarding *legitimacy cues* — he cannot accurately judge whether a source of validation is itself legitimate, because the hunger overrides the appraisal. This vulnerability persists and will be exploited again (Rogers/Hydra-Cap).

**Affect regulation in this phase** is markedly worse than Simone-era baseline. Verbal output is at career-high density. Violence is more spectacular and less efficient. Sleep is, by implication, essentially absent. The self-concept oscillation between *monster who deserved it* and *the-one-who-sees-the-joke* runs faster and the gap between the two narrows into open contradiction held simultaneously.

---

## Phase 5 (Posehn/Duggan run, 2012–2015): Domesticity, Daughter, Double Betrayal — Peak Integration, Peak Collapse

**This is the run that comes closest to actual change and demonstrates, by failing, why change is structurally blocked.**

**The Shiklah marriage.** Object choice is the clinical tell. A Succubus-coded immortal queen who literally cannot be killed by him is selected precisely because she is the one partner whose loss he cannot inflict. This is a sophisticated workaround to the Worm-schema (*I kill what I love*): marry someone who is unkillable, and the schema is preemptively defeated. The fact that the marriage nonetheless fails (and by his hand, behaviorally) demonstrates that the schema does not require the death of the loved object to operate — it will manufacture rupture by other means.

**Eleanor.** The discovery of his daughter is the single most regulating event in the entire record. Affect regulation visibly improves; child-protection drive overrides nearly all other priorities; he attempts, awkwardly and with real effort, to construct a fatherhood that is the inverse of every paternal scenario in his rotating origin stories. The cognitive style in his father-scenes is *slower* — pauses between jokes, observation before reaction, calibration to a small person's pace. This is the only context in which his nervous system tolerates stillness. The pressure-point finding from §5 is confirmed in vivo: children at risk override everything, and his own child reorganizes his behavior at a level no other relationship has accessed.

**The Butler revelation.** Learning that his family was systematically murdered to torment him reactivates the Hospice-template in compressed form: an external agent has been engineering his losses all along, confirming his deepest schema (*the world is cruel by design, the cruelty is personal*) while simultaneously exonerating him (*it wasn't me who killed them, it was done to me*). The mixed affect is observable in his violence during this arc: more focused, less performative, briefly purposive in a way the mercenary work rarely is.

**The *Original Sin* revelation.** Discovery that Steve Rogers/SHIELD manipulated him into assassinating innocents is a second-generation Hospice event. The pattern is identical: trusted authority offering meaningful purpose delivers, instead, weaponized exploitation. Wilson's response — radicalization toward conventional heroism, sincere attempt at moral repair — is the most prosocial sustained motion in the record. It demonstrates the residual ethic is not dormant but actively waiting for permission.

**The Coulson assassination under Hydra-Cap.** And then permission is revoked, by the same mechanism. The Civil War II arc closes the loop with savage symmetry: having reached for legitimacy a second time, he is exploited again, by an authority figure of the same valence as the first. The collapse following this is the deepest in the record. Self-concept post-Coulson reverts hard to the monster-schema with no countervailing position available. Affect regulation collapses to the most regressed form of the humor defense — the manic, self-disgusted, fourth-wall-breaking monologue that admits everything and metabolizes nothing.

**The clinical finding from this phase** is decisive: Wilson can reach for integration, can sustain it under good conditions, and remains catastrophically vulnerable to a specific predator class (the legitimacy-offering authority figure who exploits the hunger to be admitted to the moral community). Until that vulnerability is structurally addressed — which would require either the disappearance of such figures from his environment, or the development of an internal authority that does not require external admission — recovery has a hard ceiling.

---

## Phase 6 (Duggan solo / Kelly return / Kibblesmith / Adams, late 2010s–present): Metacommentary Thickens, Custody Lost, Circle Slowly Widens

**Affect regulation.** Post-Coulson baseline does not return to pre-Eleanor levels. There is a permanent downshift in tolerable affect intensity at rest, partially compensated by an upshift in tolerable stimulation ceiling — he can handle more chaos than ever and less stillness than ever. The bandwidth of livable internal states narrows.

**Cognitive style.** The defining development is the *thickening of metacommentary*. Fourth-wall breaks become not occasional ruptures but the ambient texture of consciousness. Diagnostically this is *depersonalization-derealization elevated to ideology*: the observation that he is a character in a comic is correct in-universe, which makes the defense ego-syntonic and non-falsifiable. He has organized his entire epistemology around a true proposition that happens to function as a defense. This is the cleanest example in the record of insight-without-mentalization: he can articulate his own condition with clinical precision and is in no way changed by the articulation, because the articulation itself has become a defense against being changed.

**Self-concept.** Splits further but in a new direction. The two old schemas (*monster*, *seer-of-the-joke*) are joined by a third, increasingly accessed: *the one who knows he is fictional and is therefore both more and less responsible than anyone else in the frame*. This third position is the most stable he has, because it cannot be invalidated by events within the frame.

**Custody loss of Eleanor.** The single most regulating attachment of the entire record is removed. He survives this — biology forbids the alternative — but the post-loss behavior is the most diffuse and least purposive of any extended period in the file. The Mercs for Money managerial-failure arc is best read as displacement of the lost paternal role into a surrogate dependency structure (a small group reliant on him) that he then fails to manage, confirming the *I cannot hold what I love* schema at a lower-stakes register. The Kraken/Monster-King storyline does similar work at a more absurd register: family-man fantasies refracted through fantasy genre, where the absurdity itself prevents the affect from settling.

**The slow widening of the survived-testing circle.** The single piece of unambiguous good news in the late record is that the cohort of attachments that have outlasted his testing has, very slowly, expanded. Blind Al, Weasel, Cable, Bob, Outlaw, and a small rotating cast of others constitute, by the present moment, a *de facto* chosen family — a configuration none of the early-canon material would have predicted possible. The mechanism is not insight; it is *time and the failure of his testing to dislodge them*. People who refuse to leave at the rate at which he tries to make them leave eventually accumulate into a holding structure that does, marginally, regulate him. This is the longitudinal good news: he cannot heal, but he can be slowly out-waited by enough people that the dysregulation has somewhere to sit.

---

## Cross-Decadal Synthesis: What Evolved, What Did Not, What Cannot

**Evolved.**
- The verbal defense thickened from compressed humor into a continuous metacommentary; the dissociation correspondingly formalized from informal multiplicity into structured self-states with stable voice-content.
- The circle of survived-testing attachments slowly widened. This is the only unambiguous improvement.
- The capacity to *reach for* prosocial integration strengthened across decades — Mithras (sabotaged early), Avengers (exploited middle), post-*Original Sin* repair (exploited late), and the persistent paternal effort with Eleanor (sustained the longest). The reach itself is more sustained each iteration even when the outcome is destroyed.
- Insight-density increased dramatically. He can now name his pathology with a precision that exceeds most working clinicians.

**Did not evolve.**
- The monster-schema is unchanged from Hospice baseline.
- Approach-then-sabotage-on-reciprocity persists with every new attachment that crosses the threshold.
- Vulnerability to legitimacy-offering authority figures remains complete and re-exploitable.
- Resting-state intolerance has, if anything, worsened.

**Cannot evolve, by structural argument.**
- Personality reorganization at this severity ordinarily requires periods of regulated collapse — controlled regression in the context of a sustaining therapeutic relationship — followed by reconstitution at a higher level of integration. Wilson cannot collapse: the healing factor, the impossibility of dying, the continuous regeneration of the very neural tissue that would have to remodel, all prevent the breakdown that precedes breakthrough. He is *held permanently at the moment of breaking* (§4), and personality growth at his level of pathology requires moving through that moment to the other side. He cannot.
- The insight he has accumulated is therefore not mobilizable into change. It functions, instead, as a sophisticated defense — the most articulate possible description of the cage, offered from inside the cage, without the bars moving.

**The closing finding.** Across the longitudinal record, what changes is not the subject but the *surround*. The variance in his functioning is almost entirely accounted for by the configuration of his attachments at any given moment. He is, in the most precise sense, an externally regulated organism whose internal regulation was foreclosed by trauma before the biology that would have permitted reorganization was installed. The intervention indicated — and it is the only one with any longitudinal support in his own record — is not therapeutic in the formal sense. It is the slow, patient maintenance of a holding environment by people who refuse to be driven away at the rate he attempts to drive them away. This is, observably, what has produced every period of relative stabilization in his recorded life, and it is, observably, what is producing the marginal trajectory of improvement detectable across three decades of file.

He is improving at the rate his biology permits, which is: barely, and only because the people who stayed, stayed.


## Psychiatric Assessment & Differential

# PSYCHIATRIC ASSESSMENT & DIFFERENTIAL

## Subject: Wilson, Wade Winston — File Designation DP-Ψ-01

---

## 0. Framing Caveats Required Before Any Axis Is Applied

Before the standard nosology is brought to bear on this subject, four irreducible features of the case must be foregrounded, because they distort every diagnostic instrument the file might otherwise lean on.

**First, the substrate is unstable.** The subject's central nervous system is in a state of continuous tear-down and reconstruction (see Medical §2). Memory encoding is unreliable not only by repression and dissociation but because the tissue performing the encoding is being replaced faster than consolidation can complete. Any diagnosis whose criteria depend on stable autobiographical memory (DID, MDD with melancholic specifiers, even ordinary PTSD's "persistent" qualifier) must be applied with the understanding that the apparatus of persistence is itself compromised.

**Second, the reality-testing benchmark is non-falsifiable.** The single most clinically arresting feature of the subject — sustained, structured awareness that he is a character being read — is, *in his universe*, accurate. Conventional reality-testing techniques (consensual validation, gentle reorientation, behavioral experiments designed to disconfirm the belief) cannot be deployed because the belief cannot be disconfirmed. This collapses the standard differential between depersonalization-derealization, delusional disorder, and schizotypal cognition, and it forces any honest assessment to treat the meta-awareness as a *coping ideology built on a true perception* rather than a symptom in the ordinary sense.

**Third, the natural endpoints of severe psychopathology are biologically forbidden to him.** Suicide cannot consummate. Catatonic collapse self-resolves within minutes as the neural substrate regenerates. Lethal substance overdose cannot be reached. Psychotic decompensation of the kind that ordinarily produces a hospitalizable break and a reset is biochemically truncated. The disorders below are therefore observed in a form **no clinician of the regular human population has ever seen**: chronic, uncollapsing, undying, and uncured by either treatment or death.

**Fourth, the patient is an unreliable historian by design, not by accident.** Wilson actively manufactures contradictory autobiographies (Kelly, *Deadpool* #-1 and #33; the recurring "true origin" gags across Way and Duggan). This is itself a diagnostic datum — not noise — and is treated as such below.

With those caveats logged, the assessment proceeds.

---

## 1. PRIMARY DIAGNOSIS

### 1.1 Complex Post-Traumatic Stress Disorder (ICD-11 6B41) — *Established, Severe, Chronic, Treatment-Resistant by Substrate*

This is the load-bearing diagnosis. Every other condition documented in this file is either a contributor to its etiology, a consequence of its presentation, or a misreading of one of its features.

**Etiology, layered.** The ICD-11 construct of CPTSD requires prolonged or repeated trauma from which escape was difficult or impossible, typically in interpersonal context. Wilson meets this threshold along at least three temporally distinct vectors:

- *Developmental adversity (presumed, content unrecoverable).* The contradictory childhood accounts — abusive father, abusive mother, dead parents, intact parents, parricide — should not be read as the absence of evidence. They are evidence of a specific pattern: a child whose early environment was sufficiently unsafe that no single narrative can be tolerated, and an adult whose defensive structure requires the originating wound to remain unfixed so that it cannot be revisited. The *affective register* of every variant is consistent (shame, abandonment, violence, blame-assignment to the self) even where the *facts* contradict. This is the signature of childhood adversity transmitted through a personality that cannot bear to know its own history.
- *Iatrogenic torture (the Hospice arc, Kelly).* Months to years of inescapable physical torment by Ajax under medical pretext, while medically dependent on the torturer's institution, while being told the torment was treatment. This is the textbook profile of complex trauma: prolonged, interpersonal, coupled with betrayal of a care-giving role, in conditions of captivity.
- *Iterated authority betrayal in adulthood.* The *Original Sin* revelation (Posehn/Duggan) that Steve Rogers's SHIELD had been weaponizing him under false pretenses; the *Secret Empire* sequence in which Hydra-Rogers used the trust Wilson had reorganized his life around to direct him to kill Coulson; the Osborn manipulation in *Dark Reign*. Each event meets the diagnostic threshold for a discrete Criterion A stressor and, in aggregate, functions as continuous re-traumatization across his adult timeline.

**Symptom presentation, behaviorally observable across the entire run:**

- *Re-experiencing.* Ajax persists as an obsessional object well past Ajax's death, returning in dream sequences, hallucinatory interludes, and ritualized combat patter (Wilson's torture-monologue idiom is Ajax's, internalized — see Identification with the Aggressor, §1.1 below).
- *Avoidance.* Two principal channels: dissociative (the boxes, the fourth-wall flight, geographical disappearance into distant theaters of operation when affect threatens consolidation) and behavioral (refusal to sit, refusal of silence, refusal of stillness, the structural impossibility of a therapy hour with him).
- *Persistent sense of threat / hyperarousal.* Chronic insomnia (implied across all major runs; he is reliably awake in the establishing panels of arcs that open at night), startle-equivalent escalation to violence, inability to be in a non-stimulated state, the constant verbal output that functions as an auditory perimeter alarm against his own internal silence.
- *Affective dysregulation (CPTSD-specific cluster).* Affect either absent or overwhelming, with no functional middle register. Tears and laughter interchangeable in the same panel. Sustained moderate sadness, moderate fear, or moderate satisfaction is essentially never observed.
- *Negative self-concept (CPTSD-specific).* The monster-schema, foregrounded in the Hospice flashbacks and in every mirror sequence across forty years of publication. "I deserved this" is the load-bearing belief; the disfigurement is treated by the subject as evidence rather than as injury.
- *Interpersonal disturbance (CPTSD-specific).* Disorganized attachment; relational testing to destruction; captive-attachment configurations; idealization of unattainable figures. See Personality §5 for the full mapping.

**Course over time.** Symptom intensity has been roughly stable across the documented decades, but the *interval between acute decompensations* has lengthened slightly, in step with the slow accumulation of attachments that have survived his testing (Cable, Bob, Weasel, Al, Eleanor when access is permitted, Outlaw and Sandi in the Simone period). The pattern is consistent with the trauma literature: CPTSD does not remit on its own, but consistent corrective relational experience produces measurable dilation of the symptom-free intervals without altering the core architecture. He is improving at the only rate his biology permits.

**Treatment-resistance, substrate-level.** Standard CPTSD modalities — phased trauma-focused work (Herman), prolonged exposure, EMDR, somatic experiencing, IFS — all presuppose a nervous system that can return to baseline regulation between sessions and a memory substrate that retains corrective experience. Wilson's substrate cannot reliably do either. Pharmacotherapy is functionally void: the healing factor metabolizes SSRIs, mood stabilizers, and benzodiazepines on a timescale shorter than their pharmacodynamics require. What works for him is not treatment but **slow relational accretion** — the corrective experience of attachments that survive his testing — which is the only intervention his biology cannot defeat.

---

## 2. PRINCIPAL COMORBIDITIES

### 2.1 Major Depressive Disorder, Recurrent, Severe, with Persistent Suicidal Ideation (DSM-5 296.33)

Distinct from the CPTSD affective dysregulation cluster, present in addition to it. Documented across every major run.

**Symptom presentation:**

- *Persistent dysphoria*, masked by stimulation-seeking and humor but consistently legible in the off-stage panels (private apartment scenes; Blind Al interludes; the rare introspective monologue, e.g. the closing pages of the Posehn/Duggan run).
- *Anhedonia*, paradoxically configured: the things that should produce pleasure (sex, food, victory, money) are pursued in volumes and frequencies suggestive of a man chasing a sensation he is no longer getting. The pursuit is itself the data.
- *Suicidal ideation, chronic and ego-syntonic.* This is not the crisis suicidality of acute MDD but a steady-state orientation of the libido toward its own termination. The personification of Death as romantic object (the Death-Wilson arc, Thanos's curse of immortality predicated specifically on Death's reciprocation of Wilson's affection) literalizes the libidinal investment.
- *Worthlessness/inappropriate guilt*, present beneath every joke, surfacing in the moments when the joke fails to land.

**Differential from the CPTSD affective cluster:** the dysphoria persists in the absence of trauma reminders, has its own circadian pattern (worse in the small hours, when no one needs him and the contracts are not in motion), and the suicidal ideation has an organized object (Death-as-person, not Death-as-relief), which is characteristic of a depressive disorder layered over the trauma rather than reducible to it.

**Course modifier — "frustrated by biology."** This is the diagnostically unique feature. The ordinary trajectory of severe MDD includes either suicide attempt (with morbidity, mortality, or rescue), pharmacological response, spontaneous remission, or progression to catatonic depression. None of these endpoints is available to Wilson. The condition is therefore observed in a form clinical literature does not contain: a depression that has been denied every one of its natural outcomes for decades and is held permanently at the suicidal-ideation phase without progression or relief.

### 2.2 Dissociative Disorder NOS (DSM-5 300.15) with Prominent Depersonalization-Derealization Features

The dissociative architecture is the second pillar of the presentation. It requires careful sub-differentiation (see §3.2 below).

**Observable phenomena:**

- *Structurally dissociated self-states (the boxes).* Stable across decades, characterologically distinct (one impulsive/aggressive, one observational/cynical, one prosocial/conscience-functioned), auditory in modality, co-conscious with the host. They commentate, argue, advise, mock, and occasionally seize narrative privilege without seizing executive control. They are best modeled as **internalized object-relations rendered audible**, with possible organic contribution from the regenerating cortical tissue.
- *Depersonalization-derealization elevated to coping ideology.* The fourth-wall awareness — recognition that he is a comic-book character — discharges the affective load of his condition by relocating it outside the self ("none of this is happening to a real person; none of this counts"). In any other patient this would be a delusional or dissociative symptom. In his universe it is true. The clinical importance lies not in the truth-value of the belief but in the *use* he makes of it, which is identical to the use a depersonalized patient makes of their derealization: distance from unbearable affect.
- *Time loss, identity confusion, and confabulation*, partially substrate-driven (the regenerating brain), partially dissociative. Diagnostically irresolvable as to which mechanism predominates in any given episode.

### 2.3 Personality Organization: Borderline Level (Kernberg), with Mixed Cluster B Features

Wilson does not cleanly meet a single DSM-5 personality disorder. He meets *features* of several, organized at borderline structural level per Kernberg's framework — identity diffusion (literalized in the contradictory origins), reliance on primitive defenses (splitting, projective identification, acting out, dissociation, denial, primitive idealization, devaluation), and reality testing that is grossly preserved but porous under stress.

**Borderline Personality Disorder features (DSM-5 301.83):** identity disturbance (criterion-level), abandonment sensitivity (criterion-level, modulated by anticipatory pre-rupture), affective instability (criterion-level), recurrent suicidal behavior and self-mutilating gestures (criterion-level, though decoupled from lethal intent by substrate), chronic emptiness (criterion-level, defended against by stimulation), inappropriate intense anger (criterion-level, expressed as theatrical violence), transient stress-related dissociation (criterion-level, chronic in his case). **Meets the threshold cleanly.** Were it not for the trauma history and the dissociative features, BPD would be the single best fit.

**Antisocial Personality Disorder features (DSM-5 301.7):** the occupational behavior (contract killing, fraud, weapons offenses, repeated violations of bodily autonomy in combat) meets antisocial conduct criteria. **The core psychological structure does not.** ASPD requires callousness, lack of remorse, and absence of empathy. Wilson demonstrates: (a) consistent empathy under conditions where it costs him (child rescues, target sparing, the refusal of certain contracts on moral grounds, the Mithras arc's reach toward meaning); (b) recoverable guilt, dissociated under ordinary circumstances but observable when defenses are stripped (Coulson aftermath; Eleanor custody loss); (c) capacity for altruistic action at personal cost (numerous documented instances of taking grievous injury to protect non-paying parties). The mercenary career is best read as a **trauma-compatible occupation** — work whose normalized violence matches his nervous system's calibration — rather than as the behavioral expression of antisocial character structure.

**Histrionic Personality Disorder features (DSM-5 301.50):** performative affect, attention-seeking, theatrical presentation, rapidly shifting and shallow emotion (publicly; less so privately), suggestibility under flattery from authority figures. **Secondary feature, in service of the humor defense.** The performative quality is a regulatory strategy, not a primary characterological hunger for attention.

**Narcissistic Personality Disorder — not supported.** The grandiosity is performative-defensive, brittle, and readily falls away under genuine threat to the survival-grandiose-self. NPD requires the entitled expectation of admiration and is destabilized by *withdrawal* of admiration. Wilson is destabilized by *receipt* of admiration. The vector is reversed. He expects to be despised and his defenses are organized around that expectation; sincere admiration produces flight, deflection, or the suspicion of a setup. This is the signature of shame-organized rather than narcissistically organized personality.

### 2.4 Substance Use Disorders (DSM-5 various) — Subthreshold by Biology, Suprathreshold by Behavior

A complicated entry. The healing factor metabolizes ethanol, cannabinoids, opioids, and most stimulants on a timescale that renders intoxication transient at best. The DSM-5 substance-use criteria nonetheless apply to *behavior*, not to subjective effect, and on that axis Wilson meets multiple criteria: time spent obtaining and using, use in physically hazardous situations, continued use despite consequences, tolerance (extreme; biologically enforced), persistent desire to cut down (occasionally voiced and never sustained). What is striking is that **the pursuit of intoxication he cannot achieve is itself a behavioral pattern of clinical interest** — the *chase* is the symptom; the unreachable goal is the diagnostically meaningful feature. This is consistent with substance use as a self-regulatory ritual rather than as pharmacological dependence, and it places his pattern closer to a behavioral-addiction model than to a substance-use disorder in the classical sense.

### 2.5 Chronic Pain Syndrome with Pain-Behavior Decoupling

Not a psychiatric diagnosis per the manuals, but operationally relevant. Wilson experiences continuous low-grade pain (regenerating tumor-tissue interface, skin) and episodic acute pain (every regenerative event). His pain receptors are intact; the healing factor does not anesthetize.
