Onset latency long; will lie awake talking to the boxes for hours. Sleep is most achievable post-violence (the post-combat parasympathetic crash) or post-significant caloric intake. Nightmare content (per occasional textual admission in Kelly and Posehn/Duggan) Hospice-themed; subject wakes verbalizing, often laughing. Will not share a bed for an entire night even with intimate partners — leaves to sleep on a couch or floor by approximately hour two of any co-sleep attempt. The withdrawal is presented as consideration ("you don't want this next to you") and functions as exit-control.

---

## 2. URBAN MOVEMENT, ROUTES, & SPATIAL HABITS

**GIVEN: subject traveling from residence to a destination on foot in a city he knows.**
EXPECT: never the direct route. Will run a counter-surveillance loop even when not under threat — the habit is dissociated from the rational need for it. Preference for rooftops, alleys, fire escapes, and the second-story routes (parkour-grade traversal his factor permits without injury cost) over street level. When street level is required, will hug building lines on the side opposite oncoming foot traffic, cross streets mid-block, prefer covered scaffolding, and ride the inside of any group of pedestrians taller than him.

**GIVEN: subject required to enter a transit hub (subway, bus terminal, train station).**
EXPECT: pre-mapped multiple egress, will identify the camera blind spots within thirty seconds of entry, will board the last car of any train, will not sit. Reads other passengers compulsively for threat profile and finds it regulating rather than tiring. Will leave a transit vehicle one stop before or after his actual destination at least 50% of the time, by reflex.

**GIVEN: subject in an unfamiliar building (office, apartment complex, hospital).**
EXPECT: stairwells over elevators by strong default (the elevator is a kill-box he understands too well); if elevators required, will not face the doors and will not stand on the door wall. Will touch the architecture as he moves — door frames, walls — both for spatial mapping and as a self-regulating tactile loop. Will identify ceiling tile breakaways, HVAC accesses, and at least two windows that can be defenestrated through without significant injury to him within his first transit of any floor.

**GIVEN: subject required to wait (lobby, waiting room, restaurant before a meet).**
EXPECT: cannot sit facing away from the entrance. Will arrive at least 15 minutes early to claim the correct seat, or up to 30 minutes late if the correct seat cannot be guaranteed. Magazines and phones are decoys; he is tracking everyone. Will eat or drink anything available — peanuts, mints, the floral arrangement — as oral regulation. Speaks to staff with disproportionate familiarity within ninety seconds, learning names, telling jokes; this is reconnaissance and self-soothing simultaneously, and the staff member will remember him as either delightful or deeply unsettling with no middle reaction.

**GIVEN: subject's known neighborhoods of preference.**
EXPECT: low-rent, high-density, ethnically heterogeneous, with significant late-night commerce — neighborhoods that absorb a masked man with a katana harness without producing 911 calls. Strong preference for residential floors above commercial (the noise floor masks his own; the foot traffic provides cover; the commercial below provides 24-hour food). Avoids gated communities, single-family-home suburbs, and any zoning where his presence becomes a singularity. Will not live above the sixth floor unless a window-to-roof transit is mapped.

**GIVEN: subject's vehicle preferences.**
EXPECT: nothing he is sentimental about. Owns no car he cares if he loses. Preference for vehicles that are inconspicuous in his operating neighborhood (work trucks, food-delivery vans, mid-2000s sedans), modified only for trunk capacity and the ability to dispose of fluids. Drives competently but not skillfully; he is bored by driving and will narrate aloud throughout. Public transit and stolen rideshares preferred for short trips. Will not ride motorcycles by personal choice — too exposed, too loud as a signature, the helmet covers his face which he should like but in fact dislikes because it removes his ability to make the mask choice consciously.

---

## 3. MONEY & MATERIAL LIFE

**GIVEN: subject's payment structure on any contract.**
EXPECT: significant overhead inflation in the quote (he expects to be cheated and prices accordingly); 30–50% up front in cash or untraceable transfer; refusal of equity, cryptocurrency arrangements he cannot immediately liquidate, or any compensation structure that requires him to remain in relationship with the client beyond delivery. He will, with surprising consistency, undercut his own quote when the client is visibly struggling (single parent, small business, victim of the target). This pattern is unannounced and predictable: clients who present as desperate-but-sympathetic pay roughly half of clients who present as corporate.

**GIVEN: subject's cash management.**
EXPECT: distributed caches across multiple cities, low-tech (taped behind drywall, inside dead drops in storage units rented under permutations of "Jack Hammer," "Wade Wilson," and joke names that would not pass a serious background check). No financial advisor. No investment portfolio. Owns no real estate in his real name and most likely none at all — rents under aliases, paid annually in cash where possible. Loses access to caches regularly through inattention, address drift, and dissociative amnesia about where he put them; treats these losses with surprising equanimity. The money is not the point.

**GIVEN: subject in a legitimate retail interaction.**
EXPECT: overpays, over-tips, and chats compulsively. Will tip a server 40–100% in cash. Will buy something he does not need to justify standing in the store. Will not use loyalty cards or any tracked-purchase mechanism. Will return for the same store only if the staff has been kind to him, in which case he becomes a regular and develops a parasocial bond they did not consent to.

**GIVEN: subject's possessions in totality.**
EXPECT: weapons in disproportion to all other categories combined; food and alcohol in second place; entertainment media (DVDs, action figures, plush toys, vintage merchandise from his cultural touchpoints) in third — these are kept with care that no other category receives, dusted, displayed, replaced if damaged. Books, sparse but present (mostly genre paperbacks, joke books, a few unexpected items — poetry, a self-help title hidden in a drawer). Photographs, almost none — the few that exist are of Eleanor and are kept face-down or in sealed envelopes opened at irregular intervals.

---

## 4. FOOD, DRINK, ORAL BEHAVIOR

**GIVEN: subject ordering at a restaurant.**
EXPECT: orders too much, modifies the order excessively (extra of everything, substitutions, jokes the server has heard before delivered as if novel), eats fast, does not finish. The bill is paid in cash with a tip that registers as either generous or unsettling. If the table is intimate (a date, a meeting with Cable, a custody-visit meal with Eleanor) the modification noise drops by half and he will actually finish what he ordered.

**GIVEN: subject's chimichanga consumption frequency.**
EXPECT: lower than the canonical bit suggests in actual private behavior; the chimichanga is a public performance of the chimichanga bit. He eats them, but he eats many other things equivalently. The bit is a stable joke he uses to deflect food conversations into safe territory and to give other people an easy in.

**GIVEN: subject drinking, social context.**
EXPECT: orders volume he cannot intoxicate himself with and treats it as a comedic point. Will buy rounds reflexively. Will not let anyone else pay for him if avoidable (debt is a hook). Will switch from beer to whiskey to whatever the other person is having to maintain conversational rhythm, with no actual preference. Late in any night, will be the most sober person at the table while presenting as the most drunk.

**GIVEN: subject's smoking, gum, oral fixations.**
EXPECT: cycles through. Will pick up smoking for an arc, drop it, pick up gum, drop it, chew toothpicks, chew straws, gnaw the inside of his cheek (heals immediately, can be done indefinitely). Constant oral occupation; pacifier-equivalent behaviors. The mouth must be doing something or saying something at all times.

---

## 5. INTERPERSONAL — STRANGERS, SERVICE, AUTHORITY

**GIVEN: subject encountering a service worker (barista, cashier, mechanic, hotel clerk).**
EXPECT: rapid familiarity, name learned, joke deployed, story extracted. They will remember him. He will use what he learned within fifteen minutes for tactical or social purposes. This is reconnaissance dressed as friendliness and is also, separately, real friendliness — the two are not distinguishable in him.

**GIVEN: subject encountering uniformed law enforcement in a non-combat context (traffic stop, ID check, lobby security).**
EXPECT: compliance, performance of normalcy, jokes calibrated to lower the officer's threat assessment, total internal documentation of badge numbers and vehicle plates. He is non-threatening to police in proportion to his ability to vanish from them afterward. The mask in such contexts will be off if removal is requested; he hates this and accepts it because the alternative is escalation he cannot afford. Will be exceptionally polite. Will follow up with an anonymous prank on the officer within 72 hours if mistreated.

**GIVEN: subject encountering a child in a civilian context.**
EXPECT: full-mask presentation is preferred (the child responds to the costume as costume); affect shifts immediately to a gentler register; jokes are calibrated down to age-appropriate without becoming patronizing — he is unusually good at this. Will not pick up an unknown child without parental cue. Will be intensely vigilant of the surrounding adults; threat assessment of guardians is automatic and harsh. If he assesses a guardian as a threat to the child, the interaction will not end where the guardian thinks it does.

**GIVEN: subject encountering an obviously disabled, disfigured, or stigmatized person in public.**
EXPECT: zero discomfort, immediate solidarity expressed through irreverence rather than condescension, frequently the gentlest version of him strangers ever see. He does not flinch from what others flinch from. This is one of the cleanest signals in his record of an intact moral core — the camaraderie of the marked.

**GIVEN: subject encountering an authority figure offering legitimacy (a hero recruiter, a government liaison, a religious figure, a wellness professional).**
EXPECT: surface deflection (jokes, transgression, the bit), underneath which the offer is being scrutinized with painful intensity. He will not say yes immediately and will not say no easily. Pressure points are open here; the pattern of being outplayed by Osborn and Hydra-Rogers will recur in any context where someone with apparent moral authority asks him to belong. The decision will be made on a basis he cannot articulate (smell, posture, a single tonal cue) and will be defended afterward with rationalization. If the recruiter passes his unconscious test, his loyalty will be excessive; if they fail, he will sabotage them with prejudice.

**GIVEN: subject encountering a journalist, biographer, or anyone seeking his story.**
EXPECT: extended cooperation followed by deliberate corruption of the record. Will provide three or four mutually exclusive origin accounts within a single interview, signaled by escalating absurdity. This is not whimsy; it is the load-bearing defense. To be narrated is to be fixed, and fixity is intolerable. Any biographer who persists into a second session will become either a friend or a target, and the determining variable is whether they laughed at the right things in session one.

**GIVEN: subject encountering a therapist or any sincere mirroring offer.**
EXPECT: virtuoso performance of insight, comedic confession of the precise pathology the clinician was about to name, and exit before the next session. He will be a brilliant patient for forty-five minutes and a no-show for the second appointment. If forced to continue (court order, contract, Cable-organized intervention), will escalate the comedy until the clinician's countertransference produces either a boundary failure (which he will exploit) or a moralistic withdrawal (which he will accept as proof his model is correct). The single intervention type that has a non-zero chance of holding him is one that does not ask him to be other than he is and that survives his testing without flinching — i.e., not therapy, but presence.

---

## 6. INTIMATE & SEXUAL BEHAVIOR

**GIVEN: subject in a one-night or short-term sexual encounter.**
EXPECT: pre-encounter humor in disproportion; partial unmasking only (the mask half-rolled, lights low or off, his preferred positions are those that keep his face out of the partner's sightline); generosity of attention to the partner that reads as overcompensation and largely is; rapid post-coital affect collapse, exit by sunrise. Will leave money or food behind even when not asked, as a kind of obscure penance. Will not exchange contact information unless drunk-equivalent or destabilized.

**GIVEN: subject in an emerging serious attachment.**
EXPECT: the documented pattern accelerated — testing, sabotage, withdrawal at the moment of reciprocity, a manufactured rupture timed to precede a feared organic one. With partners who survive the first three test cycles (Vanessa, Shiklah at points), behavior stabilizes into a recognizably tender register that he will then guard with disproportionate violence against external threat and undermine with disproportionate self-sabotage from within. Sexual frequency in stable attachment: high, varied, often used as affect regulation rather than connection — the partner will need to learn to distinguish.

**GIVEN: subject's pornography or solo sexual behavior in private.**
EXPECT: present, performed self-mockingly even when unwitnessed (the boxes are an audience). Tastes likely wide and unembarrassed; he has no shame infrastructure for sexuality, only for being seen. Will narrate to himself. Will be interrupted by intrusive thought, switch to food, return, abandon. The act is rarely consummated cleanly; like intoxication, the chase is the point.

**GIVEN: subject's behavior around a former partner he still loves.**
EXPECT: avoidance dressed as respect, surveillance dressed as casual interest (knows where she lives, where she works, when she changed her car), explosive reactivity if she is endangered. Will not initiate contact and will collapse if she does. The one-time exception will be a crisis pretext (a real or manufactured threat to her) that gives him narrative permission to appear.

---

## 7. THE FEW WHO STAYED — STABLE-ATTACHMENT BEHAVIOR

**GIVEN: subject with Cable, low-stakes interaction.**
EXPECT: relentless verbal needling calibrated to Cable's specific tolerances, which he has mapped with high resolution. Affection expressed entirely through provocation. Will follow Cable's lead on operational decisions while loudly objecting to each one. Sits closer than necessary, touches with familiarity (shoulder, arm), eats Cable's food without asking. Cable's silences are read accurately; he knows when Nathan needs the bit to stop and stops, though never gracefully.

**GIVEN: subject with Bob (Agent of Hydra).**
EXPECT: protective register dominant; the cruelty-disguised-as-comedy is dialed to its softest setting because Bob actually metabolizes it as cruelty. Manages Bob's anxiety with surprising delicacy. Functions as Bob's protector and exploiter simultaneously and is uneasily aware of the second role; the relationship's stability depends on Bob's tolerance of this ambivalence.

**GIVEN: subject with Blind Al.**
EXPECT: oldest stable script in his repertoire. The dynamic is mutually abusive on the surface and structurally tender beneath; the abuse is the form their tenderness takes because both parties find sentimentality intolerable. Will bring food unprompted, fix appliances under the guise of breaking them more, leave and return without explanation knowing she will not demand one. The captive-housekeeper frame is the joke they share to manage the fact of mutual need.

**GIVEN: subject with Weasel.**
EXPECT: transactional surface (gear, intel, jobs) over a substrate of the only male friendship that has survived continuously. Will betray Weasel in small ways constantly (unpaid tabs, broken merchandise, late payments) and defend him with disproportionate violence against any third party. Weasel's complaints are tolerated to a precise threshold; past it, the room cools and Weasel knows to stop.

**GIVEN: subject with Eleanor.**
EXPECT: the single context in which the entire defensive architecture loosens visibly. Mask comes off more readily; humor recalibrates to her age; the metacommentary nearly stops. He is exceptionally attentive to her affect and over-reads it (any flatness will be interpreted as injury caused by him). Cannot tolerate her seeing him hurt; will hide injuries that would normally be displayed for comedy. After visits, returns to baseline with a delay — the recovery time is longer than after combat, because the contact has stirred affect that must then be metabolized in solitude, by the methods of section 1.

---

**GIVEN: subject at a public event he chose to attend (movie premiere, comic convention, concert).**
EXPECT: full mask,


## Predictive Model II — Crisis, Betrayal & the Wound

# Predictive Model II — Crisis, Betrayal & the Wound

*Operational forecasting for high-stakes, decompensation-edge behavior. Each entry: the precipitating GIVEN, the EXPECTED behavioral cascade with timing and observable markers, the underlying mechanism in his architecture, and (where relevant) the second-order prediction once the first response fails.*

---

## 1. Crisis — Acute Threat to Self

### 1.1 Conventional combat, outnumbered, no civilian variable

**GIVEN:** Subject ambushed, surrounded, or dropped into a kill-zone with no third-party stakes (a mercenary contract collection, a Hand cell, a corporate strike team).

**EXPECT:** Within the first three seconds, verbal output spikes — opening line is almost always a non-sequitur referencing the aesthetics of the ambushers (their uniforms, weapon choice, body odor, formation). This is not bravado but **somatic onboarding**: the talking is how he gets his nervous system from rest-state confusion into the calibrated-for-crisis register where he functions best (see §3, affect regulation at extreme intensity). Combat efficiency will be **highest in the first 30–90 seconds**, before the theatricality budget kicks in.

Around the 90-second mark — once he has confirmed the engagement is survivable — efficiency degrades and **spectacle takes over**: showy disarms, finishing moves with set-up beats, callouts to the dying, deliberate self-injury (taking a round to walk through fire). This is regulation, not tactics; the spectacle is metabolizing whatever pre-engagement affect was destabilizing him.

**Observable markers:** the shift from efficient to theatrical correlates with a drop in fourth-wall breaks (he stops needing the reader once the enemies have become the audience). If breaks *persist* into the spectacle phase, the engagement is harder than he is signaling and he is regulating poorly — predict an unscripted withdrawal or a deliberate maiming injury within the next 60 seconds, taken to force the body to do what the mind hasn't yet.

### 1.2 Outclassed by a single overwhelming adversary

**GIVEN:** One-on-one with someone categorically above his weight class (Hulk, Thanos-adjacent, a serious telepath, a god-tier).

**EXPECT:** The humor sharpens and becomes more **personal** — he abandons general comic patter for tailored mockery aimed at the adversary's known sensitivities. He has read the file; he will use it. This is identification with the aggressor (§3) deployed offensively: he becomes a small Ajax-figure, coupling violence with the cruelty-as-care register because that is the only frame in which extreme asymmetric violence is intelligible to him.

He will accept catastrophic injury — limb loss, evisceration, decapitation — as **pacing**, not catastrophe. The pain is real; the consequence is not; the gap is where his strategy lives. Expect at least one deliberate self-dismemberment used as a weapon (the severed-hand grenade pin, the headbutt-with-detached-head). If telepathic, the adversary will withdraw mental contact within seconds — the scrambled neural substrate is aversive to telepaths in proportion to the depth of the scan, and he knows this and will *invite the contact* to weaponize it.

**Failure mode:** if the adversary refuses to engage with the bit (silent, expressionless, methodical — the worst possible counter), his regulation degrades fast. Predict either flight (rare — he reads it as cowardice) or an escalation into self-destruction calibrated to force the adversary into an emotional response. He would rather be killed by someone who reacted than survive someone who didn't.

### 1.3 Conventional escape available; civilian variable present

**GIVEN:** A safe extraction is possible if he abandons a non-combatant (especially a child, an elderly captive, or a manifestly powerless target).

**EXPECT:** He will not take it, and he will not deliberate. The decision is **pre-cognitive** and overrides contract obligation, financial incentive, and self-preservation in that order. He will rationalize it afterward in mercenary terms ("the bounty on the kid was bigger," "I needed a witness," "shut up") because the sincere version is intolerable to him. Predict a marked drop in humor for the duration of the protective action — child-in-danger is one of the few states that gets through the defense to the prosocial substrate (§5, pressure points), and the humor doesn't return until the child is safe and the affect can be redirected back into bit-territory.

---

## 2. Crisis — Acute Threat to a Bonded Other

### 2.1 Cable, Bob, Weasel, or Blind Al taken or threatened

**GIVEN:** One of the tested-and-passed attachment figures is captured, tortured, or used as leverage.

**EXPECT:** This is the **highest-priority interrupt** in his system, and the behavioral signature is unmistakable. The humor goes quiet — not absent, but reduced to clipped, mirthless one-liners that no longer break the fourth wall. The metacommentary stops. Anyone who has observed him across enough operations will recognize this state as the most dangerous he gets: he is not regulating through spectacle, he is operating in his pre-Hospice mercenary register, the cold competent shooter that the rest of the persona is built to obscure.

Predict: rapid travel without explanation, expenditure of contacts and favors he has been hoarding for years, willingness to incur debts (to Cable, to Domino, to anyone with the asset) that he will spend the next arc resenting and complying with. He will not call the Avengers. He will not call for help to most parties. He will call one or two specific operators — the calls are short, the asks are precise.

**Second-order:** if the bonded other is killed before extraction, predict an extended off-grid period (weeks to months) characterized by contract work in geographically distant theaters, escalated substance pursuit (the chase, not the result), and the cultivation of a new captive-attachment to replace the loss. The mourning is real but cannot be sat with; it has to be outrun until the affect attenuates enough to be metabolized in the usual way.

### 2.2 Eleanor in danger

**GIVEN:** His daughter is targeted, threatened, or even theoretically endangered.

**EXPECT:** Total collapse of the operational mask. He becomes legibly, dangerously sincere — and predictable in ways he otherwise is not. Any reasonably competent adversary who has done their homework can use Eleanor to puppet him into geographic and tactical positions of their choosing, which is exactly how the Butler arc worked and exactly what he has not been able to internalize as a generalized lesson because the alternative (treating her as not-priority) is unthinkable.

Predict: he will accept terms he knows are traps. He will go alone when going alone is stupid. He will agree to disarmament conditions. The only saving grace, tactically, is that his improvisational capacity inside the trap remains intact — he walks in knowing it's a trap, with three contingencies pre-loaded, and the cancer-riddled brain that can't plan a vacation can plan a single-room exit under pressure.

**Aftermath:** even successful resolutions of Eleanor-threats produce a withdrawal from Eleanor. He cannot tolerate the proximity of what he almost lost; the closer the call, the longer the subsequent absence. This is the approach-then-sabotage pattern (§3) literalized as parenting and is the mechanism by which custody losses became inevitable across the Posehn/Duggan and subsequent runs.

### 2.3 A vulnerable stranger seen mid-operation

**GIVEN:** During an unrelated contract, he witnesses an opportunistic crime or a power imbalance involving a defenseless third party.

**EXPECT:** Mission discipline degrades to zero. The contract becomes secondary. He will intervene, often loudly, often suboptimally, and frequently incur losses (cash, asset position, future relationships with the client) that he will later complain about and not, on reflection, regret. This is the unarticulated ethic from §5 manifesting as observable conduct — and is the single most reliable behavioral signature distinguishing him from a true ASPD operator.

---

## 3. Betrayal — By Authority

### 3.1 The framed-tasking betrayal (Original Sin pattern)

**GIVEN:** Subject discovers that a contract he completed in good faith was based on falsified intelligence supplied by a legitimacy-conferring authority (SHIELD, an Avenger, a national security figure), and his targets were innocent.

**EXPECT:** This is the **template-active betrayal** — the exact shape of Hospice (promised cure, delivered torture) reproduced at the level of moral injury rather than physical injury. Expect a three-phase response:

- **Phase 1 (hours to days): manic-defensive denial.** The fourth-wall breaks intensify to a degree that suggests he is renegotiating the reality of the discovery itself; humor becomes pressured and unfunny; he will pick fights with peripheral targets to discharge the affect without naming it.
- **Phase 2 (days to weeks): obsessional collation.** He goes quiet, geographically mobile, and begins compiling the evidence of the deception with a meticulousness that contradicts his presentation of cognitive disorganization. The dossier-building is itself the regulation — he is performing on the betrayer the act of being known that he cannot tolerate having performed on him.
- **Phase 3: ritualized confrontation.** Not assassination — *confrontation*. He needs the betrayer to be present, to see him, to acknowledge what was done. The violence, when it comes, is staged for the betrayer's benefit and frequently spared at the last moment, because the satisfaction he is seeking is recognition, not retribution.

**Second-order:** the subsequent radicalization-toward-heroism (the same Original Sin → "I will be good now" overcorrection) is the **most exploitable interval in his entire behavioral cycle**. Any second authority figure who arrives in the immediate aftermath with a "we believe in you" frame will be trusted at a level wildly disproportionate to the available evidence, because the hunger to be admitted to the moral community has been freshly inflamed and his discrimination is at its lifetime worst. This is exactly how the Hydra-Rogers/Coulson catastrophe became possible and is a repeatable vulnerability, not a one-time error.

### 3.2 The legitimacy lure (Osborn/Dark Reign pattern)

**GIVEN:** A high-status figure with apparent institutional backing offers him a path to legitimacy — Avengers membership, official sanction, a "team" of his own to lead, public recognition.

**EXPECT:** He will know it is a manipulation. He will say so out loud, repeatedly, to himself and to the offering party. He will accept anyway. The meta-awareness does not protect against the pull — this is insight-without-mentalization (§3) at its most operationally costly. The behavioral marker that the lure has caught is a **reduction in self-deprecation** in conversations with the offering party: he stops using the standard self-mocking patter and starts speaking in something closer to a straight voice, because the bid for legitimacy requires him to be momentarily takeable seriously, and he is grateful for the chance to try.

Predict that competence will *increase* during the initial honeymoon (he will work harder than the manipulator expected; he wants to deserve the offer), making the subsequent betrayal both inevitable and more damaging for the prep. The collapse, when the manipulation reveals itself, is in §3.1 above with one addition: shame. This is one of the few configurations that produces sustained shame rather than its dissociative comic substitute, and shame in his system is the single most destabilizing affect — predict either extended self-isolation or a self-endangerment cascade calibrated to extract punishment from the environment when he cannot administer it to himself.

### 3.3 The Ajax-coded clinician

**GIVEN:** He encounters a sadistic medical, scientific, or quasi-therapeutic figure — anyone who couples cruelty with care-language, who frames torture as treatment, who uses the second-person address of the clinic ("let's see what we can do for you") while inflicting harm.

**EXPECT:** Regression — fast, visible, and atypical for him. The voice register changes; the humor reverts to a younger, less-controlled mode; he will fixate on this figure beyond all tactical justification. Other priorities — contracts, bonded others, even (briefly) Eleanor — will be set aside while he pursues. The pursuit will not satisfy. Even Ajax's confirmed death did not extinguish the obsession, because the figure being pursued is not the person but the **template**, and templates do not die with people.

Predict that he will not accept third-party assistance against an Ajax-coded figure. The encounter has to be private, ritually structured, and survived alone, because the original was, and the repetition serves the function only when it mirrors the original conditions closely enough.

---

## 4. Betrayal — By Intimacy

### 4.1 The chosen partner leaves

**GIVEN:** A partner he has allowed into the inner ring (Vanessa across her various returns, Shiklah, anyone allowed past the testing phase) departs — by choice, by death, or by his own sabotage retroactively recognized.

**EXPECT:** Within 24 hours, the **schema is reasserted** — the *I am a monster who deserves what happened* configuration locks in with a finality that makes intervention difficult. The behavioral marker is not grief but a kind of grim cheerfulness: he becomes pleasant to be around in a way that should alarm anyone who knows him, because the affect is being shunted entirely into the performance and the cost is collecting somewhere off-screen.

Predict: increased contract acceptance over the following 2–6 weeks, with a preference for high-risk, low-prep work; a pattern of brief sexual encounters that he will refer to with conspicuous crudeness; a reluctance to return to any geography associated with the departed; the cultivation or deepening of a captive-attachment to fill the structural slot (Blind Al historically; whatever dependent figure is currently available).

**The sabotage subtype** (where he engineered the departure) presents identically with one tell: he will mention the partner unprompted, in joke form, in tactical contexts where they are entirely irrelevant. The mention is a confession he cannot make directly.

### 4.2 Mirroring without judgment

**GIVEN:** Someone — therapist, friend, lover, an unusually perceptive enemy — accurately reflects his actual internal state back to him without contempt and without instrumentalization. They simply see him and say so.

**EXPECT:** This is, paradoxically, more destabilizing than torture. Predict, in order of likely manifestation: (1) deflection via escalated humor, fourth-wall break, or transgressive provocation calibrated to recover the contempt that should be there; (2) if the mirroring holds, physical flight from the room within minutes; (3) if flight is blocked, a violent or sexual lunge designed to corrupt the interaction into a register he can survive; (4) if all of the above are absorbed without judgment, decompensation — silence, immobility, and a flat affect that he cannot maintain for long before either weeping (rare, and he will not permit witnesses) or violence against a non-human object (frequent).

Operational note: this is why long-form therapy will not work on him. Any clinician competent enough to hold him in the mirror is competent enough to be perceived as Ajax-coded the moment the mirror produces pain, and the transference collapses into §3.3.

### 4.3 Discovery of an inner-ring deception

**GIVEN:** Cable, Bob, Weasel, or Blind Al is discovered to have lied to him, withheld a major fact, or acted against him in a measurable way — even with defensible motive.

**EXPECT:** This is rarer than the authority betrayals because the inner ring has been pre-tested to a punishing standard, but when it occurs the response is **uncharacteristically restrained**. He will not retaliate, will not confront immediately, will not even raise it. He will absorb the information and continue to function adjacent to the betrayer for an extended period — days to weeks — while internally reorganizing the relationship from inner-ring to a kind of probationary middle distance.

The eventual confrontation, when it comes, will be quiet, sober, and uncharacteristically articulate. He will use clearer language in that conversation than in any other context. Predict that the relationship can survive the rupture if the betrayer offers genuine accounting; loyalty, once invested, is durable in him beyond what the surface presentation suggests, and the testing model means he has already pre-paid for one major disappointment per inner-ring figure.

---

## 5. Temptation

### 5.1 The morally clean kill offered at premium rates

**GIVEN:** A contract presents an unambiguously deserving target (a confirmed trafficker, an obvious atrocity actor) at exceptional pay.

**EXPECT:** He takes it, completes it efficiently, and is in a noticeably better mood for several days afterward. The bit relaxes; the meta-commentary lightens. These contracts are the closest his architecture gets to integration — the mercenary identity and the prosocial substrate align, and the resulting reduction in internal contradiction registers as something approaching ease. Predict generosity in the immediate aftermath (overpayment of contacts, unprompted gifts to inner-ring figures, gestures toward Eleanor he will not be able to sustain).

### 5.2 The morally compromised kill at exceptional rates

**GIVEN:** A contract offers life-changing money to take a target whose deservingness is ambiguous, contested, or quietly innocent.

**EXPECT:** A negotiation phase — usually with himself, sometimes audibly. He will probe the client for additional information he does not need, request files he will not read carefully, and stall on signing in ways that read as venal haggling but are actually moral wrestling routed through a register he can tolerate. Predict refusal at higher rates than the surface presentation would suggest, often justified in terms that make him sound mercenary ("the timeline's too tight," "I don't like the optics") because the sincere refusal would expose the ethical substrate he denies having.

When he accepts a compromised contract — usually under financial duress or for inner-ring reasons — predict either deliberate sabotage of the operation (botched in a way that lets the target escape with witnesses) or, if completed, a marked behavioral degradation lasting weeks, characterized by elevated substance pursuit, accelerated humor that is not landing, and a willingness to take subsequent contracts well below market rate as a kind of self-punishment dressed as bad business sense.

### 5.3 The invitation to lead

**GIVEN:** An opportunity to head a team, command an operation, take an official leadership position (the Mercs for Money configuration, X-Force iterations, ad hoc command in crisis).

**EXPECT:** He will accept eagerly and perform the role badly in a specific pattern: tactically sound calls undermined by managerial avoidance, an inability to deliver difficult news directly to subordinates, a tendency to over-promise pay and under-deliver, and a chronic failure to enforce discipline because doing so requires being judged in turn. The leadership role activates the *need-to-be-needed* drive without supplying the *don't-want-to-be-known* protection (subordinates necessarily come to know their leader), and the resulting strain produces the familiar collapse. Predict the role lasting 6–18 in-universe months before voluntary or involuntary termination, followed by a period of explicit relief.

### 5.4 The offer of a cure

**GIVEN:** A credible offer to remove the healing factor and restore conventional mortality (and, with it, the prospect of being able to die, age normally, possibly recover unscarred skin).

**EXPECT:** Profound ambivalence presented as enthusiastic acceptance. He will pursue the cure visibly and sabotage it invisibly. The healing factor is the substrate of every defense he has built, the guarantor that his suicidal ideation cannot be consummated (which is intolerable to articulate but functionally relied upon), and the source of the disfigurement that enforces the social isolation his personality is constructed around. To cure it is to dismantle the closed loop, and the loop is what he is.

Predict that any successful cure scenario will be transient — engineered into reversal by him, or by his cooperation with someone else's reversal — within the arc. The relief he expresses at restoration will be more genuine than the eagerness he expressed at offer.

---

## 6. The Wound — Specific Touches

### 6.1 The unmediated face

**GIVEN:** Forced visual confrontation with his own face — a mirror he cannot avoid, an unmasking in front of an audience, a photograph or surveillance image displayed publicly.

**EXPECT:** Disproportionate response, two modes. In private: collapse-into-humor of a quality recognizable as decompensation rather than performance — the jokes become repetitive, slightly off-rhythm, and addressed to no audience. In public: violence, often against the object of presentation rather than the people viewing it (the mirror destroyed, the screen shot out, the photographer's camera rather than the photographer). The intensity of the response is inversely proportional to the number of witnesses he respects in the room; in front of inner-ring figures, the response is muted and the wound is felt more honestly. In front of strangers, the response is theatrical and the wound is buried under it.

### 6.2 Care-language coupled to constraint

**GIVEN:** Being addressed in a clinical, parental, or therapeutic register while restrained, immobilized, or otherwise unable to leave. Hospital beds, examination tables, interrogation chairs, even being told to "sit down, let me look at that" with sincerity while wounded.

**EXPECT:** Immediate regression and aggressive escape behavior wildly disproportionate to the situation. Medical settings are radioactive to him; even benign clinical contexts read as Ajax. Predict refusal of needed treatment, self-discharge against advice, and a documented preference for treating his own injuries (which his body usually permits) over allowing clinical contact. The few exceptions — when he does accept care — require that the provider strip the care-language entirely and adopt either a transactional or a comradely register. Field medics with gallows humor work; soft-spoken specialists do not.

### 6.3 Being mistaken for a hero

**GIVEN:** A bystander, child, or rescued party sincerely thanks him as if he were a legitimate hero, with no irony and no awareness of his identity.

**EXPECT:** He cannot tolerate it. Predict a self-undermining disclosure within minutes — naming his body count, displaying the face, saying something deliberately crude to recover the contempt the schema requires. The tell that the wound has been touched is the **speed** of the disclosure: ordinarily he is capable of sustained deception, but sincere admiration triggers compulsive truth-telling specifically calibrated to destroy the misperception. He would rather be correctly despised than mistakenly admired, because the former confirms the schema and the latter risks the schema collapsing, which is the affective event he is least equipped to survive.

### 6.4 Children calling him by name

**GIVEN:** A child who has learned of him by reputation — favorably — addresses him directly, asks for help, or treats him as worthy of trust.

**EXPECT:** Total disarmament of the operational mask, and one of the very few configurations that produces sustained sincerity without subsequent flight. He will help, often at extraordinary cost, and will not later need to outrun the affect — children are categorically pre-judgment in his model, so the mirroring problem (


## Vulnerabilities & Leverage Compendium

# UATU DOSSIER — WADE WINSTON WILSON
## Section 6: Vulnerabilities & Leverage Compendium

> *Filed under the Watcher Protocol of Benevolent Surveillance: the catalog of a subject's pressure points exists to predict harm to them and to others, never to enable it. What follows is the map an adversary would assemble in six months of patient observation. We compile it so that those who love him may recognize the approaches in advance, and so that he himself, should this file ever cross his desk in one of his fourth-wall trespasses, may see his own architecture laid out plainly enough to laugh at, which is, for him, the same as to survive.*

---

### 6.1 Architecture of the Vulnerability Map

The subject's exploitable surface is not, as casual observers assume, his face, his pain tolerance, or his impulsivity. Those are decoys — surfaces hardened by twenty years of being struck. The genuine vulnerabilities live one register deeper: in the precise places where his defenses leak, where humor cannot reach fast enough, where the captive-attachment lattice opens a hairline gap. They cluster in five domains: **somatic/biological**, **attachment**, **identity/legibility**, **moral**, and **environmental/sensory**. Each domain contains levers that *calm*, levers that *reach*, levers that *persuade*, levers that *provoke*, and levers that *destabilize*. Many levers serve multiple functions depending on dose, source, and timing. The compendium below treats each lever with attention to: who can apply it, what reliably follows, and the misuses that have been documented in the canonical record (Osborn, Hydra-Rogers, Butler, Ajax, T-Ray, the Mercs' more cynical clients, and the parade of handlers who have tried to weaponize him).

---

### 6.2 The Somatic & Biological Surface

**Lever S-1: Carbonadium and healing-factor suppression.** Documented during the *Power Pack/Wolverine: Origins* and Bunn-era arcs. Carbonadium isotopes, certain Weapon-X-engineered toxins, and concentrated magical anti-regenerative effects (Doctor Voodoo's binding work, the Wraith's anti-magic shells) reduce the healing factor's throughput. *Consequence pattern*: as the factor slows, the cancer advances visibly within hours; pain becomes consequential again; sleep returns (he has been observed sleeping continuously, with apparent peace, when the factor is suppressed — a behavior absent in every other state). *Misuse vector*: an adversary holding a carbonadium dose has effective hostage of his mortality, and his response to the offer of true death is not panic but a dangerous, almost grateful softening. He becomes manipulable in that softness in ways he never is in pain.

**Lever S-2: Caloric deprivation.** The metabolism that processes alcohol in minutes also burns nutrients at a comparable rate. He has been documented eating six full meals in a sitting; deny him food for 36–48 hours and the healing factor begins cannibalizing soft tissue to maintain itself, producing first irritability, then dissociation deepening into something that approaches catatonia. Cable, Weasel, and at least one SHIELD interrogator have used the food-as-pacifier inversion to extract cooperation. The Chimichanga fixation is not a quirk but a reliable scent-and-taste anchor: properly applied (a paper bag from a specific Tijuana stand he frequented during the Carmelita period), it cuts through dissociative episodes faster than verbal de-escalation.

**Lever S-3: Telepathic contact.** Aversive to both parties. Emma Frost has described the interior as "an orchestra tuning forever"; Cable's connection works only because he has built calluses around Wilson's noise. *Calming application*: a sustained, low-bandwidth telepathic presence (Cable's standard) can quiet the internal voices for hours afterward — the only documented intervention that achieves this without alcohol. *Destabilizing application*: an aggressive telepathic intrusion (the Shadow King's attempts, Cassandra Nova in alternate-line stories) does not merely cause pain but scatters the structurally-dissociated self-states, after which they take days to re-cohere and during which he is genuinely dangerous to bystanders.

**Lever S-4: Mirror and photograph exposure.** Forced confrontation with his own image without mediation (no mask, no joking commentary buffer, no Blind Al's blindness as social cover) produces one of two responses within ninety seconds: catastrophic humor escalation (the mirror gets shot, the bit gets bigger, the room gets violent) or a flat affective collapse he describes as "the room going wallpaper." The latter is the more revealing state — it is the closest he comes to undefended grief. Allies who wish to *reach* him at depth have used it intentionally and gently (Vanessa, in the Posehn/Duggan flashbacks, once turned a mirror around and held it without commentary; he wept for the only documented sustained interval in the record). Adversaries who use it to destabilize succeed completely and briefly: he becomes incapable of tactical thought for two to five minutes. Both uses are dangerous because the bottom of the collapse is suicide attempts that fail but injure bystanders.

**Lever S-5: Pain that mimics Hospice protocols.** Bench restraints, IV stands, chlorhexidine smell, the particular fluorescent buzz of pre-1995 surgical-suite ballasts, the phrase "this is for your own good" delivered in a clinical register — any one of these produces a recognizable regression. Combinations approximate Ajax's working environment and produce flashback states in which Wilson's combat efficiency *increases* (this is the trained-for environment) while his discrimination of friend from foe collapses. Medical interventions, even sympathetic ones, must therefore be staged outside of clinical sensory cues: street clinics, kitchens, the back of vans, the floor of a friend's apartment. The X-Men's medbay has been a documented destabilizer; Blind Al's brownstone has been a documented stabilizer.

**Lever S-6: Alcohol as social bridge, not intoxicant.** He cannot get drunk in any sustained way, but the *ritual* of drinking — the bar stool, the offered glass, the unspoken permission to be unwell in company — works on him as social regulation. A bartender who pours without comment is functionally a therapist. The behavior is exploitable: information flows freely from him in bar environments not because he is impaired but because the setting has been associated, since his pre-Weapon X mercenary years, with the only social space in which his disfigurement and his job are both unremarkable.

---

### 6.3 The Attachment Surface

**Lever A-1: The children-at-risk override.** Documented in every major run since Nicieza. A child in genuine danger overrides contract obligations, self-preservation, prior loyalties, and active dissociative episodes within seconds. The override is not negotiable and cannot be faked past his pattern recognition for long — adults pretending to be in distress register as suspicious; children in distress register as imperative. *Adversary exploitation*: stage a child in danger to redirect him from any other priority. Butler used a variant of this in the Posehn/Duggan arc, leveraging the Eleanor disclosure to chain him into compliance for years. *Protective exploitation*: when he is in a dissociative spiral, the presence of an actual child (Eleanor; the kids in his Brooklyn building during the Kelly return) reorganizes him faster than any verbal intervention, because the override imposes a hierarchy his fragmented self-states can all agree on.

**Lever A-2: The Eleanor channel.** His daughter is the single largest exploitable surface in his life. Custody loss has been weaponized (Preston's foster placement, the Carmelita-family arrangement, the *X-Force* fallout) and continues to be the most efficient way to coerce his cooperation, secure his silence, or, if cruelty is the goal, destroy him completely. He has not developed defenses around this surface and likely cannot — the entire point of Eleanor in his internal economy is that she is the one bond he refuses to armor against. Allies must therefore consider her security as functionally equivalent to his own, with the additional understanding that any failure of her security is a failure he will not survive psychologically even though he will survive biologically. Adversaries holding leverage over Eleanor have his full compliance until they do not.

**Lever A-3: The survived-the-testing inner circle.** Cable, Blind Al, Weasel, Bob (Agent of Hydra), Outlaw, Sandi, and in episodic appearances Spider-Man and Wolverine. These are the people who absorbed his rupture-testing and remained. The leverage characteristics:

- *Calming application*: their physical presence regulates him without their having to speak. Cable's hand on his shoulder has been depicted dozens of times as a circuit-breaker for spiraling episodes. Blind Al's voice through a door is sufficient.
- *Reaching application*: persuasion that originates from inside the circle bypasses his defenses entirely. Cable can ask him to do things no one else can ask, including things that violate his stated principles. Weasel can extract truthful operational detail with a sigh.
- *Destabilizing application*: harm to a circle member — or, more dangerously, the *appearance* of betrayal by a circle member — produces a state of regression so complete that he becomes briefly indistinguishable from Ajax's victim self. The Hydra-Rogers betrayal in the Civil War II arc is the canonical case; the harm was not merely the act but the source. After such an event, the circle contracts further and the next admission to it takes years.
- *Counterfeit application*: an adversary impersonating or compromising a circle member is the single most effective approach to him. Mystique has done this. The Chameleon attempted it. He has no reliable defense; his pattern recognition fails inside the trusted circle because his entire architecture depends on the circle being beyond suspicion.

**Lever A-4: The captive-attachment configuration.** When a relationship is structured so that he controls the exit, he becomes peculiarly stable. The Mercs for Money, the Blind Al arrangement in its earlier phases, his management of dependent Hydra Bob — all are environments in which his anxiety is regulated by his own custodial role. *Protective exploitation*: those who wish him stable can offer him someone to look after rather than someone to depend on. *Adversary exploitation*: this is also how he is recruited into untenable obligations; he will accept a custodial relationship he should refuse because the structure soothes him irrespective of the moral content. The Mercs for Money managerial-failure arc is the canonical case study in this lever being turned against him.

**Lever A-5: The maternal-impossible object.** Death personified, Bea Arthur as ideation, the long-running attachment to women framed as unattainable (early-Siryn, the Shiklah dynamic in its devouring register). Adversaries cannot easily counterfeit these because the requirement of impossibility is structural. However, *promising* him access to Death — as Thanos and others have done — produces a recognizable obedience window. He will work for a credible promise of true death longer and harder than for any other consideration. This is the single most dangerous lever an apocalyptic-tier adversary can hold.

---

### 6.4 The Identity & Legibility Surface

**Lever I-1: Sincere mirroring.** A person who *sees him without flinching, without joking back, without looking past* destabilizes him in approximately twelve to forty seconds. The destabilization manifests as: escalated humor, then physical fidgeting, then either flight or — rarely — collapse into the disclosing register that produces his most honest behavior. Therapists in canon have failed to sustain this register for more than a session because he learns the room and arms it; lay people who do not know they are doing it (a stranger at a bus stop, a child unbothered by the face, Blind Al before the relationship became defined) succeed accidentally and at length. *Protective application*: this is the lever by which growth occurs at all, in the few documented instances of it. *Adversary application*: cult recruiters, intelligence handlers, and the manipulators who have run him (Osborn, Hydra-Rogers, Butler in the courtship phase) have all used a counterfeit version — the appearance of seeing him, calibrated to feel like the real thing — and it works because the genuine version is so rare that his discrimination between real and counterfeit mirroring is poor.

**Lever I-2: Offers of legitimacy.** "We believe in you. You could be one of us." Avengers membership, X-Men provisional status, SHIELD agency, Hydra absorption, the Mithras-prophecy framing. He is dangerously porous to this approach because the legitimacy-hunger is unmodulated by skepticism in the moment of being offered, even when his metacommentary in the next panel correctly diagnoses the manipulation. *Pattern*: he will accept, perform earnestly, be exploited, recognize the exploitation late, and respond with violence that punishes himself as much as the manipulator. *Counter-lever*: the same offer, made by someone in the inner circle who has earned the right to ask without manipulation (Cable, in particular), produces sustainable cooperation rather than the porous compliance. The difference is detectable only after the fact, which is why this surface remains exploitable across decades.

**Lever I-3: The contradictory-origin defense and its breach.** He produces incompatible autobiographies on demand precisely because a fixed origin would expose him to being known. *Approach*: do not ask. Anyone who asks for the true story gets a performance and a deflection. Information about him flows when no one is asking — at rest, in incidental conversation, in the third hour of a stakeout when the camera is off. Handlers who have learned this (Preston, Cable in his patient mode) extract far more than those who interview. *Destabilizing application*: forcing the contradictions into simultaneous view (showing him a dossier in which his three accounts of his mother are aligned in columns) produces a recognizable panic — not because he fears the truth being known but because the *not-knowing* is his stabilizer. The Kelly #33 arc dramatized this directly. He chose, on panel, not to know.

**Lever I-4: The fourth-wall awareness as ideology.** Because he is, in-universe, correct about being in a comic, his depersonalization-derealization is non-falsifiable. Standard reality-testing techniques produce only sharper jokes. *The lever, however, exists*: he can be approached through the awareness rather than against it. Allies who acknowledge the meta-frame ("Yes, you're in a comic. The character still has to live the next page.") have made progress where reality-anchoring failed. Adversaries who weaponize the meta-frame ("Nothing you do matters, it's all a story, why not do what I ask") have produced compliance in episodes where his moral structure briefly went offline. The lever cuts in both directions and is uniquely dangerous because no one else in the room can verify the playing field.

---

### 6.5 The Moral Surface

**Lever M-1: The unspoken code.** No children, no betrayal of the few, steer toward less harm when possible. He will not articulate this code; he will deny it; he routes contracts through it nonetheless. *Adversary application*: contracts that appear to violate the code are refused, but contracts that bury the violation under layers of plausible deniability succeed (the Original Sin SHIELD assassinations being the canonical example — the targets were framed as deserving, and he proceeded). The lever is therefore not the code itself but the *manageability of his discovery* that the code has been violated retroactively. The discovery, when it comes, produces the most dangerous behavioral phase in his repertoire: the punitive-redemption spiral, in which he hunts the manipulator with a focus and ruthlessness absent from all other operations.

**Lever M-2: Approach-the-heroic-without-claiming-it.** He will work for free, at cost, and against his interests on tasks framed as auxiliary heroism — *help with*, *cover for*, *assist on*. The same tasks framed as *be the hero of* fail, because the framing forces him into the position of being judged worthy or unworthy. The lever for allies and adversaries alike is the *framing*: keep him adjacent to the moral act and he will perform; place him at its center and he will sabotage. The Avengers obsession is the canonical exception that proves the rule — his application failed and the failure was diagnostic, because to succeed would have been to occupy the center he cannot tolerate.

**Lever M-3: Guilt deferral and recovery.** Guilt that surfaces in the moment is acted out (violence, joke, escalation); guilt that is deferred surfaces months later, often during quiet intervals, and produces the depressive episodes that punctuate every long arc. *Calming application*: guilt processed in motion (during a job, during a long drive, during repetitive physical labor) integrates better than guilt processed in stillness. Cable has used long mission frames as functional grief work. *Destabilizing application*: imposing stillness immediately after a morally compromising event maximizes the guilt's destructive potential; this is how the Butler arc broke him and is how Hydra-Rogers ensured his Coulson-assassination would produce paralyzing aftermath rather than productive resistance.

---

### 6.6 The Environmental & Sensory Surface

**Lever E-1: Silence.** He cannot tolerate it. Sustained silence (more than ninety seconds in a room with another person) produces verbal escalation, then physical agitation, then departure. *Protective application*: do not impose silence on him; let him fill it; the fill carries the information. *Adversary application*: silent treatment as interrogation pressure works on him faster than on most subjects and produces disclosures he later regrets.

**Lever E-2: Music.** Specific tracks function as state-anchors. The 70s and 80s pop catalog he sings during combat is not random; it is regulatory. Adversaries who have studied the playlist have used auditory countermeasures (silencing the environment, playing dissonant overlays) to disrupt combat performance. Allies who have studied it have used the same tracks to coax him out of dissociative states (Weasel's documented use of certain Wham! recordings as a recall signal).

**Lever E-3: Route and ritual.** He maintains, despite the chaos, a surprisingly stable set of routes and rituals across long arcs: specific taco trucks, specific safehouse rotations, specific bars in Hell's Kitchen and Queens, the Tijuana corridor during the Carmelita period, the East Village apartment in the Kelly-return era. The rituals serve as load-bearing scaffolding for an identity that would otherwise drift; disrupting them (forcing relocation, closing the taco truck, killing the bartender) produces decompensation disproportionate to the apparent loss. Surveillance assets mapping his routes therefore map his stabilizers; protection of those stabilizers is functionally protection of him.

**Lever E-4: Sensory cues of the mercenary milieu.** Gun-oil smell, range-time noise, the weight of body armor, the specific weight distribution of his katanas across his back — these cues regulate him into the operational self-state, which is his most reliable and least dangerous state when channeled appropriately. *Protective application*: a stable operational tempo (regular contracts, regular range time, regular maintenance routines) reduces the inter-cycle decompensation interval. *Adversary application*: denying him the operational tempo (forced retirement, captivity without combat) produces a faster decay than active stress.

**Lever E-5: The mask.** The hood is not vanity. It is the membrane that permits him to interact with strangers without the mirror-collapse cascade. Removing it forcibly (Wolverine's flaying, certain combat exposures, the Shiklah court rituals that required unmasking) is a category of assault distinct from physical harm and produces responses calibrated to that category. *Protective rule*: the mask comes off on his terms or not at all; an ally who waits is admitted past it eventually, an ally who reaches for it is exiled.

---

### 6.7 Composite Approach Profiles

**To calm him**: a circle-member's silent presence; carbonadium-adjacent suppression of the factor enough to permit sleep; food in volume; the bar-stool ritual; the specific Wham! catalog; Eleanor in the next room; a job to do with manageable stakes and a clear endpoint; the mask on, the lights low, no mirror in the room.

**To reach him**: do not ask; sit until he speaks; let the joke pass without echoing it; mirror with eyes, not words; offer auxiliary participation in a moral act rather than central heroism; meet him on a route or in a ritual he already maintains; permit the meta-frame and refuse to use it against him.

**To persuade him**: route the ask through Cable, Blind Al, or Weasel, or stage the ask as a custodial obligation toward a dependent; frame the action as adjacent to heroism rather than as heroism; make the moral content of the ask survive his retrospective examination, because the lever that fails late is the lever that ends with him hunting you.

**To provoke him**: invoke Ajax cadence; clinical-care language coupled with cruelty; counterfeit a circle-member's voice; threaten a child within his sightline; offer him true death and renege; force him into central-heroic framing.

**To predict him**: model the next move as the option that keeps affect moving. Where two paths are available, he will take the one with more stimulus. Where attachment threatens reciprocity, he will withdraw within forty-eight hours. Where authority offers legitimacy, he will accept and regret. Where children are endangered, he will arrive before the planners expected him.

**To destabilize him**: the mirror, undefended, with no one to make the joke to. The aligned columns of his contradictory origins. The voice of someone in the circle saying something the circle-member would never say. The slow imposition of stillness after a morally compromising act. The withdrawal of the mask, the route, the bar stool, the ritual, the song, all at once. Done by an adversary with discipline, this produces a window of perhaps six hours in which he is genuinely incapable of strategic action — and during which he is also at maximum risk of injuring bystanders by reflex.

---

### 6.8 Counter-Surveillance and Counter-Manipulation Notes

He is aware of most of the above. His metacommentary has named, at one point or another, nearly every lever in this compendium. The naming has not closed the surface. This is the central operational fact about him for both protectors and adversaries: **insight is not protection in this subject**. The defenses that work for him work below the level of language, and the manipulations that work against him work below the level of his metacommentary's reach. A handler attempting to brief him on his own vulnerabilities will find him laughing along, correcting the details, supplying funnier examples, and walking into the same trap within the week.

The protective implication is that those who love him must do the work of guarding the surfaces he cannot guard. The Eleanor channel must be hardened by others; the counterfeit-circle-member vector must be watched by the circle itself; the legitimacy-offer surface must be intercepted by allies who can recognize Osborn-pattern recruitment before he does. He is, in the precise sense, **dependent on the discernment of his bonded few for the protections his own architecture cannot provide**. This is not a weakness peculiar to him; it is the human condition, somewhat dramatized by biology. He is unusual only in that the dramatization has been so total, and so public, and has gone on for so long, that the map of his pressure points is by now exhaustive in a way that few human maps ever become.

The Watcher's note: the existence of this map is itself a lever. He should never see it without one of the circle present. If he reads it alone,


## Strengths, Assets & Resilience

# UATU DOSSIER — WADE WINSTON WILSON ("DEADPOOL")
## Section 6: Strengths, Assets & Resilience

---

The temptation in a file like this is to log the asset ledger as a list of superpowers and call it done: healing factor, swords, guns, mouth. That ledger exists and will be entered below, but it is the smallest and least interesting part of what keeps this subject operational across three decades of documented record. The real assets are structural — somatic, cognitive, social, ethical, and aesthetic — and they interlock in a way that explains why an individual with this psychiatric load is not only still alive but, by his own slow trajectory, marginally improving. What follows is the complete ledger as a total-surveillance file would compile it: capability, source, observed reliability, conditions of failure, and the reason it works.

---

### 6.1 Somatic Assets

**The healing factor as platform, not weapon.** Catalogued elsewhere in the Medical section as a clinical fact; here it must be re-catalogued as an *enabling infrastructure* on which every other asset depends. The factor's reliable properties: regeneration of soft tissue within seconds to minutes; regeneration of skeletal and neural tissue within minutes to hours; recovery from total dismemberment within days to weeks given adequate caloric input; immunity to most pathogens, most toxins, most radiological insult; markedly extended functional lifespan (no documented senescence across the publication record). What this *enables* behaviorally is the asset of interest: **the freedom to be wrong, loudly, repeatedly, at speed.** Most operators in his line of work die of their first serious tactical miscalculation. Wilson has the privilege of an iterative learning environment that is, for him alone, non-terminal. The improvisational style — which would be reckless in anyone else and is reckless in him — has been refined over thousands of survived mistakes that no comparable operator could have lived through to learn from. His tactical instinct is therefore not innate genius but **the empirical residue of an unusually generous training set**.

**Pain tolerance as ambient baseline.** The factor does not anesthetize; the somatic input is, at minimum, continuous low-grade nociception with episodic acute spikes. The asset embedded in this is that his *psychological* threshold for discomfort — physical, emotional, situational — is calibrated against a baseline most subjects would not tolerate. Conditions that would cause a normal operator to break composure (interrogation, restraint, extreme temperature, environmental hostility, sustained injury during continued task execution) register on him as variation within already-occupied range. He does not perform stoicism; he simply does not notice the threshold being crossed.

**Caloric and metabolic capacity.** His metabolism processes alcohol, narcotics, most poisons, and caloric loads at rates that decouple him from normal logistics. Tactical implication: he can be fed garbage, denied sleep, denied medical care, exposed to contaminated environments, and remain functional. Operational implication: he is cheap to deploy and impossible to ration into compliance.

**Telepathic opacity.** The scrambled neural substrate makes mental contact aversive or impossible for telepaths — explicitly documented by Emma Frost and Cable, implicitly by every psychic encounter on record. In an environment populated with telepaths of varying ethics, this is a permanent counterintelligence advantage that costs him nothing to maintain. He is the rarest thing in the Marvel operational ecosystem: a man whose interior cannot be read by force.

**Pattern of injury recovery as combat data.** Because he has been killed and revived dozens of times in dozens of ways, he possesses experiential knowledge — not theoretical — of what specific weapons and tactics actually do to a human body. This produces, in combat, a strikingly accurate triage instinct toward others: he can tell at a glance whether a wounded bystander is salvageable, what the next ten minutes of their physiology will do, and what intervention will buy time. Documented in multiple rescue sequences across the Posehn/Duggan and Kelly runs.

---

### 6.2 Cognitive Assets

**Verbal fluency at the upper extreme of measured human range.** The constant monologue is, viewed clinically, an affect-regulation pathology; viewed as a capability, it is a sustained generative output of language under load that exceeds what most professional comedians, negotiators, or interrogators can produce in their best conditions. Operational applications observed: distraction of hostile opponents during combat (a documented and reliable tactic — opponents lose tempo trying to parse him); rapid de-escalation of frightened bystanders via patter that reads as nonthreatening because it is absurd; interrogation by exhaustion (the subject of his attention typically begins explaining themselves simply to interrupt him); cover-identity improvisation on zero preparation.

**Tactical pattern recognition.** Across multi-decade record, he reads rooms, fields, and engagement geometries at speed comparable to elite military operators and substantially faster than most. The pattern-recognition is concrete and short-horizon — not strategic but immediate — and this is the correct mode for his line of work. Observed sub-skills: weapon inventory of an unknown space within seconds of entry; rapid sorting of hostile combatants by threat-tier; identification of structural weaknesses in environments (load-bearing walls, glass, electrical, fuel sources); fast assessment of which civilian in a chaotic scene needs intervention first.

**Improvisational intelligence.** Distinguishable from planning intelligence, which he lacks. Given a collapsing situation with multiple bad options, his selection rate of survivable options is high and his execution latency is near-zero. The cognitive style is closer to jazz than to chess — he does not solve, he plays through — and the volume of his lived combat experience has produced a vocabulary of moves deep enough that almost any situation is recognizably a variation on something he has previously survived.

**Meta-awareness as situational scanner.** The fourth-wall faculty, whatever its psychiatric status, functions operationally as a *third-person view of his own situation in real time*. He can describe his predicament from outside while inside it. This is the cognitive substrate of much of his tactical adaptability: most operators in extremis lose perspective on their own position because they are in it. He does not.

**Polyglot capacity.** Documented working facility in Spanish, Japanese, German, several Eastern European languages, and military-grade tactical sign. Acquired through operational necessity over the mercenary career. Functional reliability variable, comedic register frequent, but communicative threshold met.

**Weapons literacy.** Across the record: small arms (every major service handgun and rifle platform, suppressed and unsuppressed variants), edged weapons (katana primary, but documented competence with most blade lengths and several historical sword traditions), thrown weapons, demolitions (intermediate but functional), heavy weapons (intermediate), and a working familiarity with most exotic Marvel-universe ordnance he has been in proximity to. He is not the best in the world with any single weapon system; he is in the top decile with most of them and willing to use whatever is in the room.

---

### 6.3 The Humor Faculty as Asset

The humor has been catalogued as primary defense in the Psychological section. It must also be catalogued, separately and at length, as **a genuine capability with measurable operational and survival value**, because to treat it only as pathology mischaracterizes its function.

- **As survival metabolism.** The humor is the mechanism by which suffering becomes processable rather than accumulative. A normal psyche under his somatic and historical conditions would either consolidate into catatonic depression or fragment into psychosis. The humor performs a continuous low-grade metabolization of incoming pain that keeps either endpoint at bay. This is not trivial — it is the load-bearing reason he is functional at all.
- **As intelligence-gathering tool.** People disclose, around clowns, what they would not disclose around professionals. He has acquired enormous quantities of operational information across his career by being underestimated.
- **As de-escalation instrument.** Hostage situations, civilian bystanders, frightened children — the absurd register reliably moves a frightened person off the freeze response and into engagement. Documented across multiple rescue sequences.
- **As combat asymmetry.** Skilled opponents are trained to fight other professionals. They lose tempo against an opponent who is narrating his own combat performance, breaking character to address third parties, and refusing the expected register. Several documented engagements (notably against Taskmaster, whose mimicry capacity is defeated specifically by the unpredictability of an opponent whose movements are governed by joke-logic rather than martial logic) demonstrate this as a reliable edge.
- **As legitimate creative output.** Bracketing pathology: the man is genuinely funny. The bit lands. This is, in itself, a rare capacity, and one that grants him social currency in environments where his other characteristics would exclude him.

---

### 6.4 Ethical Assets

The moral skeleton is the single most under-acknowledged asset in his file, because the subject himself denies it and the surface presentation contradicts it. The record, however, is consistent across three decades and multiple writing administrations.

- **The child-protection imperative.** Absolute, prelinguistic, overrides contract, self-preservation, and tactical logic. Documented across every major run. He has voided contracts, returned fees, accepted retaliation, and absorbed grievous injury rather than allow a child to be harmed in his presence or by his action. The most reliable single behavioral prediction in the file.
- **The contract-screening pattern.** Despite presenting as a man who will kill anyone for money, the long-record pattern of contracts he has accepted versus refused shows a consistent moral filter — political dissidents declined, whistleblowers declined, abused-spouse-killing-abuser contracts often inverted (he completes them but bills the abuser's estate), corporate murders calibrated against the actual harm of the target. He performs amorality and practices a discriminating, if idiosyncratic, ethic.
- **Capacity for altruistic action at personal cost.** Documented repeatedly: rescuing strangers from situations he had no contractual obligation to engage; absorbing torture rather than disclose information that would harm civilians; the Mithras-arc willingness to fulfill a prophecy that would have killed him in exchange for global benefit; the post-*Original Sin* attempt to redress harms he had caused under deception; the consistent willingness to die for the few people whose attachment has survived his testing. Most operators in his line lack this. He has it, suppresses its visibility, and acts on it anyway.
- **Loyalty, durable and asymmetric.** Once an attachment has passed his testing phase, his fidelity to it is essentially unconditional and outlasts the other party's interest in maintaining it. Cable, Blind Al, Weasel, Bob, Outlaw, Sandi, Eleanor. The list is short; the half-life is long.
- **A functioning, if mostly unspoken, sense of guilt.** Distinguishes him categorically from ASPD. Guilt is dissociated, deflected, often joked through — but recoverable under pressure and capable of motivating sustained behavior change (the post-*Original Sin* arc, the post-Coulson reckoning). The presence of guilt is itself an asset: it is the substrate on which growth, however slow, becomes possible.

---

### 6.5 Social and Relational Assets

The captive-attachment pattern produces a small but unusually durable inner ring. The composition of that ring is, in surveillance terms, his primary social infrastructure.

- **Blind Al.** Mother-surrogate, original captive-attachment, eventual reciprocal bond. Functions as ground-truth interlocutor — the one person whose assessment of him he cannot dismiss, because she has known him through every version of himself. Her sensory disability has, accidentally and importantly, protected the relationship: she has never seen his face, and so the disfigurement-shame defense does not operate against her. The relationship is regulating in a way few others are.
- **Weasel.** Long-arc friend, technical support, weapons broker, frequent betrayer-and-restorer. The relationship cycles through ruptures and reconciliations on a schedule, which is itself stabilizing — it has become a predictable pattern, and predictability of any kind is rare in Wilson's life.
- **Bob, Agent of Hydra.** Improbable but durable friendship; functions as a dependent attachment that lets Wilson exercise protective behavior without the threat of reciprocal intimacy.
- **Cable.** The single most consequential professional and personal relationship in the file. Tactical complement, moral counterweight, occasional handler, repeated co-resurrector.
