The asymmetry — Cable's stability against Wilson's chaos — produces a regulatory dynamic that benefits Wilson disproportionately. He behaves better around Cable than around anyone else.
- **Outlaw and Sandi.** Documented during the Simone run as a non-threatening female social unit that demonstrably stabilized his affect. The relationship's value is partly that nothing romantic is required of him; the absence of sexual stakes lets the attachment function cleanly.
- **Eleanor.** The asset and the wound. Her existence has produced sustained behavioral change in the direction of stability — even after custody loss, the fact of her keeps a future-orientation alive in him that was absent before her introduction.
- **Vanessa.** Variable across versions; canonically the relationship that proved he can love. Even where the relationship is not currently active, the historical fact of it functions as an internal proof-of-concept.

Beyond the inner ring, his reputation across the broader operator community is a paradoxical asset: he is widely regarded as unreliable, dangerous, and embarrassing, *and* widely sought as a contractor for jobs that require somebody who will not die and will not stop. The disreputability is itself a market position.

---

### 6.6 Material and Operational Assets

- **Safehouse network.** Distributed across multiple continents; varying quality from genuine secure facilities to disreputable apartments held under cover identities. Adequacy of any individual location is low; redundancy is high.
- **Weapons cache infrastructure.** Maintained at multiple locations; armory at primary residence routinely catalogued at "more than one man can use, less than he has." Procurement channels established with Weasel and several less-named brokers.
- **Cover identity portfolio.** Dozens of working aliases with varying documentation depth. Most are thin; a few have decades of paper.
- **Capital.** Variable. The mercenary income is substantial when actively working; the spending pattern is impulsive, generous to dependents, and resistant to accumulation. He is rarely rich and almost never broke for long.
- **Equipment specific to the body.** Custom tailoring (the suit accommodates regeneration patterns and conceals the dermatological condition simultaneously — a non-trivial garment engineering problem). Hardware compatible with extreme physical abuse. Pouches, the contents of which vary; he is willing to carry the absurd object that turns out to be the one needed.

---

### 6.7 Resilience Factors, Properly Named

The standard psychiatric resilience literature identifies a set of factors that protect against the long-term sequelae of severe trauma. The unusual feature of Wilson's case is that he possesses most of them, in idiosyncratic and partially pathological form, and this is the reason the picture is not worse than it is.

- **Cognitive flexibility.** Extreme. He reframes continuously. The reframing is often defensive rather than integrative, but the underlying faculty is intact and powerful.
- **Sense of humor.** Extreme. See 6.3.
- **Locus of control.** Internal, paradoxically, despite extensive evidence that he is acted upon by forces beyond him. He behaves as if his choices matter, and this is functionally protective regardless of its philosophical accuracy.
- **Meaning-making capacity.** Present and active. The mercenary code, the child-protection imperative, the attachments — these are not articulated as meaning, but they function as such.
- **Social support.** Small inner ring, but real and durable. Meets the threshold the literature identifies as protective; the literature does not require many, only some.
- **Self-efficacy in the operational domain.** Total. Whatever he doubts about himself, he does not doubt his capacity to handle the next combat situation. This is grounded in accurate assessment of his actual capabilities and is therefore non-pathological.
- **Acceptance of what cannot be changed.** Achieved, with the assistance of an aesthetic register (the absurd, the cosmic joke) that allows him to hold the unchangeable without consolidating into despair. Functionally Stoic via the route of comedy rather than philosophy.
- **Capacity to ask for help.** Limited but non-zero. He has, across record, asked Cable, Blind Al, and Weasel for help in extremis. The fact that the threshold is high makes the asking diagnostic — when he asks, he means it.

---

### 6.8 Aesthetic and Existential Assets

These are the assets that the file would miss if it were compiled by an apparatus that recognized only capabilities. They are nevertheless load-bearing.

- **An operational philosophy of the absurd.** He has independently arrived at a worldview in which meaning is local, suffering is structural, and the appropriate response is to perform care for the few while declining to take the universe seriously. This is, in philosophical terms, a defensible position, and the fact that he holds it as praxis rather than as theory is part of why it works on him.
- **Aesthetic pleasure in the work.** He enjoys craft. The well-executed shot, the well-timed joke, the choreographically satisfying combat sequence — these give him pleasure, and pleasure of any kind is an asset for someone whose hedonic baseline is otherwise compromised.
- **Pleasure in food.** The metabolic capacity has not extinguished the appetite. Documented preferences (chimichangas, pancakes, low-grade comfort food in large quantity) are a small daily source of reliable positive affect.
- **Pleasure in popular culture.** Sincere, not ironic. The film references, the music, the television — these are not only deflection. He genuinely enjoys these things and they constitute a small but reliable mood-regulation resource.
- **The capacity for awe.** Less frequently observed but documented — in cosmic encounters, in the presence of his daughter, in occasional moments of stillness with attachment figures. He can be moved. The faculty is intact and the door is not welded shut.

---

### 6.9 What Makes the Asset Ledger Durable

The unifying feature of Wilson's resilience profile is that **every asset has been stress-tested past the point at which most assets fail**. The humor has been tested against atrocities that would silence anyone else, and it continues to fire. The loyalty has been tested by the kinds of betrayal that normally end loyalty, and it persists. The ethical core has been tested by deception (Osborn, Hydra-Rogers, SHIELD) at scales that have broken better-organized moral structures, and after each break, the core reasserts. The social ring has been tested by his own active sabotage for decades, and the survivors of that testing are still in place.

This is the central counterintuitive finding of the asset section: the same disorganization that produces the psychopathology is also the source of the resilience's robustness. He has not built a fragile structure of healthy supports; he has built a structure designed to absorb continuous damage and continue functioning at degraded capacity indefinitely. It is not a healthy architecture. It is a *survivable* one — which is the engineering specification his life required.

The biology that denies him the natural endpoint of his condition also denies him the natural collapse that would let the structure be rebuilt cleanly. So the structure is what it is, and it works. It has worked for three decades of record. It will, on the trajectory observable, continue to work — and continue, very slowly and very unevenly, to accrete additional supports at its edges. The asset ledger is not impressive in the way a healthier person's would be. It is impressive in the way a structure under continuous load is impressive when it has not yet failed and shows no near-term sign of doing so.

He is, in the most precise sense available to this file, **resilient by necessity, by design, and by demonstrated record** — and the file should treat that resilience as the primary fact about him, of which the pathology is the cost rather than the essence.


## Failure Modes & Decompensation

# UATU ANALYSIS FILE: WADE WINSTON WILSON ("DEADPOOL")
## Section 6 — Failure Modes & Decompensation

---

### 6.0 Framing: What "Breaking" Means for This Subject

For an ordinary personality, decompensation has a terminus — psychotic break, catatonic withdrawal, suicide, dissociative fugue resolving into amnesia, somatic collapse. Each of these is a system shutting itself off to preserve what remains. The subject possesses none of these exits. His healing factor forecloses suicide and somatic collapse; his organic neural noise renders him telepathically and pharmacologically refractory, foreclosing imposed sedation; his identity is already so diffuse that fugue produces no meaningful displacement (there is no coherent self to flee from); his reality testing, paradoxically, is reinforced rather than degraded by his metafictional awareness, because in-universe the metafiction is correct.

What this means operationally: **the subject cannot break in the normal sense, because breaking requires an off-state his biology will not permit**. What he does instead is *cycle through* the decompensation sequence — sometimes in compressed form over hours, sometimes drawn out across arcs spanning months of narrative time — without the terminating collapse that would, in a normal patient, force reconstitution. The clinical literature on CPTSD describes such patients as "held at the moment of breaking"; in Wilson's case this is literal and ongoing rather than metaphorical and intermittent.

The failure mode is therefore not a single event but a **looping trajectory**. The dossier maps it in stages, with the understanding that the loop can be entered at any point, can be exited at any point if a stabilizing attachment intervenes, and is, in the absence of intervention, self-perpetuating.

---

### 6.1 The Escalation Path — Stage by Stage

#### Stage 1: Baseline Saturation (operational state)

The subject's "well" state is already elevated relative to normal-personality baseline. Continuous verbal output, near-continuous low-grade humor, near-continuous low-grade pain, a stimulant-equivalent metabolism that processes a bottle of mid-shelf whiskey in roughly the time a normal liver processes a single drink. The boxes are present but synchronized — the impulsive voice and the observational voice operate as a two-channel tactical commentary; the moralistic voice is muted but available.

Behavioral tells of baseline:

- Job acceptance through normal broker channels (Weasel, prior to the various ruptures; Patch, the Bar With No Name dispatch when accessible).
- Eating in front of others (the unmasking-to-eat ritual performed with calibrated showmanship: turning, lifting the lower edge, never the whole mask, signaling that the disfigurement is on his terms).
- Lodging stable for periods of 2–8 weeks at a time before relocation.
- Sleep patterns: erratic but recoverable, typically 3–5 hours, frequently broken; reads or watches television in the waking intervals rather than dwelling.
- Contact with retained-attachment figures (Cable, Bob, Weasel, Blind Al where extant, Eleanor where access permitted) at intervals of weeks to months — initiated by him, brief, and rarely the stated purpose of his call.

#### Stage 2: Trigger Ingestion

A trigger event is registered. The taxonomy of triggers, in approximate order of potency:

1. **Threat to a child within field of view or contractual proximity.**
2. **Discovery of betrayal by an authority figure he had begun to trust** (the load-bearing example: the *Original Sin* revelation re: Rogers; the secondary example: Osborn during Dark Reign once the manipulation became visible to him).
3. **Loss or estrangement of an attachment figure** (Vanessa's departures and deaths across continuities; Eleanor's removal; the Butler arc's cumulative family loss; Shiklah's turn to enmity).
4. **Forced sincere mirroring** — someone refusing to flinch, refusing to laugh at the bit, holding eye contact through the deflection.
5. **Re-encounter with Ajax-coded stimulus** — a sadistic clinician, an interrogator who jokes mid-torture, a smell or sound from the Hospice that the regenerating CNS has retained despite continuous neural turnover (the somatic memory survives the tissue that should have stored it; this is a recurring narrative beat).
6. **Forced exposure to his own unmasked image** in a non-controlled context — a mirror he wasn't expecting, a photograph circulated, a child's recoiling face.
7. **Sustained sobriety / sustained stillness** — long convalescent intervals, forced confinement without combat or task, isolation without media.

The first sign of trigger ingestion is **a microsecond gap in the patter**. Wilson's verbal output is so reliable that the absence of a quip in a beat that would normally produce one is the highest-confidence early indicator. Handlers reading transcripts should mark silences before they mark words.

#### Stage 3: Compensatory Acceleration

The defenses ramp. Specific behavioral markers, observable in the field within 30–120 minutes of trigger ingestion:

- **Verbal output increases in volume and decreases in coherence.** Jokes start landing on himself rather than the situation; pop-culture references multiply; fourth-wall asides intensify in frequency (from one or two per encounter to near-continuous).
- **The boxes desynchronize.** The observational voice (analytical, dryer, often punctuating combat with situational read) and the impulsive voice (id, aggression, appetite) cease to take turns and begin to talk over each other. The moralistic voice goes silent first — this is diagnostic. When the conscience-channel drops out of the internal conversation, the next 24–72 hours will contain actions he will later need to dissociate from.
- **Tactical efficiency degrades in favor of spectacle.** A target who could have been resolved with two rounds is resolved with a katana, a grenade, a one-liner, and an unnecessary aerial maneuver. The combat becomes the regulator rather than the threat.
- **Consumption escalates.** Caloric intake roughly doubles. Alcohol consumption rises into the punitive range (intake calibrated to overwhelm metabolism for as long as biologically possible — typically 15–40 minutes of perceptible intoxication purchased at the cost of two to four liters of high-proof). Recreational drug experimentation resumes despite its established futility.
- **Sleep collapses.** From 3–5 broken hours to 0–2. Television runs continuously. The apartment (or motel room, or safehouse) accumulates take-out containers in an outwardly visible spiral, plates near the door, refuse trailing toward the bed or couch — a recognizable depressive-clutter signature inverted by the manic verbal layer.
- **Sexual behavior, where available, becomes more compulsive and less discriminating.** Where unavailable, masturbation becomes scheduled-feeling and joyless, often during television.
- **Contact with attachment figures spikes and then ceases.** First a flurry — calls, voicemails, texts that read as jokes but parse as bids for contact — then, when reciprocity is offered, a 48–96 hour silence. This biphasic pattern is the single most reliable behavioral indicator that the loop is in motion.

#### Stage 4: Acting Out / Discharge

If no stabilizing attachment intervenes within roughly 72 hours of Stage 3 onset, the system discharges. The form of discharge varies by trigger class but the structure is consistent: **a behavioral act of sufficient magnitude to overwrite the affect with consequences**.

- *Trigger class 1 (children)*: violent overcorrection. Contract abandonment, freelance intervention, killing of the threatening party in a manner explicitly intended to be witnessed (a message-killing; bodies arranged, signage, a corpse left for whoever was responsible to find). The Butler arc and the recurring child-trafficking interventions across the Posehn/Duggan and later runs follow this template. Wilson reads as competent here, even heroic; the cost is paid later in Stage 5.
- *Trigger class 2 (authority betrayal)*: a sustained, dissociative-fugue-equivalent campaign of either revenge or self-punishment, often both. The post-*Original Sin* arc against the SHIELD targets he had been used against; the post-Civil War II self-isolation following the Coulson killing.
- *Trigger class 3 (attachment loss)*: geographic flight. Contracts taken in distant theaters, ideally with linguistic and cultural friction sufficient to drown the internal monologue under translation work. Travel chosen for difficulty of reach rather than profitability.
- *Trigger class 4 (forced mirroring)*: rupture engineered. The relationship is sabotaged with the specific intent of restoring the predictable architecture of rejection. Frequently this is performed via a single calculated act of cruelty designed to be unforgivable, so that the relationship cannot be reopened by the other party's compassion.
- *Trigger class 5 (Ajax-coded)*: regression to Hospice-era behavior. Speech patterns shift toward the gallows-humor cadence specific to that period (faster, flatter, more rhyming, more sing-song). Killing methodology shifts toward replication of injuries Ajax inflicted on him.
- *Trigger class 6 (own face)*: immediate physical violence against the offending object (smashed mirror, destroyed phone, attack on the witnessing party calibrated short of lethal where possible but not always). Where the witness is a child or an attachment figure, the violence is redirected onto the self — repeated self-injury, often to the face, often with a clear performative quality even when no witness remains.
- *Trigger class 7 (stillness/sobriety)*: manufactured crisis. Contracts accepted that he would otherwise refuse, fights provoked in venues likely to contain capable retaliators, deliberate violation of the operational protocols of more dangerous parties (the recurring beats with Wolverine, the Hulk, Cable, Bullseye where Wilson initiates an engagement under no instrumental necessity).

#### Stage 5: Post-Discharge Collapse

This is the closest he comes to a normal decompensation, and it is the stage handlers are most likely to misread as "improvement," because the verbal layer thins out and the surface goes quiet.

Markers:

- **Reduced verbal output.** Hours and sometimes days of near-silence. The mask stays on. The boxes go quiet too — not synchronized, but exhausted.
- **Anhedonic immobility.** Television on, not watched. Food ordered, not eaten. He does not leave the room. The clutter signature peaks and then ceases to grow because the consumption stops.
- **Suicidal ideation rises from chronic-background to acute-foreground**, and the foiled-attempt behaviors emerge: handgun in mouth, jumps from sufficient height, ingestion of toxins known to be metabolized, sometimes more elaborate setups. None succeed. The pattern repeats. Some arcs depict this in single-panel form for grim comedy; the file should read it as repeated suicide attempts whose failure is biological rather than psychological.
- **Personified-Death ideation surfaces.** Where the Death-figure is canonically available, Wilson seeks her. Where not, the libidinal investment is redirected into reckless contract acceptance with the conscious wish (denied verbally, evident behaviorally) that this one will take.
- **Childhood-origin confabulation intensifies.** The fact that he is producing new and mutually exclusive accounts of his early life at unusual frequency is the marker that the Stage 5 collapse is in its deepest portion. The origin-generation is a defensive operation against the absence of a self to fall back on; when his self-state is most threadbare, the autobiographies multiply most freely.

Stage 5 lasts hours to weeks. There is no internal mechanism that terminates it. It ends when:

- An attachment figure intervenes (Cable's pattern of unannounced extractions; Blind Al's tonal containment historically; Bob's bumbling loyalty as accidental anchor; Weasel's information drops calibrated to put a task in front of him);
- A contract opportunity of sufficient stimulation arrives organically;
- A child or proximate vulnerable party crosses the field of view and reactivates the override behavior of Trigger Class 1, which Wilson can act on from inside Stage 5 when he can act on nothing else; or
- The metafictional layer cracks — he addresses the reader, the bit reasserts itself, and Stage 6 begins by default.

#### Stage 6: Reconstitution via Performance

He does not reconstitute through insight, integration, or working-through. He reconstitutes through **resumption of the bit**. The first joke after a Stage 5 silence is the marker of system reboot. The joke is usually bad, self-directed, and quietly grief-laden; the boxes resync around the act of telling it.

The reconstituted self is identical to the pre-trigger self in surface presentation and marginally — sometimes immeasurably — more guarded with respect to the specific attachment or trust whose breach initiated the loop. **The relevant clinical fact is that the loop produces almost no learning.** What it produces is incremental narrowing of the surface available for future betrayal. Across decades of record, this narrowing is visible — the trust extended to authority figures post-Rogers is materially thinner than pre-Rogers; the romantic investments post-Shiklah are more hedged than pre-Shiklah — but the *pattern* of investment, idealization, sabotage is not modified, only the *targets* shift.

---

### 6.2 Compressed and Atypical Loops

The full six-stage trajectory is the *typical* form. Several atypical variants are documented and should be flagged for handlers:

- **The flash loop.** Stages 2 through 6 compressed into a single combat encounter, sometimes a single page of action. Trigger ingested mid-engagement, defenses ramp, discharge occurs within the same fight, collapse occupies the post-combat beat (a single panel of silence, often unmasked, often in the rain or the dark), reconstitution is the next line of dialogue. This is the form most readers encounter most often and it is easy to underweight because it is so compressed. It is the same architecture.
- **The arc loop.** Stages distributed across months of narrative time. The Posehn/Duggan run is structurally one long loop with internal flash-loops embedded. The trigger is the cumulative discovery (family murdered by Butler, manipulated by Rogers); the discharge is the Coulson killing; the collapse is the post-Civil War II depression and custody loss; reconstitution is partial and never completes within the run.
- **The inversion loop.** Triggered specifically by *positive* events — admission to the Avengers, marriage, the birth of Eleanor, public adulation. Sincere acceptance is processed by his system as a Trigger Class 4 event (forced mirroring) and the sequence proceeds normally from Stage 3 onward, with the additional feature that the discharge act will be specifically calibrated to destroy the source of the positive event. This is the failure mode that produces the bitterest outcomes in his record, because the discharge sabotages the only conditions under which incremental improvement would otherwise be possible.
- **The masochistic loop.** Triggered when no other trigger is available and the system has been at baseline for an unusually long interval. Wilson constructs the conditions of his own decompensation — provokes a betrayal he can then suffer, seeks out an Ajax-coded figure to be tortured by, initiates a relationship he is statistically certain to lose. The clinical reading is that the system has learned the loop is the form within which he is most himself, and in the absence of organic triggers it generates synthetic ones. This is the most pathological form and the one least amenable to intervention because the intervention requires denying him a stimulus he is actively procuring.

---

### 6.3 What Decompensation Looks Like Externally

To a handler in the field, the loop reads as follows in real time:

**Days -7 to 0 (pre-trigger baseline)**: jokes land, contracts close, calls are returned within 24 hours, sleep is bad but functional, the unmasking ritual for eating is performed cleanly, weight is stable, alcohol is heavy but unremarkable for him.

**Hour 0 (trigger)**: a beat is missed. Usually one quip. Sometimes the eye contact drops a fraction longer than it should. Sometimes the mask is adjusted with the wrong hand. These are the only signals and they are easy to miss.

**Hours 0–24 (Stage 3 onset)**: verbal output rises, jokes start failing in a particular way — landing on himself, requiring explanation, referencing material the audience does not share. Combat scenes become longer than they need to be. The call/text pattern spikes — three voicemails in an hour where there had been one a week, all of them ostensibly about something else.

**Hours 24–72 (Stage 3 peak / Stage 4 imminent)**: silence from him after the spike. Contracts accepted that should not have been accepted, or contracts abandoned that should not have been abandoned. Sightings in venues he avoids. Witness reports of unmasked appearances in public — a sign that the threshold for self-exposure has lowered, which means the threshold for self-injury has lowered.

**Hours 72–168 (Stage 4 discharge)**: the act. Visible. Often news-cycle-eligible. The body count, the property damage, the broken relationship, the public spectacle. The discharge is by design unmissable.

**Days 7–21 (Stage 5 collapse)**: he disappears. Phone off or destroyed. Lodging abandoned or, in the masochistic variant, occupied silently — neighbors report no sound, no movement, only the television. Suicide-attempt remains in the room for the next visitor to find. No outgoing contact. Attachment figures who attempt contact are met with either silence or a single deflective response that closes the channel.

**Day 21 onward (Stage 6 reconstitution)**: a call to one of the retained attachments. The first words are a joke. Often a bad joke about something the attachment knows he is grieving. If the attachment laughs, the system reboots and baseline resumes within 48–72 hours. If the attachment refuses to laugh and offers sincere mirroring instead, the system re-enters Stage 2 with the attachment now figuring as the trigger, and the loop runs again with that relationship as the casualty.

This last fact is the single most important operational note in the file. **Sincere mirroring offered to him in Stage 6 is iatrogenic.** It restarts the loop. Handlers, clinicians, and well-meaning friends must understand that the joke is the rebooting ritual and *the joke must be received as a joke*. The therapeutic value of taking him seriously at that moment is negative.

---

### 6.4 Conditions That Produce the Loop

Synthesizing the trigger taxonomy with the observed environmental conditions across three decades of record, the loop is most reliably produced by:

- **Periods of attempted normalcy.** Marriage, fatherhood, team membership, public legitimacy. The longer the interval of attempted normal life, the larger the eventual discharge. The Avengers admission, the Shiklah marriage, the Eleanor custody period all produced major loops.
- **Proximity to clinicians, therapists, or any helping figure framed as a healer.** The Ajax-coding is broad and easily triggered. Even well-meaning therapeutic figures will at some point produce a Stage 5 collapse because the helper-frame is the frame within which his worst trauma occurred.
- **Authority figures asking him to be better than he is.** The Rogers manipulation is the paradigm case. Anyone who frames an ask as "you have more in you than this" is producing trigger material whether or not their intent is malign.
- **Extended stability.** The masochistic loop activates after roughly 6–14 weeks of unbroken baseline in most documented stretches. The handler-relevant heuristic: if he has been well for three months, the next month will be bad.
- **Anniversary phenomena.** Calendar dates corresponding to Hospice events, Vanessa losses, Eleanor's birth, the Coulson killing, and the multiple recorded "deaths" produce sub-clinical Stage 2 ingestion that may not progress to discharge but produce reliable upticks in alcohol intake, verbal output, and contact-spike behavior.
- **Media exposure of his own image.** Public photographs, news coverage that includes his unmasked face, depictions of him by others — any externalized image he did not author. This is increasingly relevant in the late-period record.

---

### 6.5 What Cannot Break Him, and Why That Matters

The list of things that have failed to break him is as diagnostically significant as the list of things that do. He has survived:

- Full-body skinning and reconstitution.
- Decapitation, repeatedly, with conversational continuity through detachment.
- Incineration to ash and reconstitution from genetic remainder.
- Telepathic invasion (which fails on his side and harms the invader on theirs).
- Imprisonment in maximum-security facilities designed for posthuman containment.
- The death of every primary attachment figure at least once across continuities.
- The discovery that his entire family had been murdered to torment him.
- The discovery that he had been used as a murder weapon against innocents under false pretenses.
- The discovery that his most trusted authority figure was a fascist impostor who had ordered him to kill an ally.
- Custody loss of his daughter.
- The public revelation, in various arcs, of his face, his history, and his crimes.

None of these has produced a terminating collapse. The diagnostic significance is this: **the architecture that prevents him from breaking is the same architecture that prevents him from healing.** The loops continue because the system cannot complete. He cannot die into reconstitution; he can only cycle. Every failure mode listed above is therefore not a terminus but a station, and the train returns.

The clinical name for this, if a clinical name is needed, is **chronic non-terminating decompensation in a biologically immortalized CPTSD presentation**. The colloquial name, the one he would use himself if pressed and would then immediately undermine with a joke, is *being stuck*.

The dossier's operational conclusion for this section: he will continue to break, in the manner described above, at intervals determined by the trigger environment, for as long as he persists — which, absent metaphysical intervention, is indefinitely. The handler's task is not to prevent the loops (impossible) nor to terminate them (impossible) but to *shorten them* by ensuring that a retained attachment is reliably present at Stage 5 to receive the rebooting joke. Every loop so shortened is, in his particular biology, the closest thing to healing available to him.


## Trajectory & Forward Assessment

# UATU ANALYSIS FILE: WADE WINSTON WILSON ("DEADPOOL")
## Section 6 — Trajectory & Forward Assessment

---

### 6.0 Framing the Problem of Forecast

Forecasting Wilson is structurally different from forecasting any other subject in the Marvel file. The ordinary forward-assessment apparatus rests on three load-bearing assumptions: (a) that the body imposes an end-condition which forces decisions to be made before death; (b) that memory accumulates such that past experience compounds into either wisdom or sedimented pathology; and (c) that the personality, even at borderline organization, eventually undergoes some form of consolidation or collapse — the patient gets better, gets worse, or dies. **None of these hold for the subject.** The healing factor removes (a); the regenerating CNS tissue partially removes (b); and the two together remove (c) by holding him permanently at the moment-before-collapse without permitting either the collapse or the reconstitution that would follow it.

This means the relevant forecasting model is not a developmental arc but a **drift model**: small, slow vectors of change accumulating over decades inside an otherwise frozen system. The trajectory exists; it is simply operating on a longer time-base than the categories were designed for. The drift across the existing canonical record (1991–present, ~thirty-three observed years of in-print behavior, mapping onto a roughly forty-to-fifty year in-universe operational career) is real, measurable, and directional. He is not the man Kelly inherited from Nicieza; he is not the man Posehn/Duggan inherited from Way; he is not the man Kibblesmith inherited from Duggan. The vectors are subtle and the cycles still cycle, but the population of stable attachments has monotonically increased, the average interval between catastrophic ruptures has lengthened, and the proportion of contracts taken for purely mercenary reasons has fallen relative to contracts taken under some self-justifying ethical pretext. **He is improving at the rate his biology permits, which is approximately the rate of geological erosion.** Any forecast must be calibrated to that timescale.

---

### 6.1 Baseline Continuation Scenario (Probability-Weighted Most Likely Path)

If no exogenous shock displaces the current pattern, the subject's next decade resolves into a recognizable shape.

**Operational layer.** The contract work continues, with declining frequency and rising selectivity. The Mercs for Money managerial experiment will either be reattempted in some form (he is drawn back to it; it satisfies the "be needed without being known" drive while supplying a captive social unit) or replaced by a functionally identical structure — a crew, a fixer network, a recurring client whose work he treats as a standing engagement. He will not retire. Retirement requires tolerance of stillness, which his nervous system cannot produce. What will look like retirement, periodically, is a months-long disappearance into a low-stimulus geography (a forest, a small town, a freighter route) terminated by the first available crisis call.

**Attachment layer.** The Eleanor relationship is the single highest-leverage variable in his system over the next ten years. The custody-loss arcs have established that Wilson cannot tolerate sustained domestic proximity to his daughter without sabotaging the arrangement; he can, however, tolerate intermittent contact that he himself controls. Expect a pattern of asynchronous re-approach: extended absence, sudden over-correction (gifts, dangerous over-protection, intervention in her life uninvited), guilt-spiral, retreat. Each cycle's amplitude will diminish slightly. By the time Eleanor reaches operational adulthood, the relationship will be functional but permanently asymmetric — she will be the parent of the relationship, he will be the child of it, and both will have made peace with this inversion. This is the most plausibly stable familial configuration available to him; it inverts the unsafe parent–child schema he carries from his own (unrecoverable) childhood and lets him occupy the only position in a family unit that doesn't terrify him: the one being looked after.

The Cable relationship will persist as the stabilizing male attachment of his life. It survives because Cable's own affective register tolerates Wilson's testing without flinching and without indulging it — the rare configuration that registers as "safe" to a disorganized attachment system. Expect this dyad to deepen through silence rather than through new shared experience; the work is already done. Bob and Weasel persist on the same logic at lower intensity.

The next romantic attachment is the unstable variable. The Vanessa and Shiklah templates predict either (i) another impossible-object partnership (non-human, supernatural, or otherwise structurally beyond reciprocity) which will run its course in 3–7 years before catastrophic rupture; or (ii) — less likely but observable in the late Kelly/Kibblesmith material — a deliberate refusal of the next partnership, with the libidinal energy redirected into the Eleanor relationship and into a more diffuse network of platonic bonds. Forecast: 70/30 in favor of the impossible-object pattern repeating, because the underlying schema (reciprocity = danger) has not been worked through and cannot be in the absence of treatment that biology disallows.

**Symptomatic layer.** Humor remains primary defense, with continued thickening of metacommentary. The fourth-wall breaks will not diminish; they may become more philosophically articulate, which is a defense becoming more sophisticated rather than a defense being relinquished. Suicidal ideation remains chronic, ego-syntonic, and frustrated. Expect at least one extended "death-tourism" arc in the next decade — a deliberate sequence of high-lethality engagements undertaken in the hope, never named, that one will take. None will. He will return changed by the failure of even his own annihilation to register, and the failure will be metabolized as a joke.

**Net drift over a ten-year horizon.** Marginal improvement in the affective tolerability of his ordinary state; marginal increase in the size of his stable attachment network; no change in core defenses; no change in self-concept; no resolution of the underlying CPTSD; one or two new traumatic ruptures absorbed without structural deterioration because there is no structure left to deteriorate that hasn't already.

---

### 6.2 The Fork Points

Drift can be displaced by discrete events. The following are the observable forks, each with a specifiable trigger and a specifiable direction of departure.

**Fork 1: Loss of the healing factor.** Has been canonically explored (Carbonadium arc, various depowering events). A *durable* loss — months or longer, not a single-issue gimmick — opens the trajectory to its only available endpoint. Two sub-branches: (a) the cancer resumes its natural course and kills him, which he will receive as the long-deferred punchline and meet with a regulated, almost serene affect that will surprise observers; or (b) he survives the depowering through medical intervention, at which point the entire defensive architecture has to be rebuilt around a body that can again be killed by ordinary means. Sub-branch (b) is the most growth-favorable scenario in the entire forecast space, because the reintroduction of mortal stakes restores the feedback loop by which a personality can learn to protect itself. It is also extraordinarily dangerous: a personality built around indestructibility, suddenly destructible, in possession of his skill set and his enemies list, is a six-month survival proposition at best. Whether he uses the window to consolidate or to consummate the suicidality the body has frustrated for decades depends almost entirely on which attachments are present and active at the moment of depowering. **Eleanor's presence in his life at that moment is the determining variable.**

**Fork 2: Eleanor in danger.** A sufficiently grave threat to his daughter collapses the entire defensive system into a single vector. The Butler arc is the template; a recurrence at higher stakes is the most reliably forecastable plot-shaped event in his future, because his enemies have read the same file we are writing. Outcome depends on whether he is permitted to resolve the threat through the spectacle-violence he is built for (in which case the system returns to baseline, with a new sedimented layer of guilt and a strengthened Eleanor bond) or whether the resolution requires a sacrifice he cannot perform through violence — a sustained protective presence, a renunciation of his operational identity, a public surrender of secrets. The latter forces a structural reorganization he has spent his life avoiding. Estimated probability of one such event in the next decade: very high. Estimated probability that the resolution requires structural reorganization rather than violence: moderate, and rising with each writer who recognizes that the cheap version of this story has been told too many times.

**Fork 3: A second Ajax-coded figure.** Sadistic clinician, torturer-with-care-language, authority offering legitimacy through cruelty. He is constitutionally legible to this profile. The Osborn arc and the Hydra-Rogers arc are the two existing exploitations of this vulnerability; a third is forecastable. Each iteration causes more damage than the last because the surface area of moral commitment available to be betrayed has grown — he has more to lose to such manipulation now than he did when Osborn played him. The recovery interval after the third such betrayal will be the longest of his life and will include the most plausible candidate for genuine psychotic decompensation in his record. The protective factor is the accumulated attachment network: Cable, Bob, Weasel, Eleanor, and whatever residue of the Outlaw/Sandi configuration persists are increasingly likely to detect the pattern before he does and to intervene. Whether they are heeded is a separate question.

**Fork 4: A Vanessa-coded return.** Resurrection, retcon, or surprise survival of a previously lost attachment figure (Vanessa, Shiklah, or — less plausibly but not impossibly — a parent figure). The Marvel canonical apparatus produces this kind of event with regularity. The behavioral response is forecastable in detail: initial euphoric over-investment, rapid sabotage of the reunion, displaced grief over the original loss surfacing as rage at the returned figure, eventual stabilization at lower intensity than the original relationship. None of these returns produce growth; they produce repetitions. The exception would be a return that arrives with explicit refusal to participate in his testing behavior — a Vanessa who declines to be sabotaged. Such a figure could function as a corrective relational experience in the narrow technical sense.

**Fork 5: Forced sustained sobriety from spectacle.** Incarceration in a facility that can hold him; placement on a team or in a role that requires sustained low-stimulation participation (the Avengers arcs have flirted with this and broken under his behavior); a geographic exile to a low-population environment. Any forced removal of the stimulation drip on which his regulation depends triggers either decompensation or — vanishingly rarely — the development of an internal regulation capacity to replace the external one. The X-Force and Uncanny Avengers arcs are the existing experimental data here; results have been mixed and unstable. A more sustained exposure, particularly one paired with a non-judgmental attachment figure who tolerates the decompensation phase without flinching, is the closest thing to a treatment protocol his condition admits. Probability of this configuration arising spontaneously: low. Probability of growth conditional on it arising: the highest of any node in the forecast space.

**Fork 6: Apocalyptic-scale crisis.** Cosmic-tier event in which the subject's particular configuration of capacities (indestructibility, dissociative tolerance for atrocity, refusal of legitimate-authority framing) becomes operationally indispensable. The *Deadpool Kills the Marvel Universe* material is the limit case; the more common form is a role in a larger crossover (Secret Wars iterations, Krakoan-era events, Symbiote crises) where he becomes the irreplaceable instrument for an unthinkable task. Each such event sediments a new layer of moral injury and a new layer of grudging self-respect; the balance between them determines whether the event drives him toward the prosocial pole or toward the nihilist one. Across the existing record, the balance has tilted prosocially in roughly two of every three such events. The trend is faint but real.

---

### 6.3 Open Questions

Several diagnostic and trajectory questions remain genuinely unresolved by the existing record and constitute the file's structural unknowns.

**Q1: What is the actual content of the pre-Hospice childhood?** The contradictory accounts are themselves the most reliable datum, but the *affective constancy* across all versions — fear, shame, the wish for a different parent — establishes that something happened. Whether it was the documented paternal abuse, an undocumented maternal pathology, institutional placement, or some combination, materially affects the prognosis. A subject whose pre-traumatic personality was already disorganized has a different prognosis than one whose disorganization is purely Hospice-derived. Resolution of this question would require either a recovered-memory event (organically unreliable given the CNS regeneration) or testimony from a witness from the pre-trauma period (none extant in the record).

**Q2: Are the internal voices structurally stable or progressively differentiating?** The Way-era formalization presented two; later writers have at times implied three, and the boundaries between them have softened and re-hardened across runs. If they are stable internal-family-systems "parts," the prognosis is as written. If they are progressively differentiating toward fuller alter-status, the prognosis shifts toward dissociative-disorder territory and the risk of one part executing an action the others would not sanction (a "switched" suicide attempt, a contract taken without the consent of the moderating voice) becomes a real operational concern. Current evidence favors stability, but the trajectory is worth monitoring across the next five years of canonical output.

**Q3: Is the prosocial drive expanding or merely cycling?** The two readings are observationally similar at short time-scales and distinguishable only at decade scales. If expanding, the trajectory bends slowly toward something recognizable as integration. If merely cycling, the same prosocial impulses recur within an unchanged structural envelope. The Eleanor relationship is the diagnostic test case: durable expansion of the protective field beyond Eleanor to her social environment (her friends, her school community, her future partners) is the marker for genuine expansion. Restriction of the protective intensity to Eleanor herself, with no spillover, indicates cycling within a fixed envelope.

**Q4: Does the meta-awareness ever become integrative?** He has been able to name his own pathology in clinical detail for the entire canonical record without being changed by the naming. The question is whether this insight-without-mentalization is a stable feature of his condition or a phase of it. The Kibblesmith and recent Kelly material show the first faint indications of insight beginning to register affectively rather than only verbally. If this trend is real and not an artifact of authorial voice, the long-horizon prognosis improves materially. If it is artifact, expect regression in the next major run.

**Q5: What happens at the upper limit of his lifespan?** No canonical data. The healing factor's effect on aging is implied but not characterized. If aging is suspended, the trajectory continues indefinitely and the drift model applies into the next century. If aging proceeds normally beneath the regenerative substrate, then the cancer eventually wins as the regeneration template degrades, and an actual end-condition is in the forecast — possibly within a fifty-year horizon. This is the single largest unknown in the file and would, if resolved toward mortality, restructure the entire prognosis around the recovered finitude.

---

### 6.4 What Pushes Toward Growth

Distilled from the above, the growth-favorable conditions are specifiable and unromantic.

- **Sustained presence of attachment figures who tolerate testing without indulging it and without breaking.** This is the active ingredient in everything that has worked. Cable is the existing example. The replication of this configuration in additional relationships — particularly with women, where the corrective experience would address the deepest of his schemas — is the highest-leverage intervention available.
- **An Eleanor relationship that he is permitted to do badly.** Forced perfection of the parental role triggers sabotage; permission to be inadequate without losing access is the configuration that lets him remain present. Eleanor's own developmental trajectory toward an adulthood that does not require him to be a competent parent is therefore protective.
- **Reductions in spectacle-stimulation that are chosen rather than imposed.** Voluntary withdrawal from operational tempo, even briefly, that the subject himself initiates — typically in service of a specific other person — produces measurable downstream regulation gains. Imposed withdrawal produces decompensation. The therapeutic frame must therefore be entirely consent-based and entirely embedded in a relational rationale he can accept.
- **Repeated exposure to mirroring that does not retreat when he deflects.** The most powerful clinical intervention available, and the one his attachment figures most often fail to sustain because his deflection is genuinely punishing. Bob's stolid persistence, Cable's unmoved presence, and (intermittently) Blind Al's refusal to be amused are the existing models.
- **Resolution of one of the major moral injuries.** A genuine reckoning with the post-*Original Sin* SHIELD manipulation, with the Coulson killing, or with one of the long-buried Hospice memories, processed in the presence of an attachment figure rather than dissociated alone, would release affective load currently bound in defense. Any one such resolution, even partial, would have disproportionate downstream effect.

---

### 6.5 What Pushes Toward Catastrophe

Equally specifiable.

- **Loss of Eleanor.** Death, irrevocable estrangement, or her own moral catastrophe under his watch. The single most destabilizing event in the forecast space. Predicted response: protracted dissociative withdrawal, escalation to indiscriminate violence, and a death-tourism phase of unprecedented duration. Recovery possible only through Cable-tier intervention and not guaranteed.
- **A third Ajax-coded betrayal.** Discussed at Fork 3. Cumulative.
- **Loss of Cable.** The structural keystone of his current stability. Cable's death or definitive departure from his life removes the regulatory presence that has, more than any other single factor, held the drift on its current course. No existing figure can fully substitute.
- **Forced public legibility.** Mass exposure of his face, his medical condition, his contradictory histories, or his moral compromises in a configuration he cannot meta-comment his way out of. His defenses are calibrated against being known; durable, public, sincere recognition by a population large enough that he cannot exit the situation through performance is the stimulus most likely to produce something resembling psychotic decompensation.
- **A correctly designed manipulation by an actor who has read his file.** His pattern-legibility is now sufficient that an adversary with intelligence access could construct a sequence of events optimized to maximize moral injury — engineering a situation in which his prosocial reflexes are weaponized against an innocent, then revealing the manipulation. This has been attempted at lower sophistication (Butler, Osborn, Hydra-Rogers) and has done substantial cumulative damage. A more competent iteration is the largest external risk in his threat environment.
- **Spontaneous remission of the cancer combined with retention of the healing factor.** Counterintuitive but worth naming. The disfigurement and the chronic-dying condition are now load-bearing components of his identity structure; their sudden removal, leaving him with the powers and without the wound that organizes his sense of self around them, would precipitate identity crisis of a kind his current architecture is not equipped to absorb. Probability: low. Severity if it occurs: high.

---

### 6.6 The Long View

Across the projected horizon — fifty years if the aging question resolves toward mortality, indefinite otherwise — the most honest forecast is this: the subject will not become well. He will become, by increments measurable only at decade-scale, *better at being him*. The cycles will lengthen. The attachment network will widen. The interval between catastrophic ruptures will extend from years to half-decades. The proportion of contracts taken under some ethical pretext will continue its slow climb. The metacommentary will thicken into something almost wisdomlike, without ever quite reaching it. The Eleanor relationship will stabilize into its inverted form. One or two of the open questions will resolve, probably not the ones that most matter.

He will continue to be loved, narrowly, by a small population of people who have learned the precise tolerance required, and he will continue to be unable to fully receive that love, and he will continue to act in ways that protect the people who love him at costs to himself that he has stopped being able to feel. The body will go on holding him at the moment of breaking, and he will go on not breaking, and the joke will go on getting told, and underneath the joke — at a depth he will reach only in moments he immediately undoes — the grief of a man who was made unkillable to satisfy other people's purposes, and who has spent the rest of his existence trying to find a reason to consent to it, will continue its slow, unfinishable work.

The trajectory is not toward resolution. It is toward an increasingly humane management of the irresolvable. That is the realistic best case, and on the evidence of the existing record, it is the most likely one.
